Atharvavedaparisistas

"The ParishiShTas of the Atharvaveda",
Vol. 1, parts 1 and 2 (all published), Leipzig: Harrassowitz 1909--1910

Revised by Arlo Griffiths (Leiden and Groningen Universities)
in collaboration with Reinhold Gruenendahl (Niedersaechsische StAts und Universitaetsbibliothek, Goettingen)

(ParishiShTa_1. nakShatrakalpaH)
(AVParis_0,0.0)     shrIgaNeshAya namaH || oM namo 'tharvAtmane vAmadevAya shivAya || shrIsarasvatyai namaH ||

(AVParis_1,1.1)     atha nakShatrakalpaM vyAkhyAsyAmaH ||
(AVParis_1,1.2)     kR^ittikA rohiNI mR^igashira ArdrA punarvasU puShyAshleShA maghA(H) phAlgunI phalgunyau hasta(sh) citrA svAti(r) vishAkhe anurAdhA jyeShThA mUla(m) pUrvAShADhA uttarAShADAbhijic chravaNaH shraviShThA shatabhiShaH pUrvaproShThapadottaraproShThapadau revaty ashvayujau bharaNyaH ||

(AVParis_1,2.1)     ShaT kR^ittikA ekA rohiNI tisro mR^igashira ekArdrA dve punarvasU ekaH puShyaH ShaD AshleShAH ShaN maghAH catasraH phalgunyaH paJNca hasta ekA citrA ekA svAtir dve vishAkhe catasro 'nurAdhA ekA jyeShThA sapta mUlam aShTAv aShADhA eko 'bhijit tisraH shravaNaH paJNca shraviShThA ekA shatabhiShA catasraH proShThapadau ekA revatI dve ashvayujau tisro bharaNyaH ||
(AVParis_1,2.2)     iti saMkhyAparimitaM brahma ||

(AVParis_1,3.1)     AgniveshyaH kR^ittikA rohiNy AnurohiNI shvetAyinaM mR^igashira ArdrA bArhadgavI vAtsyAyanau punarvasU bhAradvAjaH puShyo jAtUkarNyo 'shleShA vaiyAghrapadyo maghA(H) pArAsharyau pUrve phAlguNyAv aupashivyA uttare mANDavyAyano hastash citrA gautamI kauNDinyAyanaH svAtiH kApile vishAkhe maitreyy anurAdhA kaushikI jyeShThA kautsaM mUlaM hAritayaj~nI pUrvAShADhA kAshyapy uttarA shaunako 'bhijid AtreyaH shravaNo gArgyaH shraviShThA dAkShAyaNI shatabhiShag vAtsyAyanyau pUrve proShThapade AgastyAv uttare shAN^khAyanI revatI kAtyAyan(y)Av ashvayujau mAtR^ibhyo bharaNyaH vasiShThaH kashyapa Adityash candramA brahmANo nakShatreShu ||

(AVParis_1,4.1)     kR^ittikA agnidevatyA rohiNyAM tu prajApatiH | saumyaM mR^igashiraM vidyAn marutash cAtra daivatam ||
(AVParis_1,4.2)     rudrasyArdrAditeH punarvasU puShye vidyAd bR^ihaspatim | ashleShA[[H]] sarpadaivatyA maghAsu pitaraH smR^itAH ||
(AVParis_1,4.3)     bhagas [tu] pUrvayoH phalgunyor aryamottarayor api | haste ca savitA daivaM citrA tu tvaShTR^idaivatA ||
(AVParis_1,4.4)     svAtau tu daivataM vAyur indrAgnI tu vishAkhayoH | anurAdhAsu mitro vai jyeShThAyAm indramahAdevau ||
(AVParis_1,4.5)     ahir budhnyash ca mUlasya nirR^itish cAtra daivatam | ApaH pUrvAsv aShADhAsu vishve devAs tathottare ||
(AVParis_1,4.6)     abhijid brahmadevatyaH shravaNe viShNur ucyate | shraviShThA vasudevatyA shatabhiShag varuNendrayoH ||
(AVParis_1,4.7)     aja ekapAd dishash ca Adityash ca tathottare | revatI pUShadaivatyA ashvinyAm ashvinau smR^itau ||
(AVParis_1,4.8)     bharaNyo yamadevatyA devatAH saMprakIrtitAH ||

(AVParis_1,5.1)     kR^ittikA maghA mUlaM [[ca tathA]] pUrvANi dvandvinAm | etAni purastAdbhAgAny ahaHpUrvANi jAnIyAt ||
(AVParis_1,5.2)     ArdrAM shatabhiShajaM svAtim AshleShA bharaNIr api | naktaMbhAgAni bruvate jyeShThayA saha brahmANam ||
(AVParis_1,5.3)     punarvasU vishAkhe ca uttarANi ca dvandvinAm | rAtrIm ubhayataH pakShau bhajante yA ca rohiNI ||
(AVParis_1,5.4)     mR^igashiraH puShyo hastash citrA tu sahAnurAdhaiH | shravaNash ca shraviShThAsh ca revaty ashvayujau nava ||
(AVParis_1,5.5)     etAny upariShTAdbhAgAni rAtrIpUrvANi jAnIyAt | muhUrto 'bhijid ucyate ||
(AVParis_1,5.6)     purastAdbhAgAny anAgatenopariShTAdbhAgAny atikrAntena ubhayatobhAgAni vartamAne[[na]] naktaMbhAgAni samaM candreNa vA ||
(AVParis_1,5.7)     [[ShaD a]]nAgatayogIni sthitayogIni dvAdasha | navAtikrAntayogIni tathA yogaH pradR^ishyate ||

(AVParis_1,6.1)     bahUni jAtAni graho hinasti kR^ittikAsu tiShThann uta dIrgham AyuH | ajAvayo mUShikAsh ca vyathante visho brahmaNaH saha mlecchavAMsh ca ||
(AVParis_1,6.2)     kaliN^gAnAM vyathate nanu rAjA hiraNyakArAMsh ca nihanti kR^itsnam | ayaskArA lohakArA AhitAgnish ca kR^itsnaM niyanti sahAgnitaptaiH ||
(AVParis_1,6.3)     ayo lohaM rajataM jAtarUpaM hiraNyamishraM [yac] ca patanti sAram | kAshAH kushA yac ca suvarNavarNaM yac cAgnivarNaM phalamUlapuShpam ||
(AVParis_1,6.4)     [ye tatra jAtAH] sarAMsi shuShyanty apayanti nadyaH prajA vyathante pashavo mR^igAsh ca || prajApater hR^idaye pIDyamAne sarvaM jagad vyathate sapradesham ||
(AVParis_1,6.5)     mahAbhaumo rAjA mariShyatIti vidyAd ekAriNAM chavakAm invakAsu | nakShatrabhAge niyanti yojadhAnAH tathA hi nUnaM triNavena sR^iShTam ||
(AVParis_1,6.6)     tathA sa ninye nidhAnadarshanAya tatra teShAM sahAkShemaM tasya vidyAt | paritya ye pUrvapadAn balena uttiShThanti vIryavanto mR^igAnAm ||
(AVParis_1,6.7)     bhagena devy upayanti divyam ArdrAbhAge sahino bhavanti | tatra daivAn mAnuShyAMsh ca punarvasvor nakShatra bhAge niniyoja dhAnAH ||
(AVParis_1,6.8)     tathA hi nUnaM puShyo bhAga ekadhA brAhmaNAnAM tathA vidur nakShatraveditAraH tathA hi nUnam ||
(AVParis_1,6.9)     shatadrayaH kaishikA dakShiNArdhA AndhrAsh ca yogahAsayA pravR^iddhAH || ashleShAbhAge sahino bhavanti tatra ||
(AVParis_1,6.10)     veNUn pitÌMs trirujAhur devatAm | maghAbhAge aShTame devasR^iShTam | saMyujyante devaprasAdanena tatra ||

(AVParis_1,7.1)     rAj~nAM rAkAyAm atha madrakaikayA manomApAyanasahaparisunniyojasahAntau | tunyam atha saptamAtraM pUrvabhAge navake phalgunIShu ||
(AVParis_1,7.2)     matsyA mAgadhAsh cedayash ca shAlvA matsyA ubhe phalgunIShu | saMyujyante devaprasAdanena tatra ||
(AVParis_1,7.3)     pUrvAcAryA icchamAnAsh ca sarve yakR^it kloma saha bhAgena haste | saMyujyante devaprasAdanena tatra ||
(AVParis_1,7.4)     ye pUrvArdhe nijIhate carantaH shAntA mR^igA [jantu]pashavo apagAminas te | pashavo bhavatAsh ca sarve citrAyA bhAge sahino bhavanti || tatrA-
(AVParis_1,7.5)     -cyutakeshaM vAhanaM jayArthaM kumAryo anaDvAn sahate atra ye | vij~nAyate devasR^iShTaM purANaM svAtiM bhajante tR^iNavash ca sarve ||
(AVParis_1,7.6)     vR^ikShA vR^ikShamUlam ikShvAkavash ca vishAkhAyAM yojitAH sAMpadena | tasmin gR^ihIte bhayam eva teShAM daivopasR^iShTe tu balena kAryam || ye tatra jAtAH ||
(AVParis_1,7.7)     ye pashcArdhe nijIhate caranta Asavo mR^igA uttarArdhAsh cAndhrAH | anUrAdhAsu magadhavaN^gamatsyAH sarve samagrAH sahino bhavanti tatra ||
(AVParis_1,7.8)     paJNcaikadhA janapadA bhavanti sayujaHkAsaubaladAdauShyadhAH | bAhlIkA jyeShThA upayanti bhaktyA tatra ||
(AVParis_1,7.9)     ikShvAkUNAM nirmathyA mUlam AhuH | tathA vidur nakShatraveditAras tathA hi nUnam
(AVParis_1,7.10)     kAmbojAH kAlamR^iShAsh ca krandA ucchuShmANaH shvAnash cAvadhUmamarkaTAsh ca pUrvAShADhA upayanti bhaktyA tatra ||

(AVParis_1,8.1)     vishve devAH saha paJNcAlajyeShThA Apash ca yAH pAntu bhUtaM bhaviShyat | uttarAShADhA upayanti bhaktyA tatra ||
(AVParis_1,8.2)     nArkavindA nArvvidAlA nasR^iN^gAvau naiShadhA jantavo mataN^gAH | abhijitaM hArthavij~nAya bhejire tatra ||
(AVParis_1,8.3)     pAJNcAlAH shravaNam upaiti bhaktyA sunvantash cobhe vidvAn bhUtA niniyoja devaH || pUrvakartA bhUtabhaviShyakAlas tathA ni nUnam
(AVParis_1,8.4)     kurUn shraviShThAs tathA shivAs tathAhur nakShatrabhAge niniyoja dhAnAH || tathA hi nUnam
(AVParis_1,8.5)     aN^gAdayo janapadA guhAshayA apsu ca ye kShipanti shatabhiShaji bheShajasya bhejire tatra ||
(AVParis_1,8.6)     khaDgA hastino gavayA varAhA ahInarA kuntayash cApi sarve | pUrvau proShThapadA upayanti bhaktyA tatra ||
(AVParis_1,8.7)     ushInarA uttarayoH proShThapadayor nakShatrabhAge niniyoja dhAnAH | tathA hi nUnam
(AVParis_1,8.8)     AvR^itAH shUdrAH saha kAravash ca dakShiNapUrve yUkabhiH saha revatIM hArthavij~nAya bhejire tatra ||
(AVParis_1,8.9)     acyutakeshaM vAhanaM ca padArtham ucAvacajanapadA mahAntaH | ashvayujau hArthavij~nAya bhejire tatra ||
(AVParis_1,8.10)     ubhaye kIkaTAH kaushalAsh ca rahash ca[vo] ye ca prasuptAsh caranti bharaNIH sahArthavij~nAya bhejire tatra teShAM sahAkShayam asya vidyAt ||

(AVParis_1,9.1)     kariShyamANaH saMgrAmaM pratirAjena kShatriyaH | brAhmaNaM pUrvam anvicched vidvAMsaM shAstravittamam ||
(AVParis_1,9.2)     utpAtAn yas tu yAn vidyAd divyAntarikShapArthivAn | taM vai lipsitum arhati rAjA rAShTre jijIviShuH ||
(AVParis_1,9.3)     grahANAM yaH sthitiM vidyAn nakShatrANAM ca sAMpadam | anabhyaktam upAsIta nakShatrasamatAM ca yat ||
(AVParis_1,9.4)     AyudhIyAn bibhrad rAjA kR^ittikAsu na riShyati | tad dhi tejasvi nakShatraM bahulaM divi rocate ||
(AVParis_1,9.5)     atho hi kR^ittikA iti nakShatraM bhAnumattamam | Agneyam agninakShatraM rAjA hy asmin pravardhate ||
(AVParis_1,9.6)     rohiNyA[M] sArdham AsIta rajjupalyAni kArayet | mR^igashirasy ashvAn bibhR^iyAt sAsya senA na riShyati ||
(AVParis_1,9.7)     saumyaM somasya nakShatraM rAjA hy asmin pravardhate | ArdrAyAM mR^igayAM yAyAd amitrebhyash ca hAvayet ||

(AVParis_1,19.1)     varco vai nAmaitan nakShatraM yan madhyAhnainaM varco gacchaty upainaM varcas tiShThati nAsmAd varco apakrAmati varcasvI prajayA pashubhiH shriyA gR^ihair dhanena bhavatIti veda

(ParishiShTa_2. rAShTrasaMvargaH)

(AVParis_2,1.1)     om | brahmaNe brahmavedAya rudrAya parameShThine | namaskR^itya pravakShyAmi sheSham AtharvaNaM vidhim ||
(AVParis_2,1.2)     daivaM prabhavate shreShThaM hetumAtraM tu pauruSham | daivena tu suguptena shakto jetuM vasuMdharAm ||
(AVParis_2,1.3)     daivAt puruShakArAc ca daivam eva vishiShyate | tasmAd daivaM visheSheNa pUjayet tu mahIpatiH ||
(AVParis_2,1.4)     daivakarmavidau tasmAt sAMvatsarapurohitau | gR^ihNIyAt satataM rAjA dAnasaMmAnaraJNjanaiH ||
(AVParis_2,1.5)     apitA tu yathA bAlas tathAsAMvatsaro nR^ipaH | amAtR^iko yathA bAlas tathAtharvavivarjitaH || arimadhye yathaikAkI tathA vaidyavivarjitaH ||
(AVParis_2,1.6)     dharmeNa pR^ithivIM kR^itsnAM vijayiShyan mahIpatiH | vidyAlakShaNasaMpannaM bhArgavaM varayed gurum ||
(AVParis_2,1.7)     caturvidhasya karmaNo vedatattvena nishcayam | prajApatir athaiko hi na vedatrayam IkShate ||

(AVParis_2,2.1)     atharvabhinnaM yac chAntaM tac chAntaM netarais tribhiH | vij~nAnaM triShu lokeShu jAyate brahmavedataH ||
(AVParis_2,2.2)     atharvA sR^ijate ghoram adbhutaM shamayet tathA | atharvA rakShate yaj~naM yaj~nasya patir aN^girAH ||
(AVParis_2,2.3)     divyAntarikShabhaumAnAm utpAtAnAm anekadhA | shamayitA brahmavedaj~nas tasmAd rakShitA bhR^iguH ||
(AVParis_2,2.4)     brahmA shamayen nAdhvaryur na chandogo na bahvR^icaH | rakShAMsi rakShati brahmA brahmA tasmAd atharvavit ||
(AVParis_2,2.5)     senAyA rakShaNe tasmAt svarAShTraparivR^iddhaye | shAntyarthaM ca mahIpAlo vR^iNuyAd bhArgavaM gurum ||

(AVParis_2,3.1)     gurave pArthivo dadyAt kotiM varaNadakShiNAm | ardhamardhaM mahIbhAgaM tR^itIyaM tu tribhAgataH ||
(AVParis_2,3.2)     evaM bhUmipramANena koTibhAgaM vinirdishet | yena vA parituShyeta gurus tat pArthivash caret ||
(AVParis_2,3.3)     ghnanti daivopasargAsh ca na ca devo 'bhivarShati | vIrAs tatra na sUyante yad rAShTram apurohitam ||
(AVParis_2,3.4)     na haviH pratigR^ihNanti devatAH pitaro dvijAH | tasya bhUmipater yasya gR^ihe nAtharvavid guruH ||
(AVParis_2,3.5)     samAhitAN^gapratyaN^gaM vidyAcAraguNAnvitam | paippalAdaM guruM kuryAc chrIrAShTrArogyavardhanam ||

(AVParis_2,4.1)     tathA shaunakinaM vApi vedamantravipashcitam | rAShTrasya vR^iddhikartAraM dhanadhAnyAdibhiH sadA ||
(AVParis_2,4.2)     AtharvaNAd R^ite nAnyo niyojyo 'tharvavid guruH | nR^ipeNa jayakAmena nirmito 'gnir ivAdhvare ||
(AVParis_2,4.3)     bahvR^ico hanti vai rAShTram adhvaryur nAshayet sutAn | chandogo dhananAshAya tasmAd AtharvaNo guruH ||
(AVParis_2,4.4)     aj~nAnAd vA pramAdAd vA yasya syAd bahvR^ico guruH | desharAShTrapurAmAtyanAshas tasya na saMshayaH ||
(AVParis_2,4.5)     yadi vAdhvaryavaM rAjA niyunakti purohitam | shastreNa vadhyate kShipraM parikShINArthavAhanaH ||

(AVParis_2,5.1)     yathaiva paN^gur adhvAnam apakShI cANDajo nabhaH | evaM chandogaguruNA rAjA vR^iddhiM na gacchati ||
(AVParis_2,5.2)     purodhA jalado yasya maudo vA syAt kadA cana | abdAd dashabhyo mAsebhyo rAShTrabhraMshaM sa gacchati ||
(AVParis_2,5.3)     palAlakam idaM sarvam R^igyajuHsAmasaMsthitam | sAraM sAraparaM dhAnyam atharvAN^giraso viduH ||
(AVParis_2,5.4)     trayo lokAs trayo devAs trayo vedAs trayo 'gnayaH | ardhamAtre layaM yAnti vedash cAtharvaNaH smR^itaH ||
(AVParis_2,5.5)     na tithir na ca nakShatraM na graho na ca candramAH | atharvamantrasaMprAptyA sarvasiddhir bhaviShyati ||

(AVParis_3,2.1)     hastyashvaM gurave dadyAn narayAnaM tathaiva ca | divyam AbharaNaM caiva AtapatrAdim eva ca ||
(AVParis_3,2.2)     ucchiShTArthaM na gR^ihNIyAn maN^galArthaM mahIpatiH | mantrauShadhyo na sidhyanti rAjA tatra vinashyati ||

(AVParis_3,2.5)     hInAdhikAN^ge purarAShTrahAniH kANe jaDe vAhanakoshanAshaH | stene tv ashakte ca samastadoShAH klIbe vivarNe nR^ipatir vinashyet ||

(AVParis_3,3.1)     bhinnasvare jAyate gAtrabhedo dveShye gurau vipratipattim AhuH | vivarNanetre patite tu putrAn adhvaryuNA ca nihanti pautrAn ||
(AVParis_3,3.2)     kR^iShNe koshakShayaM vidyAd rakte vAhanasaMkShayaH | piN^galaH pArthivaM hanyAd rAShTraM hanyAt tu kekaraH ||
(AVParis_3,3.3)     bahvR^icaM hi niyuJNjyAd yaH paurohitye tu pArthivaH | sa tArapaN^ke hastIva saha tenaiva majjati ||
(AVParis_3,3.4)     adhvaryuM hi niyuJNjyAd yaH paurohitye tu pArthivaH | uttitIrShur ivAshmAnam Adatte svavadhAya saH ||
(AVParis_3,3.5)     vadhabandhaparikleshaM koshavAhanasaMkShayaH | karoty etAnvaye 'vasthAs tapoyukto 'pi sAmagaH ||
(AVParis_3,3.6)     anvayAkR^itisaMpannaM tasmAd bhR^igvaN^girovidam | gotrAN^girasavAsiShThaM rAjA kuryAt purohitam ||
(AVParis_3,3.7)     makheShu rAShTreShu pureShu caiva senAsu rAj~nAM svaniveshaneShu | ya utpAtAs trividhA ghorarUpAs tAn sarvAn shamayed brahmavedavit ||
(AVParis_3,3.8)     tasmAd guruM vedarahasyayuktaM caturvidhe karmaNi cApramattam | shAntaM ca dAntaM ca jitendriyaM ca kuryAn narendraH priyadarshanaM ca || priyadarshanaM ceti ||
iti rAjaprathamAbhiShekaH samAptaH ||

(ParishiShTa_4. purohitakarmANi)

(AVParis_4,1.10)     hastivarcasam iti hastinam ||
(AVParis_4,1.11)     yat te mAtA yat te piteti narayAnam ||
(AVParis_4,1.12)     khaDgaM cAbhimantrayAmIti khaDgam ||
(AVParis_4,1.13)     khaDgaM cAbhimantrayAmi yaH shatrUn mardayiShyati | marditAH shatravo 'nena vasham AyAntu te sadeti ||
(AVParis_4,1.14)     paryaN^kam AsanaM khaDgaM dhvajaM chattraM sacAmaram | ratham ashvagajaM shreShThaM dhanur varma shareShudhim ||
(AVParis_4,1.15)     AJNjanaM gandhamAlyAni vastrANy AbharaNAni ca | sarvAn shAntyudakenaitAn abhyukShyec cAbhimantrayet ||
(AVParis_4,1.16)     dUrvAdIn mUrdhni nikShipya svastyayanair abhimantrayet | abhayaM dyAvApR^ithivIty abhimantrito brAhmaNAn praNipatya prAk ||
(AVParis_4,1.17)     yuShmatprasAdAc chAntim adhigacchAmIti ||
(AVParis_4,1.18)     tathAstv ity ukto nirgacched iti ||
(AVParis_4,1.19)     evaMkR^ityasvastyayano yad evAvalokayati ta sidhyati ||
(AVParis_4,1.20)     tad api shlokAH ||
(AVParis_4,1.21)     asuraiH pIDyamAnas tu purA shakro jagatprabhuH | kArayAm Asa vidhivat purodhastve bR^ihaspatim ||
(AVParis_4,1.22)     sa vR^ito bhayabhItena shamanArthaM bubhUShatA | maN^galAni sasarjAShTAv abhayArthaM shatakratoH ||
(AVParis_4,1.23)     proktAni maN^galAny aShTau brAhmaNo gaur hutAshanaH | bhUmiH siddhArthakAH sarpiH shamI vrIhiyavau tathA ||
(AVParis_4,1.24)     etAni satataM puNyAni saMpashyann arcayann api | na prApnoty ApadaM rAjA shriyaM prApnoty anuttamAm ||

(AVParis_4,2.1)     atha rAjakarmANi 
(AVParis_4,2.2)     vishvAvasau muhUrte snAto abhiShekamantrair abhimantritaH ||
(AVParis_4,2.3)     anulepanair anuliptaH ||
(AVParis_4,2.4)     pUrvoktena vidhinA vastrAlaMkArAdibhiH
(AVParis_4,2.5)     suvarNaniShkaM kR^iShNalaM vA vAmahastena saMgR^ihya ||
(AVParis_4,2.6)     yad duHkR^itaM yac chabalaM sarvaM pApmAnaM dahatv ity
(AVParis_4,2.7)     anena mantreNa suvarNaM sharIre nighR^iShya dakShiNena hastena viprAya dadyAd
(AVParis_4,2.8)     dhenuM cArogAm
(AVParis_4,2.9)     aparimitaguNAn tilAn sauvarNamaye tAmramaye vA pAtre sthApayitvA yad aj~nAnAd ity abhimantrya viprAya dadyAt ||
(AVParis_4,2.10)     yad aj~nAnAt tathA j~nAnAd yan mayA shabalaM kR^itam | tat sarvaM tiladAnena dahyatAm iti hi prabho ||
(AVParis_4,2.11)     bhUmish ca sasyasaMpannA brAhmaNe vedapArage | yathAshakti pradeyA hi bR^ihaspativaco yathA ||
(AVParis_4,2.12)     sa bhuktvA vividhAn bhogAn saptasAgaramekhalAm | pR^ithivIM prApya modeta candravat pR^ithivIpatiH ||
(AVParis_4,2.13)     annaM tu vividhaM nityaM pradadyAt dvijAtaye | tUryaghoSheNa saMyuktaH kR^itasvastyayanas tathA ||
(AVParis_4,2.14)     gR^ihadevAMs tu saMpUjya kAryash cApy utsavo gR^ihe | chattrAdIni ca yAnAni pUjayed vidhivat svayam ||
(AVParis_4,2.15)     [puShpaish ca vividhaiH shubhraiH phalaish cApy arcayed budhaH] tasmAt sarvANi satataM dAnAni tu mahIpatiH | dattvA shraddhAnvito viprair vR^ito bhuJNjIta vAgyataH ||

(AVParis_4,3.1)     atha piShTamayIM rAtriM caturbhir dIpakaiH saha | arcitAM gandhamAlyena sthApayet tasya cAgrataH ||
(AVParis_4,3.2)     namas kR^itvA tato rAtrim arcayitvA yathAvidhi | dhUpena cAnnapAnena stotreNa ca samarcayet ||
(AVParis_4,3.3)     pAhi mAM satataM devi sarAShTraM sasuhR^ijjanam | uShase naH prayacchasva shAntiM ca kR^iNu me sadA | ye tvAM prapadyante devi na teShAM vidyate bhayam ||
(AVParis_4.3.4)     rAtriM prapadye jananIM sarvabhUtaniveshanIm | bhadrAM bhagavatIM kR^iShNAM vishvasya jagato nishAm ||
(AVParis_4,3.5)     saMveshanIM saMyamanIM grahanakShatramAlinIm | prapanno 'haM shivAM rAtriM bhadre pAram ashImahi ||
(AVParis_4,3.6)     yAM sadA sarvabhUtAni sthAvarANi carANi ca | sAyaM prAtar namasyanti sA mAM rAtry abhirakShatv iti ||

(AVParis_4,4.1)     A rAtri pArthivam iShirA yoShA trAyamAna ity rAtryANi ||
(AVParis_4,4.2)     mamobhA mahyam Apa iti sUktAbhyAm anvAlabhya japet ||

(AVParis_4,4.5)     abhayam ity R^icA catasraH sharkarAH pradakShiNaM pratidishaM kShipet ||

(AVParis_4,4.12)     naisham abhayaM karma mausalIputraH paiThInasiH ||

(AVParis_4,5.1)     athAto rAtrisUktAnAM vidhim anukramiShyAmaH ||
(AVParis_4,5.2)     shuciH shuklavAsAH purohitaH ||

(AVParis_4,5.4)     piShTamayIM rAtriM kR^itvA ||

(AVParis_4,5.16)     evamevam aharahaH kuryAt ||

(AVParis_4,6.2)     yasya rAj~no janapade sa nAsti vividhair bhayaiH | pIDyate tasya tad rAShTraM paN^ke gaur iva majjati ||

(ParishiShTa_5. puShyAbhiShekaH)

(AVParis_5,1.1)     om atha puShyAbhiShekasya vidhiM vakShyAmi sAMpadam | dharmArthakAmasaMyuktaM rAjA kuryAt purohitam ||
(AVParis_5,1.2)     sauvarNarAjatais tAmraiH kalashaiH pArthivair api | sahasreNa shatenAtha toyagrahaNam iShyate ||
(AVParis_5,1.3)     caturNAM sAgarANAM tu nadInAM ca shatasya tu | abhiShekAya rAj~nas tu toyam AhR^itya yatnataH ||
(AVParis_5,1.4)     ekadvitricaturNAM vA sAgarasya tu paJNcamam | oShadhIs teShu sarveShu kalasheShUpakalpayet ||
(AVParis_5,1.5)     sahA ca dahadevI ca balA cAtibalA tathA | madayantI vacA shvetA vyAghradantI sumaN^galA ||

(AVParis_5,2.1)     shatAvarI jayantI ca shatapuShpA sacandanA | priyaN^gU rocano ashIram amR^itA ca sasArikA ||
(AVParis_5,2.2)     ashvatthaplakShabilvAnAM nyagrodhapanasasya ca | shirIShAmrakapitthAnAM pallavaiH samalaMkR^itAn ||
(AVParis_5,2.3)     hemaratnauShadhIbilvapuShpagandhAdhivAsitAn | AcchAditAn sitair vastrair abhimantrya purohitaH ||
(AVParis_5,2.4)     sAvitry ubhayataH kuryAc chaM no devI tathaiva ca | hiraNyavarNAH sUktaM ca anuvAkAdyam eva ca ||
(AVParis_5,2.5)     dharaNI pAdapIThaM syAd dUrvAmUlAN^kurAn shubhAn | tasyopari nyaset pIThaM haimaM raupyam athApi vA ||

(AVParis_5,3.1)     anaDudvyAghrasiMhAnAM mR^igasya ca yathAkramam | catvAri carmANy etAni pUrvAd Arabhya vinyaset ||
(AVParis_5,3.2)     cAturhotravidhAnena juhuyAc ca purohitaH | caturdikShu sthitair viprair vedavedAN^gapAragaiH ||
(AVParis_5,3.3)     bilvAhAraH phalAhAraH payasA vApi vartayet | saptarAtraM ghR^itAshI va tato homaM prayojayet ||
(AVParis_5,3.4)     gavyena payasA kuryAt sauvarNena sruveNa tu | vedAnAm Adibhir mantrair mahAvyAhR^itipUrvakaiH ||
(AVParis_5,3.5)     sharmavarmA gaNash caiva tathA syAd aparAjitaH | AyuShyash cAbhayash caiva tathA svastyayano gaNaH ||

(AVParis_5,4.1)     etAn paJNca gaNAn hutvA vAcayeta dvijottamAn | hiraNyenAkShatArgheNa phalaish ca madhusarpiShA ||
(AVParis_5,4.2)     puNyAhaM vAcayitvAsya ArambhaM kArayed budhaH | tiShyanakShatrasaMyukte mahUrte karaNe shubhe ||
(AVParis_5,4.3)     uccairghoSha iti tUryANy abhimantrya purohitaH | sarvatUryaninAdena abhiShikto hy alaMkR^itaH ||
(AVParis_5,4.4)     siMhAsanaM samAruhya pIThikAM vA yathAkramam | cAmarachattrasaMyuktaM pratihAravibhUShitam || 
(AVParis_5,4.5)     mattadvipacatuShkaM ca caturdikShu prakalpayet | upaviShTas tato rAjA prajAnAM kArayed dhitam | akarA brAhmaNA gAvaH strIbAlajaDarogiNaH ||

(AVParis_5,5.1)     tatas tu darshanaM deyaM brAhmaNAnAM nR^ipeNa tu | shreNIprakR^itimukhyAnAM strIjanaM ca namaskaret ||
(AVParis_5,5.2)     AshiShas te hi dAsyanti tuShTA janapadA bhuvi | evaM prajAnurajyeta pR^ithivI ca vashA bhavet ||
(AVParis_5,5.3)     purohitaM mantriNaM ca senAdhyakShaM tathaiva ca | ashvAdhyakShaM gajAdhyakShaM koShThAgArapatiM tathA ||
(AVParis_5,5.4)     bhANDAgArapatiM vaidyaM daivaj~naM ca yathAkramam | yathArheNa ca yogena sarvAn saMpUjayen nR^ipaH ||
(AVParis_5,5.5)     rAjyaM purohite nyasya sheShANAM ca yathAkramam | sthAnAntarANi cAnyAni dattvA sukham avApnuyAt ||
(AVParis_5,5.6)     dUrvAsiddhArthakAn sarpiH shamIr vrIhiyavau tathA shuklAni caiva puShpANi mUrdhni dadyAt purohitaH ||
(AVParis_5,5.7)     atharvavihito hy eSha vidhiH puShyAbhiShecane | rAjA snAto mahIM bhuN^kte shakralokaM sa gacchati || 
iti puShyAbhiShekaH ||

(ParishiShTa_6. piShTarAtryAH kalpaH)

(AVParis_6,1.8)     A mA puShTe ca poShe cety etAbhir upasthAya ||

(AVParis_6,1.10)     Avatas ta iti japan samantAt talpasyAvakIrya
(AVParis_6,1.11)     ayaM pratisara iti pratisaram Abadhya sharkarAn pratidishaM kShipet ||
(AVParis_6,1.12)     dhUpasheShaM rAj~ne dadyAd ||
(AVParis_6,1.13)     abhayapradaM karma ||
(AVParis_6,1.14)     pashcAt sarveShu koneShu dvimukhIm ekamukhIM vA | sarvato vijayAM rakShAm ekAM vA teShu caturmukhIm ||
(AVParis_6,1.15)     ekamukhIM vA sarvatrApratirathajapa ity eke
(AVParis_6,1.16)     sarvatra sharkarAkShepash ceti ||

(AVParis_6,2.1)     gR^ihItvA piShTarAtriM tu veshmadvAre visarjayet
(AVParis_6.2.2)     vanaspatir aso madhya iti guggulukuShThadhUpaM dadyAd
(AVParis_6,2.3)     yas te gandha iti bhUtim abhimantrya
(AVParis_6,2.4)     tryAyuSham iti rAj~ne rakShAM kR^itvA
(AVParis_6,2.5)     asapatnam iti sharkarAn abhimantryAN^guShThAd [abhi]pradakShiNaM pratidishaM kShipet ||
(AVParis_6,2.6)     shAntA dyaur iti japitvA rAjAnaM vAsagR^ihaM nayet ||
(AVParis_6,2.7)     bhUtinA rakShAM kR^itvA niShkramya
(AVParis_6,2.8)     evamevam ahar ahaH kuryAd iti ||
piShTarAtryAH kalpaH samAptaH ||

(ParishiShTa_7. ArAtrikam)

(AVParis_7,1.1)     oM na suShvApa purA shakro dAnavAnAM purodhasA | prayuktair auShadhair yogair mantrANAM japahomataH ||
(AVParis_7,1.2)     praNipatya bR^ihaspatim atharvANaM puraMdaraH | dAnavaiH paribhUto 'haM trAhi mAm ity uvAca ha ||
(AVParis_7,1.3)     tato 'sAv evam uktas tu prabhUtabalavardhanam | ArogyadaM bhUtikaraM kShudropadravanAshanam ||
(AVParis_7,1.4)     ArAtrikaM hi kartavyaM tasya trAtum idaM tadA | kR^itvA piShTamayaM dIpaM suvartisnehasaMyutam ||
(AVParis_7,1.5)     ati nihaH prAnyAn iti dvAbhyAm enaM pradIpayet | pAtre sapuShpe saMsthApya sarShapAMsh ca sahAkShataiH ||
(AVParis_7,1.6)     priyaN^guM shatapuShpAM ca dUrvAM caiva shatAvarIm | sapApahAriNIM bhUtiM tatraiva ca baliM nyaset ||
(AVParis_7,1.7)     apsarobhiH parivR^ito gurur gatvA puraMdaram | prAptasattvaM sumanasam Asane prAnmukhaM sthitam ||
(AVParis_7,1.8)     preto yantv ekashataM ca dIpaM samabhimantrayet | triH paribhrAmayed rAj~no mantreNAtha sumaN^galam ||
(AVParis_7,1.9)     shAmyanty asya tato rogA grahA vighnavinAyakAH | svasty astu nrparAShTrAya svasti gobrAhmaNAya ca ||
(AVParis_7,1.10)     tatas tu shaN^khadhvaninA dIpaM gR^ihItvA satoyadhArAM prayato 'pi nirharet | purohito jyotiShiko 'pi vA svayaM hitaiShinI dhAtry atharvo (pakAritA ||
(AVParis_7,1.11)     AcAmyAtha ha rAjAnam AcamyAdau purohitaH | brAhmaNAya yathAshakti rukmaM prAtaH pradApayet ||
(AVParis_7,1.12)     mUlakarmAdikaM tasya paJNcaguhyakakAritam | bhayaM rAj~no na bhavati tejo vIryaM ca vardhate ||
(AVParis_7,1.13)     evaM vidhAnam akhilaM vihitaM yathAvad etat samastashubhadaM gaditaM nrpANAm | naivApadaH samupayAnti nR^ipaM kadA cid ArAtrikaM pratinishaM kriyate tu yasya || ity ArAtrikaM samAptam ||

(ParishiShTa_8. ghR^itAvekShaNam)

(AVParis_8,1.1)     om atha ghrtAvekShaNaM vakShyAmaH ||
(AVParis_8,1.2)     prAtaHprAtaH shaN^khadundubhinAdena brahmaghoSheNa vA prabodhito rAjA shayanagR^ihAd utthAyAparAjitAM disham abhiniShkramyopAdhyAyaM pratIkSheta ||
(AVParis_8,1.3)     atha purohitaH snAtAnuliptaH shuciH shuklavAsAH krtamaN^galaviracitoShNIShI shAntigR^ihaM pravishya devAnAM namaskAraM kR^itvA svastivAcanam anuj~nApya vinItavad upavishet ||
(AVParis_8,1.4)     yamasya lokAd yathA kalAM yo na jIvo 'sIti svastyayanaM kR^itvollikhyAbhyukShya paristIrya shantAtIyena tilAn ghR^itAktAn juhuyAt ||
(AVParis_8,1.5)     tAn hutvA sauvarNarAjatam audumbaraM vA pAtraM ghR^itapUrNaM sahiraNyaM ghR^itasya jUtiH sahasrashR^iN^go yamasya lokAd uru viShNo vi kramasvety abhimantryAjyaM teja iti tadAlabhate ||
(AVParis_8,1.6)     AjyaM tejaH samuddiShTam AjyaM pApaharaM param | Ajyena devAs trpyanti Ajye lokAH pratiShThitAH ||
(AVParis_8,1.7)     bhaumAntarikShadivyaM vA yat te kalmaSham Agatam | sarvaM tad AjyasaMsparshAt praNAsham upagacchatv iti ||
(AVParis_8,1.8)     tasmin ghR^itapAtrasthaM hi sarvam AtmAnaM ca pashyet ||
(AVParis_8,1.9)     dadhnA shiro hR^idayam anvAlabhya japet ||
(AVParis_8,1.10)     uccA patantam iti dvAbhyAm
(AVParis_8,1.11)     sUryasyAvR^itam iti pradakShiNam AvR^itya sheShaM kArayed ity
(AVParis_8,1.12)     atra shlokAH ||

(AVParis_8,2.1)     ayaM ghR^itAvekShaNasya prokto vidhir atharvaNA | upAsyo nityakAlaM tu rAj~nA vijayakAN^kShiNA ||
(AVParis_8,2.2)     etat samAharet sarvaM prayatas tu samAhitaH | rAjA vijayate rAShTraM nashyante tasya shatravaH ||
(AVParis_8,2.3)     dvijottamAya kapilAM rAjA dadyAt tu gAM shubhAm | AshIrvAdaM tatas tena shrutvA tanmukhaniHsR^itam ||
(AVParis_8,2.4)     guruNA vAcito yasmAd dIrgham Ayur avApnuyAt | putrAn pautrAMsh ca maitrAMsh ca labhate nAtrasaMshayaH ||
(AVParis_8,2.5)     AyuShyam atha varcasyaM saubhAgyaM shatrutApanam | duHsvapnanAshanaM puNyaM ghR^itAsyAvekShaNaM smR^itam iti || iti ghR^itAvekShaNaM samAptam || shrIsAmba | yamasya lokAd adhy AbabhUvitha iti R^icaH 6, yathA kalAM yathA shapham iti R^icaH 6, ghR^itasya jUtir iti R^icaH 4 ghR^itAvekShaNamadhye paippalAdA mantrAH ||

(ParishiShTa_9. tiladhenuvidhiH)

(AVParis_9,1.1)     om atha tiladhenuM pravakShyAmi sarvapApapraNAshanIm | tilAH shvetAs tilAH kR^iShNAs tilA gomUtravarNakAH ||
(AVParis_9,1.2)     tilAnAM tu vicitrANAM dhenuM vatsaM ca kArayet | droNasya vatsakaM kuryAc caturdroNA tu gauH smR^itA ||
(AVParis_9,1.3)     suvAsAyAM shucau bhUmau dhUpapuShpair alaMkrtA | kR^iShNAjine tu kartavyA bahUnAM vApi kArayet ||
(AVParis_9,1.4)     karNau ratnamayau kuryAc cakShuShI dIpakau tathA | ghrANe tu sarvagndhAMs tu jihvAyAM shAradaM ghR^itam ||
(AVParis_9,1.5)     danteShu mauktikaM dadyAl lalATe tAmrabhAjanam | Udhasi tu madhUshIram apAne ca ghR^itaM madhu ||

(AVParis_9,2.1)     hR^idaye candanaM dadyAj jaN^ghayor ikShukANDakam | suvarNashR^iN^gI raupyakhurI raupyalAN^gUladakShiNA ||
(AVParis_9,2.2)     vastrachannA tu dAtavyA kAMsyapAtraM tu dohanI | 
(AVParis_9,2.3)     prajApatish cety abhimantrya viprAya dadyAt
(AVParis_9,2.4)     tatra shlokAH ||
(AVParis_9,2.5)     dhenuM vatsaM ca yo dadyAd vinAtharvAbhimantritAm | vinAnena vidhAnena devatvaM nopajAyate ||
(AVParis_9,2.6)     vishvarUpAH sthitAH sarvA dhenavaH parikIrtitAH | dhenutvaM na sa prayAti vinA sUktAbhimantritAm | niShphalaM nashyate sarvaM vinAbhimantritaM satAm ||
(AVParis_9,2.7)     bAlatve yac ca kaumAre yat pApaM yauvane kR^itam | vayaHpariNatau yac ca yac ca janmAntareShu ca ||
(AVParis_9,2.8)     yan nishAyAM tathA prAtar yan madhyAhnAparAhNayoH | saMdhyayor yat kR^itaM pApaM karmaNA manasA girA ||

(AVParis_9,3.1)     prasUyamAnAM yo dhenuM dadyAd brAhmaNapuMgave | kR^iShNAjinaM guDadhenuM ghR^itadhenuM tathaiva ca ||
(AVParis_9,3.2)     suvarNaratnadhenuM ca jaladhenuM tathA parAm | kShIradhenuM madhudhenuM sharkarAlavaNaM tathA ||
(AVParis_9,3.3)     rasAdidhenUH sarvAnyA anena vidhinA smR^itAH | yat tu bAlye kR^itaM pApaM yauvane caiva yat kR^itam ||
(AVParis_9,3.4)     mAnakUTaM tulAkUTaM kanyAnR^itagavAnR^itam | udake ShThIvitaM caiva musalaM cApi laN^ghitam ||
(AVParis_9,3.5)     vR^iShalIgamanaM caiva gurudArAniShevaNam | surApAnasya yat pApaM tiladhenuH prashAmyati ||

(AVParis_9,4.1)     yA sa yamapure ghore nadI vaitaraNI smR^itA | yatra lohamukhAH kAkAH shvAnash caiva bhayAvahAH ||
(AVParis_9,4.2)     vAlukAntAH sthalAsh caiva pacyante yatra duShkR^itaH | asipattravanaM yatra shAlUkAH shAlmalI tathA ||
(AVParis_9,4.3)     tAn sukhena vyatikramya dharmarAjAshramaM vrajet | svAgataM te mahAbhAga svasti te 'stu mahAmate ||
(AVParis_9,4.4)     vimAnam etad yogyaM te maNiratnavibhUShitam | atrAruhya narashreShTha gaccha tvaM paramAM gatim ||
(AVParis_9,4.5)     mA ca cArabhaTe dadyAn mA ca dadyAt purohite | mA ca kANe virUpe ca kuShThivyaN^ge tathaiva ca ||
(AVParis_9,4.6)     vedAntagAya dAtavyA vedAntagasutAya vA | ekaikasmai ca dAtavyA mAghamAse tu pUrNimAm ||
(AVParis_9,4.7)     ya imAM paThate nityaM yash cemAM shR^iNuyAd api | devalokam atikramya sUryalokaM sa gacchati || sUryalokaM sa gacchatIti || iti tiladhenuvidhiH samAptaH ||

(ParishiShTa_10. bhUmidAnam)

(AVParis_10,1.1)     om atha rohiNyAM sakalAyAm upoShito brahmA sarvabIjarasaratnagandhAvakIrNaM tIrthodakapUrNakalasham AdAyAtisR^iShTo apAm ity abhiShekamantrair yathoktair dAtAram abhiShiJNcati ||
(AVParis_10,1.2)     vratena tvaM vratapata iti vratam upaiti
(AVParis_10,1.3)     yAcitAradAtArAv ayAcitAshinAv adhahshAyinau bhavato
(AVParis_10,1.4)     vratopacAram
(AVParis_10,1.5)     yathAshaktyaikarAtraM paJNcarAtraM dvAdasharAtraM vA vrataM caritvA
(AVParis_10,1.6)     shvo bhUte tantram AjyabhAgAntaM kR^itvAnvArabhyAtha juhuyAt ||
(AVParis_10,1.7)     kAmasUktaM kAlasUktaM puruShasUktaM mahAvyAhR^itibhiH saMkhyApUrvikAbhiH sarva R^itvijo juhvaty
(AVParis_10,1.8)     atha suvarNamayIM bhUmiM bhUmeH pratikR^itiM gocarmamAtrAM kR^itvA
(AVParis_10,1.9)     maNDapavedyAM samAnIya vedyuttarato yasyAM vedim ity upasthApya
(AVParis_10,1.10)     girayas te parvatA iti parvatAn avasthApya
(AVParis_10,1.11)     hiraNyarajatamaNimuktApravAlAdibhir upashobhayed yad adaH saMprayatIr iti
(AVParis_10,1.12)     sA mandasAneti nadIH kalpayitvA rasaish ca paripUrayed
(AVParis_10,1.13)     apAm agram asi samudraM vo 'bhyavasR^ijAmIti samudrAn
(AVParis_10,1.14)     vanaspatiH saha devair na Agann iti bR^ihaspatineti vanaspatIn anyAMsh ca
(AVParis_10,1.15)     yaj~ne tvA manasA saMkalpayen manasA saMkalpayatItha bhavatIha bhavatIha bhavati
(AVParis_10,1.16)     nidhiM bibhratI bahudheti namaskArayitvA
(AVParis_10,1.17)     satyaM bR^ihad ity anuvAko ye devA divy ekAdasha stheti puNyAhaM vAcayet
(AVParis_10,1.18)     saMsthApayen
(AVParis_10,1.19)     nava divo devajanenety abhimantrya brAhmaNebhyo dadyAd
(AVParis_10,1.20)     dAtur esAsmai rohiNI kAmaM nikAmaM vA dugdha iti
(AVParis_10,1.21)     yathA rohanti bIjAni phAlakR^iShTe mahItale evaM kAmAH prarohante pretyeha manasaH sadA
(AVParis_10,1.22)     sarveShAm eva dAnAnAM yat phalaM samudAhR^itam | tattat prApnoti viprebhyo dattvA bhUmiM yathAvidhi || dattvA bhUmiM yathAvidhIti || iti bhUmidAnaM samAptam ||

(AVParis_11,1.1)     om athAtash tulApuruShavidhiM vyAkhyAsyAmas

(AVParis_11,1.6)     agne gobhir agne 'bhyAvartinn agneH prajAtam iti saMpAtAn udapAtrAnIyAbhiShekakalasheShu ninayed
(AVParis_11,1.7)     athAsyendro grAvabhyAm ity abhiShecayed
(AVParis_11,1.8)     idam Apo yathendro bAhubhyAm ity abhiShecayitvA
(AVParis_11,1.9)     yathoktam aJNjanAbhyaJNjanAnulepanaM kArayitvA vAso gandhasrajash cAbadhnIyAt

(AVParis_11,1.11)     acyutA dyaur iti catasR^ibhir avarohayet
(AVParis_11,1.12)     sUryasyAvR^itam iti pradakShiNam AvR^itya brAhmaNebhyo nivedayitvAtmAlaMkArAn kartre dadyAt
(AVParis_11,1.13)     sahasradakShiNaM grAmavaram
(AVParis_11,1.14)     dvijAn annena tarpayet
(AVParis_11,1.15)     atha cen niHsvapakSheNa yathA saMpadyate dhanam | dhAtubhiH saha taulyam atu vAsobhish ca rasais tathA | vrIhyAdisaptadhAnyair vA yathAsaMpadyate gR^ihe ||

(AVParis_11,2.1)     sakhaDgaH sashirastrANaH sarvAbharaNabhUShitaH | tapanIyam agare kR^itvA pashcAt tolyo narAdhipaH ||
(AVParis_11,2.2)     indreNedaM purA dattam adhirAjyAptaye varam | sarvapApapraNAshAya sarvapuNyavivR^iddhaye ||
(AVParis_11,2.3)     mahAdAnAtidAnAnAm idaM dAnam anuttamam | akShayyaphaladaM shreShThaM dAtÌNAM shreyavardhanam ||
(AVParis_11,2.4)     yat pApaM sve kule jAtais triH sapta puruShaiH kR^itam | tat sarvaM nashyate kShipram agnau tUlaM yathA tathA ||
(AVParis_11,2.5)     anAmayaM sthAnam avApya daivair alaN^ghanIyaM sukR^itair hiraNmayaiH | suvarNatejAH pravimuktapApo divIndravad rAjati sUryaloke || divIndravad rAjati sUryaleketi || iti tulApuruShavidhiH samAptaH ||

(AVParis_13,2.1)     hiraNyagarbhAya svAhA || agnaye svAhA || brahmaNe svAhA || prajApataye svAheti hutvA

(AVParis_13,2.9)     tair anuShThitaH

(AVParis_13,3.1)     ud ehi vAjinn iti dvAbhyAM praveshayet

(ParishiShTa_14. hastirathadAnavidhiH)

(AVParis_14,1.1)     om atha hastirathadAnAnAm anukramaM vakShye
(AVParis_14,1.2)     jAtarUpamayaM krtvA ekacakraM sushobhanam | hastibhiH saptabhir yuktam arcayitvA yathAvidhi ||
(AVParis_14,1.3)     atha vA caturbhir yuktaM haimaM rAjatam eva vA | aspR^iShTaM dArujaM vApi sarvasaMbhArapUritam ||
(AVParis_14,1.4)     hastiyugmena saMyuktaM saurabheyayutena vA | bhuN^kte saptaiva janmAni saptadvIpAM vasuMdharAm ||
(AVParis_14,1.5)     hastena yukte candramasi paurNamAsyAm amAvAsyAyAM vA puNye vA R^ikShe shuciH shucau deshe tantram ity uktam ||
(AVParis_14,1.6)     prAJNcam idhmam upasamAdhAyAnvArabhyAtha juhuyAt ||
(AVParis_14,1.7)     savitre svAhA || pataMgAya svAhA || pAvakAya svAhA || sahasrarashmaye svAhA || mArtaNDAya svAhA || viShNave svAhA || prajApataye svAhA || parameShThine svAhA iti hutvA.
(AVParis_14,1.8)     kanakAsh ca tilA gAvo dAsI gR^ihamahIrathAH | kanyA hastI ca vidyA ca mahAdAni vai dasha ||
(AVParis_14,1.9)     tasmAt sarveShu dAneShu anuktavidhikeShu ca | agniM brUma iti sUktam AjyatantreNa homayet ||
(AVParis_14,1.10)     ashvadAtA vrajet svargam ashvArUDhash ca mAnavaH | pUjyate devagandharvair apsarokiMnarais tathA ||
(AVParis_14,1.11)     hastivarcasaM prathatAm iti kalashe saMpAtAn AnIya yugaM yoktraM ratham iti sarvaM saMprokShya ||
(AVParis_14,1.12)     ashrAntasya tvA manasA yunajmIti yojayet ||
(AVParis_14,1.13)     ashrAntasya tvA manasA yunajmi prathamasya ca | utkUlam udvaho bhavo uduhya prati dhAvatAt ||
(AVParis_14,1.14)     yuktAyArthaM dadyAt ||
(AVParis_14,1.15)     shyAvair yuktaH shitipadbhir hiraNyayo yasya rathaH pathibhir vartate sukhaiH | sa no hastena savitA hiraNyabhug ghiraNyapANiH savitA no 'bhirakShatu ||
(AVParis_14,1.16)     bR^ihaddhastirathaM yuktaM hastena tu dadan naraH | savituH sthAnam Apnoti divyAM kAmajavAM sabhAm ||

(ParishiShTa_15. ashvarathadAnavidhiH)

(AVParis_15,1.1)     om athAshvarathadAnavidhiH.
(AVParis_15,1.2)     goShTha udakAnte shucau vA deshe prAJNcam idhmam upasamAdhAyAnvArabhyAtha juhuyAt ||
(AVParis_15,1.3)     vataraMhA bhava vAjin yujyamAna ity etenAshveShu saMpAtAn AnIyAshrAntasya tveti samAnam
(AVParis_15,1.4)     tvam indras tvaM mahendra iti savitre arghaM dattvA
(AVParis_15,1.5)     punantu mety AtmAnam Alabhya japed
(AVParis_15,1.6)     rakShantu tvAgnaya iti yajamAnam abhimantrya samR^iddhihomAnte
(AVParis_15,1.7)     varAM dhenuM kartre dadyAd ashvarathaM grAmavaraM ceti
(AVParis_15,1.8)     ya evaM vidhinA dadyAd viduShe ashvarathaM sudhIH | jyaiShThyaM shraiShThyaM ca sAmrAjyaM prajAnAm iha gacchati ||
(AVParis_15,1.9)     saptAnAM lokAnAm ante jyotirlokam anAmayam | gatvA sa paramAnandaM bhuN^kte yAvad vibhAvasuH ||

(ParishiShTa_16. gosahasravidhiH)

(AVParis_16,1.1)     om athAto gosahasravidhiH ||
(AVParis_16,1.2)     goShTha udakAnte shucau vA deshe prAJNcam idhmam upasamAdhAyAnvAlabhyAtha juhuyAt ||
(AVParis_16,1.3)     A gAva iti sUktenAjyaM juhuyAt ||
(AVParis_16,1.4)     mahAvrIhINAm aindraM caruM saumyaM ca sahasratamyAH payasi shrapayitvA gAva eva surabhava ity etena juhuyAt ||
(AVParis_16,1.5)     paJNcAnAM nadInAM tIrthodakam ||
(AVParis_16,1.6)     pashcAd agnes tIrthodakena pUrNaM kalasham avasthApya hiraNyavarNA ity abhimantrya saM vo goShTheneti dasha gAH snApayet ||
(AVParis_16,1.7)     tvaramAnanayAH samabhyukShya sahasratamyAH sAnodanekemam indra vardhaya kShatriyaM ma iti rAjAnam abhiShicya ||
(AVParis_16,1.8)     imA Apa iti ShaDbhir yothoktam aJNjanAbhyaJNjanAnulepanaM kR^itvA ||
(AVParis_16,1.9)     sahasratamIM prathamAm alaMkR^itya ||
(AVParis_16,1.10)     A gAvo mAm upatiShThantAm ity upatiShThet ||
(AVParis_16,1.11)     prajAvatIH sUyavasAd iti ca sarvAH pAyayet ||
(AVParis_16,1.12)     priyam ashanaM dattvAddhi tR^iNam aghnya iti sahasratamIm Alabhya japet ||
(AVParis_16,1.13)     mayA gAvo gopatinA sacadhvam iti mantrAnetnArghaM dattvA ||
(AVParis_16,1.14)     sahasratamyAH pucham aupasaMgR^ihya bhUmiSh TvA pratigR^ihNAtv iti japan ||
(AVParis_16,1.15)     sahasratamyAH pR^iShThato vrajan ||
(AVParis_16,1.16)     sarvAH pradakShiNIkR^itya namaskR^itya svastivAcya brAhmaNebhyo nivedya dasha gA dakShiNAM kartre dadyAt sahasratamIM vastrayugmam aca ||
(AVParis_16,1.17)     tad api shlokAH ||

(AVParis_16,2.1)     saptAjanmAnugaM pApaM puruShaiH saptabhiH krtam | tatkShaNAd vidhinAnena nAshayed goprado naraH ||
(AVParis_16,2.2)     sarveShAm eva dAnAnAM phalaM yat parikIrtitam | tad avApnoti virebhyo gosahasraprado naraH ||
(AVParis_16,2.3)     ashvamedhaM vR^iShotsargaM gosahasraM ca yaH sutaH | dadyAn madIya ity AhuH pitaras tarpayanti hi ||
(AVParis_16,2.4)     tasmAd anena vidhinA gosahasraM daden naraH | sarvapApavishuddhAtmA yAti tat paramaM padam iti ||

(ParishiShTa_17. rAjakarmasAMvatsarIyam)

(AVParis_17,1.1)     om atha pratisaMvatsaraM rAjakarmANi krameNa vakShyAmaH ||
(AVParis_17,1.2)     athAshvayuje mAse shuklapakShasya tR^itIye 'hani ||
(AVParis_17,1.3)     haridrAyavAnAm ||
(AVParis_17,1.4)     rakShantu tvAgnaya iti catasR^ibhI rakShAm ashvAnAM baddhvA hastyashvAnAM nIrAjanaM kuryAt ||
(AVParis_17,1.5)     ashvo 'si kShiprajanmAsi ....pradadyAt sa vishuddhAtmA saptadvIpAM vasuMdharAm ||
(AVParis_17,1.6)     hastena yukte candramasi paurNamAsyAm amAvAsyAyAM vA puNye nakShatre shucau deshe || tantram ity uktam ||
(AVParis_17,1.7)     prAJNcam idhmam upasamAdhAyAnvArabhAthajuhuyAt ||
(AVParis_17,1.8)     savitre svAhA || pataMgAya svAhA || pAvakAya svAhA || sahasrarashmaye svAhA || mArtaNDAya svAhA || viShNave svAhA || prajApataye svAhA || parameShThine svAheti hutvA kanakAnAM baddhvA hastyashvAnAM pUrvavan nIrAjanaM kuryAt ||

(AVParis_17,2.1)     atha navamyAm aparAhNe vAhanAni snApayitvA ahatavAsA brahmA dvAdashamitAM vediM kR^itvA || tantram ity uktam ||
(AVParis_17,2.2)     shAntikR^ityAdUShaNena vAhanaM triH prokShya parIyAn ||
(AVParis_17,2.3)     niHsAlAm iti sUktaM japan pratyetyAbhiShiJNcayed enam ||
(AVParis_17,2.4)     ashvam alaMkR^itaM shabalakaNThaM kR^itvopasthApya dadhyAd ||
(AVParis_17,2.5)     evam eva maishradhAnyAny udapAtrANy antarAsu dikShu ||
(AVParis_17,2.6)     tatraiva devatA yajet || agniM vAyuM varuNam ashvinAv iti ||
(AVParis_17,2.7)     payasi sthAlIpAkaM shrapayitvA ||
(AVParis_17,2.8)     samAs tvAgne tvaM no agne mA no vidann abhayair aparAjitair AyuShyaiH svastyayanair apratiratheneti ca hutvA saMsthApya ||
(AVParis_17,2.9)     agner ado 'sIty ahatavAsobhiH prachAdya rasaiH kumbhAn audumbarAn pUrayitvA pratidisham avasthApya mamAgne varco abhayaM dyAvApR^ithivI ud uttamaM varuNAshvinA brahmaNA yAtam iti juhuyAt ||
(AVParis_17,2.10)     paurNamAsI prathameti ca juhuyAd dundubhim AhanyAd ity uktam ||
(AVParis_17,2.11)     upa shvAsaya pR^ithivIm iti tatraivAnumantraNaM ca ||
(AVParis_17,2.12)     sarvANi ca vAditrANi vAhanAni ca ||
(AVParis_17,2.13)     janasyAn praharShaya paJNcamIM pratiShThApayet ||
(AVParis_17,2.14)     na taM yakShmA aitu deva iti guggulakShThadUpaM dadyAt ||
(AVParis_17,2.15)     yas te gandhas tryAyuSham iti bhUtiM prayacchet ||
(AVParis_17,2.16)     dUShyA dUShir asIti pratisaram Abadhya ye purastAd iti pratidishaM kShipet ||
(AVParis_17,2.17)     bahir niHsR^ityottareNa gatvA bAhyenopaniShkramya suhR^ide kuryAc chraddadhate kuryAd vAhanAnAm abhayaM karma ||

(ParishiShTa_18b. rAjakarmasAMvatsarIyam)

(AVParis_18b,1.4)     mahAm indro ya ojaseti sUktena tR^itIyAyAM hy agnau hutvA indrAya svAhetyAdi lokapAlAMsh ceShTvA rAjAnam anvAlabhya Adivaj juhuyAd arvAJNcam indram indraH sutrAmA imam indra vardhaya kShatriyaM me shataM jIvataH sarada iti ||

(AVParis_18b,1.7)     dhAtA te granthim iti badhnAti ||
(AVParis_18b,1.8)     uttaratantraM hiraNyaM dakShiNA ||

(AVParis_18b,2.1)     mahAnavamyAM hastyashvadIkShA pratipatprabhR^iti navarAtram ||

(AVParis_18b,2.3)     trtIyAyAM hastyashvavAhagrAmyAshvAnAM karma saptamyAM hastyashvAnAM darshanam ||

(AVParis_18b,6.2)     abhyAtAnAntaM kR^itvA ye 'syAM prAcI dig iti ||

(ParishiShTa_18c. vR^iShotsargaH)

(AVParis_18c,1.1)     atha vR^iShotsargaH ||
(AVParis_18c,1.2)     kArttikeyAM paurNamAsyAM raivatyAm AshvayujyAM vA gavAM goShThe paurNamAsatantram AjyabhAgAntaM kR^itvA rudraraudrAbhyAm AjyaM juhuyAt ||
(AVParis_18c,1.3)     pUShA gA anu etu na iti catasR^ibhiH pauShNasya juhuyAt ||
(AVParis_18c,1.4)     pUShA gA anu etu naH pUShA rakShAtu sarvataH | pUShA vAjaM sanotu naH ||
(AVParis_18c,1.5)     pUShann anu pra gA ihi(iti) yajamAnasya sunvataH | asmAkaM stuvatAm uta ||
(AVParis_18c,1.6)     pUShan tava vrate vayaM pari pUShA purastAd iti ||
(AVParis_18c,1.7)     indrasya kukShiH sAhasras tveSha iti R^iShabhaM saMpAtavantaM kR^itvA ya indra iva deveShu iti R^iShabhasya dakShiNe karNe japet ||
(AVParis_18c,1.8)     lohitena svadhitina iti vatsatarIm anumantrayate ||
(AVParis_18c,1.9)     ayaM prajAnAM janitA prajApatir gavAM goShTha iha madhyato vasaH | vatsatarIShu apasadane gavAm adhi tiShTha pashUn bhavanasya gopAH ||
(AVParis_18c,1.10)     iti maNDalAni bhrAmayati
(AVParis_18c,1.11)     retodhAyai tvAtisR^ijAmi vayodhAyai tvAtisR^ijAmi yUthatvAyai tvAtisR^ijAmi gaNatvAyai tvAtisR^ijAmi sahasrapoShAyai tva7atisR^ijAmi aparimitapoShAyai tvAtisR^ijAmIti paryukShyaikarUpaM dvirUpaM bahurUpaM vA yo vA yUthaM chAdayati yUthena tejasvinAlaMkR^itenAlaMkR^itam aparAjitAM dishaM niShkrAmayeyuH saha vatsatarIbhis tantraM saMsthApayeyur
(AVParis_18c,1.12)     atha brahmaNe gAM payasvinIM dadyAt pAyasena brAhmaNAn bhojayitvotsR^ijya sarvAn kAmAn Apnoti akShayAN ca lokAn ApnotIti

(ParishiShTa_19. indramahotsavaH)

(AVParis_19,1.1)     atha rAj~nam indramahotsavasya upacArakalpaM vyAkhyAsyAmaH ||
(AVParis_19,1.2)     prauShThapade shuklapakShe ||
(AVParis_19,1.3)     saMbhR^iteShu saMbhAreShu brahmA rAjA ca ubhau snAtau ahatavasanau surabhisujAtAnulepanau karmaNyau vratavantau upavasataH
(AVParis_19,1.4)     [vratavantau] shvo bhUte shamnodevyAH pAdair ardharcAbhyAm R^icA ShakR^itvodakaM pari vAcam AcAnto
(AVParis_19,1.5)     barhir upakalpayitvA rAjAnam anvAlabhya juhuyAt ||
(AVParis_19,1.6)     arvAJNcam indraM trAtAram indram indraH sutrAmA imam indra vardhaya kShatriyaM me hantAya vR^iSha indrasya indro jayAti iti ca hutvA rAShTrasaMvargaish cA
(AVParis_19,1.7)     atha indram utthApayanti A tvA ahArSham antar dhruvAdyaur vishas tvA sarvA vAJNchantu iti sarvato 'pramattA dhArayerann
(AVParis_19,1.8)     adbhutaM hi savanAnayet samutthitaM bhavati || yadi prAcyAm agnibhayam || yadi dakShiNasyAM yamabhayam || yadi pratIcyAM varuNabhayam || yadi udIcyAM kShudbhayam || yadi antardeshebhyobhayato vidyAd
(AVParis_19,1.9)     agnir mA pAtu agniM te vasumantam R^icchantv iti || yathAsvaliN^gaM dvAbhyAM-dvAbhyAM pradakShiNaM pratidisham upasthApayet ||
(AVParis_19,1.10)     gR^idhrash ced asmin nipatati mR^ityor bhayaM bhavati || yad vA kR^iShNashakunir antarikShrNa patati iti japed yas tvA gR^idhraH kapota iti antato japet
(AVParis_19,1.11)     sarvatra anAj~nAteShu trirAtraM ghR^itakambalam ||
(AVParis_19,1.12)     shirobhaN^ge tu rAjAnaM madhyabhaN^ge tu mantriNam | AdibhaN^ge janapadaM mUlabhaN^ge tu nAgarAn ||
(AVParis_19,1.13)     indrATako yadA bhidyAd rAjakosho vilupyate | rajjuchede parijAte nR^ipatis tu vinashyati ||

(AVParis_19,2.1)     sAvitryA abhimantritaM kR^itvA pradakShiNam Avartayed rAjAnam abhibhUr yaj~na iti etais tribhiH sUktair anvArabdhe rAjani pUrNahomaM juhuyAt ||

(AVParis_19,3.1)     atha pashUnAm upAcAram ||
(AVParis_19,3.2)     indradevatAH syur ye rAj~no bhR^ityAH syuH sarve dIkShitA brahmacAriNaH syur
(AVParis_19,3.3)     indraM copasadya yajeran || trirAtraM saptarAtraM vA
(AVParis_19,3.4)     trir ayanam ahnAm upatiShThante havisA ca yajante ||
(AVParis_19,3.5)     AvR^ita indram aham iti indra kShatram iti haviSho hutvA
(AVParis_19,3.6)     brAhmaNAn svastivAcya indram avabhR^ithAya vrajanti
(AVParis_19,3.7)     apAM sUktair Aplutya pradakShiNam AvR^itya apa upaspR^ishya anapekShamANAH pratyetya brAhmaNAn bhaktyA yad IpsitaM varapradAnaiH paritoShayet ||
(AVParis_19,3.8)     atha haiShamitikam iti ||
(AVParis_19,3.9)     shvaHshvo 'sya rAShTraM jyAyo bhavati eko 'syAM pR^ithivyAM rAjA bhavati na purA jarasaH pramIyate ya evaM veda yash caivaMvidvAn indramaheNa carati iti brAhmaNam ||

(ParishiShTa_19b. brahmayAgaH)

(AVParis_19b,1.1)     oM bhArgavaM praNipatyAtha bhagavA¤ shaunako 'vadat | brahmayAgavidhiM kR^itsnaM vistareNa vadasva me ||
(AVParis_19b,1.2)     paripR^iShTaH sa tena atha atharvA yajatAM varaH | vidhiM kR^itsnaM pratiShThAya AkhyAtum upacakrame ||
(AVParis_19b,1.3)     sarveShAm eva yAgAnAM paramo 'yam udAhR^itaH | brahmayAgaM prayatnena shR^iNu etaM tad yathAkramam ||
(AVParis_19b,1.4)     hR^idye manohare shubhre sarvAbAdhAvivarjite | shleShmAntakAkShagR^idhrAdiparityakte same shubhe ||
(AVParis_19b,1.5)     maNDapaM kArayet tatra yathoktavidhinA guruH | patAkAtoraNir yuktaM dvAraish ca api pR^ithagvidhaiH ||

(AVParis_19b,2.1)     abhyukShya shAntitoyena paJNcagavyena vA sakR^it | gomayena pralipya Adau pUjayed varNakiH pR^ithak ||
(AVParis_19b,2.2)     puShpaish ca vividhaiH shubhraiH phalaish ca api arcayed budhaH | tato baliM hared rAtrau caturdikShu vidhAnavit ||
(AVParis_19b,2.3)     pradIpAn ghR^itapUrNAMsh ca pradadyAd vividhAn tathA | ttato maNDapamadhye tu vartayed divyamaNDalam || [caturashraM caturdvAraM vR^ittAkAram atha api vA] ||
(AVParis_19b,2.4)     sitacUrNena tanmadhye likhet padmaM sushobhanam | bahish ca varNaiH shubhrair nAnA shobhAM prakalpayet ||
(AVParis_19b,2.5)     madhye padmaM tu saMsthApya brahmANaM parameshvaram | brahmajaj~nAnasUktena yathoktam upakalpayet ||

(AVParis_19b,3.1)     tatha imA Apa ityA dyair yathAvad adhivAsayet | rocanAcandanAdyaish ca puShpair dhUpaish ca pUjayet ||
(AVParis_19b,3.2)     ghR^itapradIpamAlyaish ca vastrair bhakShaish ca shobhanaiH | sitacandanakarpUraM dadyAd vA api hi guggulam ||
(AVParis_19b,3.3)     pradakShiNaM tataH kR^itvA namet sarvAN^gakair naraH | dakShiNe pashcime vA api bhAge vediH prashasyate ||
(AVParis_19b,3.4)     kR^itvAjyabhAgaparyantaM tataH shAntyudakaM punaH | brahmajaj~nAnasUktena kuryAc caivAtra pUjanam | tathaiva raudramantraish ca abhiShekAya kalpayet ||
(AVParis_19b,3.5)     hutvAbhyAtAnamantrAMsh ca tato rudragaNena ca | nIlarudraish caruM vidvAn vidhinA shrapayed budhaH ||

(AVParis_19b,4.1)     homayet kutsasUktena ucchuShmaish ca yathAvidhi | japen mantrAn tathAyuShyAn maN^galyAMsh cApi yatnataH ||
(AVParis_19b,4.2)     hutvA ca cAtanaM tatra mAtR^inAmagaNena ca | snApayet paJNcagavyena tathA shAntyudakena ca ||
(AVParis_19b,4.3)     phalasnAnaM ca kurvIta yukto maN^galavAdibhiH | bandibhir vedavidbhish ca strIsaNgItair manoramaiH ||
(AVParis_19b,4.4)     cArucAmarahastAbhish citradaNDaiH sadarpaNaiH | snApayed brahmasUktena raudreNApi tathArcayet ||
(AVParis_19b,4.5)     tataH pradakShiNaM kR^itvA jAnubhyAM dharaNIM gataH | AshAsyeShTaphalaM tatra yukto maN^galapAThakaiH ||

(AVParis_19b,5.1)     tUryaghoSheNa saMyuktaH kR^itasvastyayanas tathA | kuryAd dundubhinAdaM tu shaN^khabheriprapUritam ||
(AVParis_19b,5.2)     kuryAd uttaratantraM ca sadasyAn vAcayet tataH | bhojayec chaktitas tatra brAhmaNAn vedapAragAn ||
(AVParis_19b,5.3)     dInAnAthAndhakR^ipaNAn bhakShabhojyair anekadhA | annapAnavihInAMsh ca visheSheNa prapUjayet ||
(AVParis_19b,5.4)     dattvA ca dakShiNAM shaktyA dadyAd gaNabaliM nishi | gR^ihadevAs tu saMpUjyAH kAryash cApy utsavo gR^ihe ||
(AVParis_19b,5.5)     yogino bhojayet pashcAd gR^ihesu gR^ihamedhinaH | achedyAs taravaH kAryAH prANihiMsAM ca varjayet ||
(AVParis_19b,5.6)     bandhanasthAsh ca moktavyA baddhAH krodhAc ca shatravaH | abhayaM ghoShayed deshe guruM ca paripUjayet ||
(AVParis_19b,5.7)     abhayaM sarvato dattvA iShTe ca parameshvare | dIrgham Ayur avApnoti kR^itsnAM bhuN^kte vasuMdharAm ||
(AVParis_19b,5.8)     brahmayAgavidhiH kR^itsno bhaktAnAM tu mayoditaH | atharvaNA surendrAya praNatAya shubhecchayA ||
(AVParis_19b,5.9)     kR^itAbhiShekaH kR^itayAga eSha kR^itAhhnikaH kR^itarakShaH sureshaH | atharvaNo 'nugraham Ashu labdhvA triviShTapaM virarAjAsapatnam || iti ||

(ParishiShTa_20. skandayAgaH or dhUrtakalpaH)

(AVParis_20,1.1)     athAto dhUrtakalpaM vyAkhyAsyAmaH ||
(AVParis_20,1.2)     caturShucaturShu mAseShu phAlguNAShADhakArttikapUrvapakSheShu nityaM kurvIta ||
(AVParis_20,1.3)     shvo bhUte ShaShThyAm upavAsaM kR^itvA prAgudIcIM dishaM niShkramya shucau deshe manohare noShare maNDalaM trayodasharatniM kR^itvA madhye maNDapasya sarvavAnaspatyAM mAlAM kR^itvA ghaNTApatAkAsrajaH pratisaraM ca mAlApR^iShThe kR^itvA madhye darpaNAMsh copakalpayitvA tatra yaM vahanti hayAH shvetA ity AvAhayet ||

(AVParis_20,2.1)     yaM vahanti hayAH shvetA nityayuktA manojavAH | tam ahaM shvetasaMnAhaM dhUrtam AvAhayAmy aham ||
(AVParis_20,2.2)     yaM vahanti gajAH siMhA vyAghrAsh cApi viShANinaH | tam ahaM siMhasaMnAhaM dhUrtam AvAhayAmy aham ||
(AVParis_20,2.3)     yaM vahanti mayUrAsh ca citrapakShA vihaMgamAH | tam ahaM citrasaMnAhaM dhUrtam AvAhayAmy aham ||
(AVParis_20,2.4)     yaM vahanti sarvavArNAH sadAyuktA manojavAH | tam ahaM sarvasaMnAhaM dhUrtam AvAhayAmy aham ||
(AVParis_20,2.5)     yasyAmoghA sadA shaktir nityaM ghaNtApatAkinI | tam ahaM shaktisaMnAhaM dhUrtam AvAhayAmy aham ||
(AVParis_20,2.6)     yash ca mAtR^igaNair nityaM sadA parivR^ito yuvA | tam ahaM mAtR^ibhiH sArdhaM dhUrtam AvAhayAmy aham ||
(AVParis_20,2.7)     yash ca kanyAsahasreNa sadA parivR^ito mahAn | tam ahaM siMhasaMnAhaM dhUrtam AvAhayAmy aham ||
(AVParis_20,2.8)     AyAtu devaH sagaNaH sasainyaH savAhanaH sAnucaraH pratItaH | ShaDAnano 'ShTAdashalocanash ca suvarNavarNo laghupUrNabhAsaH ||
(AVParis_20,2.9)     AyAtu devo mama kArttikeyo brahmaNyapitraiH saha mAtR^ibhish ca | bhrAtrA vishAkhena ca vishvarUpa imaM baliM sAnucara juShasva ||
(AVParis_20,2.10)     saMvishasveti saMveshayet ||

(AVParis_20,3.1)     saMvishasva varaghaNTApsaraHstave yatra subhujo hi nirmitAH | saMviShTo me dhehi dIrgham AyuH prajAM pashUMsh caiva vinAyakasena ||
(AVParis_20,3.2)     imA Apa iti gandhodakaM pAdyaM dadyAt || pratigR^ihNAtu bhagavAn devo dhUrta iti || Shat caiva hiraNyavarNA itIme divyo gandharva iti gandhAn yas te gandha iti cemAH sumanasa iti sumanasaH || priyaM dhAtur iti... ||
(AVParis_20,3.3)     vanaspatir aso medhya iti dhUpam || yakShyeNa te divA agniH shukrash ceti dIpam || yo vishvataH supratIka iti parNAni ||
(AVParis_20,3.4)     prakShAlya haviShy upasAdayed dadhyodanaM kShIrodanaM guDodanaM mudgapayasamishradhAnyamodakAni sarvagandhAn sarvarsAn udakapUrNaM mUlapurNaM puShpapUrNaM phalapUrNaM rasapUrNaM copakalpayitvA
(AVParis_20,3.5)     indraH sItam ity ullikhya agne prety agniM praNIya prajvalya prAJNcam idhmam upasamAdhAya bhaga etam idhmam iti tisR^ibhir etam idhmaM sugArhaspatya ity upasamAdhAya samiddho agnir iti samiddham anumantrayate ||

(AVParis_20,4.1)     bhadram icchanto hiraNyagarbho mamAgne varcas tvayA manyo yas te manyo yad devA devaheDanam iti Shat kAmasUktAdayo dasha mahIpataye svAhA ||
(AVParis_20,4.2)     dhUrtAya skandAya vishAkhAya pinAkasenAya bhrAtR^istrIkAmAya svacchandAya varaghaNtAya nirmilAya lohitagAtrAya shalakaTaN^kaTAya svAheti hutvA agnaye prajApataye ye devA divy ekAdasha stheti anumataye agnaye sviShTakR^ita iti ca ||

(AVParis_20,5.1)     shivAgnikR^ittikAnAM tu stoShyAmi varadaM shubham | sa me stuto vishvarUpaj sarvAn arthAn prayacchatu ||
(AVParis_20,5.2)     dhanadhAnyakulAn bhogAn sa me vacanavedanam | dAsIdAsaM tathA sthAnaM maNiratnaM surAJNjanam ||
(AVParis_20,5.3)     ye bhaktyA bhajante dhUrtaM brahmaNyaM ca yashasvinam | sarve te dhanavantaH syuH prajAvanto yashasvinaH ||
(AVParis_20,5.4)     yathendras tu varAn labdhvA prItas tu bhagavAn purA | dehi me vipulAn bhogAn bhaktAnAM ca visheShata iti ||
(AVParis_20,5.5)     kAmasUktenopahAram upaharet ||
(AVParis_20,5.6)     upahAram imaM deva mayA bhaktyA niveditam | pratigR^ihya yathAnyAyam akruddhaH sumanA bhava ||

(AVParis_20,6.1)     sadyojAtaM prapadyAmi sadyojAtAya vai namaH | bhavebhave nAdibhave bhajasva mAM bhavodbhaveti bhavAya namaH ||
(AVParis_20,6.2)     devaM prapadye varadaM prapadye skandaM prapadye ca kumAram ugram | ShaNNAM sutaM kR^ittikAnAM ShaDAsyam agneH putraM sAdhanaM gopathoktaiH ||
(AVParis_20,6.3)     raktAni yasya puShpANi raktaM yasya vilepanam | kukkuTA yasya raktAkShAH sa me skandaH prasIdatu ||
(AVParis_20,6.4)     AgneyaM kR^ittikAputram aindraM ke cid adhIyate | ke cit pAshupataM raudraM yo 'si so 'si namo 'stu ta iti ||
(AVParis_20,6.5)     svAmine namaH shaN^karAyAgniputrAya kR^ittikAputrAya namaH ||
(AVParis_20,6.6)     bhagavAn kva cid apratirUpaH svAhA bhagavAn kva cid apratirUpaH ||
(AVParis_20,6.7)     maNiratnavarapratirUpaH || kAJNcanaratnavarapratirUpa iti ||
(AVParis_20,6.8)     ete [te] deva gandhA etAni puShpANy eSha dhUpa etAM mAlAM triH pradakShiNAM kR^itvA AdityakartitaM sUtram iti pratisaram AbadhnIyAt ||

(AVParis_20,7.1)     AdityakartitaM sUtram indreNa trivR^itIkR^itam | ashvibhyAM grathito granthir brahmaNA pratisaraH kR^itaH ||
(AVParis_20,7.2)     dhanyaM yashasyam AyuShyam ashubhasya ca ghAtanam | badhnAmi pratisaram imaM sarvashatrunibarhanam ||
(AVParis_20,7.3)     rakShobhyash ca pishAcebhyo gandharvebhyas tathaiva ca | manuShyebhyo bhayaM nAsti yac ca syAd duShkR^itaM kR^itam ||
(AVParis_20,7.4)     svakR^itAt parakR^itAc ca duShkR^itAt pratimucyate | sarvasmAt pAtakAn mukto bhaved vIras tathaiva ca ||
(AVParis_20,7.5)     abhicArAc ca kR^ityAtaH strIkR^itAd ashubhaM ca yat | tAvat tasya bhataM nAsti yAvat sUtraM sa dhArayet ||
(AVParis_20,7.6)     yAvad Apash ca gAvash ca yAvat sthAsyanti parvatAH | tAvat tasya bhayaM nAsti yaH sUtraM dhArayiShyatIti ||
(AVParis_20,7.7)     anvAyaM bhuktvA devaM visarjayet ||
(AVParis_20,7.8)     pramodo nAma gandharvaH pradoSho paridhAvati | muJNca shailamayAt pApan muJNcamuJNca pramuJNca ca ||
(AVParis_20,7.9)     [yAvat] imA ApaH pavanena pUtA hiraNyavarNA anavadyarUpAH | tAvad imaM dhUrtaM pravAhayAmi pravAhito me dehi varAn yathoktAn ||
(AVParis_20,7.10)     uditeShu nakShatreShu gR^ihAn praviShTo gR^ihiNIM pashyet dhanavati dhanaM me dehIti ||
(AVParis_20,7.11)     yad bhoktuM kAmajAtaM jagatyAM manasA saMhIhate tattad dvijanmA pinAkasenayajamAnAt kAmam upabhukto bhuktvAmR^itatvaM tadvad evAbhyupaiti ||

(ParishiShTa_21. saMbhAralakShaNam)

(AVParis_21,1.1)     oM saMbhArAn kIrtayiShyAmo yathAlakShaNasaMyutAn | yaiH karma kriyamANaM hi phalavat syAd dvijanmanAm ||
(AVParis_21,1.2)     achinnAgrAn kushAn ArdrAn indranIlasamaprabhAn | shuShkAn api shvetavarNAn AhuH shAntikarAn budhAH ||
(AVParis_21,1.3)     surabhINi ca puShpANi susvAdUni phalAni ca manoharANi vAsAMsi saMbhAreShUpakalpayet ||
(AVParis_21,1.4)     surabhINy eva bIjAni anyavastUni yAni ca | arghacandanadhUpAdi hemaratnAdi cottamam ||
(AVParis_21,1.7cd)     gAvash ca dakShiNArthaM hi payasvinyaH sulakShaNAH |
(AVParis_21,1.8ab)     ShoDashAShTau ca catvArash caturNAM vedavittamAH ||
(AVParis_21,1.5)     R^itvijas tu samAkhyAtA vayaHshIlaguNAnvitAH | dvAtriMshat ShoDashAShTau vA shAntikArye tathAdbhute ||
(AVParis_21,1.6)     sahiraNyAH savastrAsh ca sAlaMkArAH savatsakAH | te sadasyA iti proktA vAcane yaj~nakarmaNi ||
(AVParis_21,1.7ab)     sarve te 'pi hy atharvANa R^itvijaH ShoDasha smR^itAH |
(AVParis_21,1.8cd)     shuddhAtmAno japair homair vaidikair vItamatsarAH ||

(AVParis_21,2.1)     tAmrarAjatahaimAnAM mR^inmayAnAm athApi vA | achidrANAM savarNAnAM kalashAnAM ca saMgrahaH ||
(AVParis_21,2.2)     carUNAm atha pAtrANAm indhanAnAM visheShataH | yavavrIhitila''AdInAm AjyasyAharaNaM tathA ||
(AVParis_21,2.3)     achidrAsphAtitAvakrA dIrghaparvAH sumadhyamAH | shamIdUrvAtarUNAM tu j~neyAH shAntau shabhAvAH ||
(AVParis_21,2.4)     puShkaratantugovAlatruTisarShapayavasya tu | ShaDguNitaHShaDguNito [bhavati] narasyAN^gulamAne ||
(AVParis_21,2.5)     gopucchasadR^isho daNDaH samaH shlakShNo manoharaH | sruvash ca shAntuke j~neyaH srug uktA yaj~nalakShaNA ||

(AVParis_21,3.1)     sauvarNaH shAntike proktaH pAlasho vAtha khAdiraH | abhicAre visheSheNa kuryAt sruvam ayomayam ||
(AVParis_21,3.2)     kAMsyaM yccATane kuryAd AshvatthaM vashyakarmaNi | visheSheNa tu vidveShe sruvo nimbamayaH smR^itaH ||
(AVParis_21,3.3)     pauShTike rAjataM vidyAt tAmraM ca vijayAvaham | amR^itAdau tu vij~neyash cAndanaH siddhidaH sruvaH ||
(AVParis_21,3.4)     sruvANAM viShayaM j~nAtvA kIlakAnAM vidhiM tathA | gR^ihasyAshmavidhiM dikShu karmasiddhim avApnuyAt ||
(AVParis_21,3.5)     shleShmAtakArkakaNTakikaTutiktAdivarjite | ariShTagR^idhrakaushikavihaMgaish ca vivarjite ||

(AVParis_21,4.1)     gulmavallIlatAyukte hR^idyaish ca madhurair drumaiH | taruNaiH phalavadbhish ca shmashAnAsthivivarjite ||
(AVParis_21,4.2)     mayUracakravAkAdihaMsakAraNDavAdibhiH | susvarair nAdite deshe hR^idyAN^kurasamanvite ||
(AVParis_21,4.3)     nadItaTe samudrasya saMgame vA visheShataH | anindye digvibhAge ca uttare vAparAjite ||
(AVParis_21,4.4)     bhUmiM saMshodhayet kartA prAgudakppravaNe shubhe | prAcIM saMshodhya yatnena maNDapaM tatra kArayet ||
(AVParis_21,4.5)     navakoShThaM samaM vApi hastaiH ShoShashabhir mitam | caturashraM caturdvAram ekordhvadvAram eva vA ||

(AVParis_21,5.1)     tata IshAnakoNe tu snAnavediM samAcaret | dashadvAdashahastaM vA yathAvitAnam eva vA ||
(AVParis_21,5.2)     caturguNocchrayAsh caiva mUlastambhAs tu ye tataH | upastambhAs tu ye pArshve tadardhena prakIrtitAH ||
(AVParis_21,5.3)     kumbhAH stambhais tathA deyAH kAmair dvAraM dishAM smR^itam | yajamAnocchrayaM vApi tadardhena prakIrtitAH ||
(AVParis_21,5.4)     kuNDAkR^iti gR^ihaM kuryAd dviguNaM pariveShtitam | sarvadikShu plavaM caiva kuNDasyordhvaM na chAdayet ||

(AVParis_21,6.1)     parito dvAdashasthUnaM catu[H]stambhaM tu madhyataH | arcitaM pUjitaM nityaM shAntau shAntigR^ihaM smR^itam ||
(AVParis_21,6.2)     netrAdyullocashobhiShThaM nAnAvarNadhvajAkulam | raktA pItA ca dhUmrA ca kR^iShNA nIlAtha pANDurA ||
(AVParis_21,6.3)     vicitrA hIndranIlAbhA patAkAH ShoDasha smR^itAH | [aindrAyudhadhUmrakR^iShNanIlapANDuravarNakAH] ||
(AVParis_21,6.4)     [pItaraktasitAH shyAmA patAkAH ShoDasha smR^itAH |] kalashAn ShoDashAn tatra upariShTAn mahAdhvajaH ||
(AVParis_21,6.5)     vastreNAchAditAn kuryAt sahiraNyAn pR^ithakpR^ithak | maNimuktAphalaiH puShpair hR^idyaish ca madhuraiH phalaiH ||
(AVParis_21,6.6)     samantAd dikShu vinyastaiH pradIpaish cApy alaMkR^itam | dhUpair balyupahAraish ca jayaghoShaish ca bandinAm ||
(AVParis_21,6.7)     shaN^khatUryaninAdais tu vINAdundubhisasmitaiH | pUjyamAno hi nR^ipatiH pravishet sapurohitaH ||
(AVParis_21,6.8)     tataH shAntyudakaM kR^itvA cAtanenAnuyojitam | saMprokShya vidhivan mantrair Anayed araNI tataH ||

(AVParis_21,7.1)     mathite 'gnau vidhAnena shAntyudakena samantrakam | homaM kR^itvA yathoktaM tu nimittAny upalakShayet ||
(AVParis_21,7.2)     meghadundubhinirghoShaiH prajvalan sarvatas tathA | avyavachinnadIrghArciH susnigdhaH siddhikArakaH ||
(AVParis_21,7.3)     kiMshukAshokapadmAbho nIlotpalanibhas tathA | vahniH siddhikaro j~neyaH saptarAtrAn na saMshayaH ||
(AVParis_21,7.4)     hutamAtre prajvalati vihasann iva dR^ishyate | taM vidyAt siddhidaM vahniM padmavarNanibhaM tathA ||
(AVParis_21,7.5)     asnigdhArciH sadhUmo yaH kR^iShNavarNo 'pradakShiNaH | yathoktaviparItas tu na vahniH syAt prayaMkaraH ||
(AVParis_21,7.6)     yasmin prasannatAm eti hUyamAne hutAshane | tatra nityaM mahAsiddhir asamApte vinirdishet || asamApte vinirdishet || iti saMbhAralakShaNaM samAptam ||

(ParishiShTa_22. araNilakShaNam)

(AVParis_22,1.1)     om athAtaH saMpravakShyAmi araNyosh caiva lakShaNam | rUpam athA pramANaM ca guNadoShAn tathaiva ca ||
(AVParis_22,1.2)     coditAn shabdashAstreNa AcAryeNa tu dhImatA | purA kalpe ca yad dR^iShTam R^iShibhish caiva lakShaNam ||
(AVParis_22,1.3)     gR^ihyAgniM parisaMgR^ihya dharmapatnyA sahaiva tu | vaitAnikAs tataH kuryAd AdhAnAdyA yathoditAH ||
(AVParis_22,1.4)     tithau shubhAyAM nakShatre dishaM gatvA tv aninditAm | ashvatthAt tu shamIgarbhAd uktam AharaNaM shruteH ||
(AVParis_22,1.5)     shamIvR^ikShe tu yo 'shvattho nAnyavR^ikSheNa saMyutaH | madhye mUlaM na bAhye tu sa garbhaH parikIrtitaH ||

(AVParis_22,2.1)     abhAve tu shamIgarbhe ashvatthAd eva vAharet | prApte caiva shamIgarbhe samAropya visarjayet ||
(AVParis_22,2.2)     caturviMshAN^gulA dIrghA vistareNa ShaDaN^gulA | caturaN^gulocchrayA ca araNish cottarAraNiH ||
(AVParis_22,2.3)     A skandhAd uraso vApi iti staudAyanaiH smR^itA | bAhumAtrA devadarshair jAjalair UrumAtrikA ||
(AVParis_22,2.4)     cAraNavaidyair jaN^ghe ca maudenAShTAN^gulAni ca | jaladAyanair vitastir vA ShoDasheti tu bhArgavaH ||
(AVParis_22,2.5)     shiraHpramANe nAbhau tu caturviMshatikaiva hi | shaunakAdibhir AcAryair etan mAnaM prakIrtitam ||

(AVParis_22,3.1)     tasyAs tu piNDaH ShaDbhAge caturbhAge tu vistare | caturashrA ca shlakShNA ca chidragranthivivarjitA ||
(AVParis_22,3.2)     klinnA bhinnAgnisaMspR^iShTA sphuTitA vidyutA hatA | anyaish ca doShaiH saMyuktA varjanIyA prayatnataH ||
(AVParis_22,3.3)     shirogranthir harec cakShush chidrA patnIvinAshinI | klinnA vinAshayet putrAn sphuTitA shokam Avahet ||
(AVParis_22,3.4)     UrdhvashuShke na kartavyA kR^iShNe rUkShe tathaiva ca | ubhe apy ekavR^ikShe ca araNish cottarAraNiH ||
(AVParis_22,3.5)     tatpramANA tadardhA vA bhUyasI vA yathecchayA | anenaiva tu manthavyo na kuryAd yonisaMkaram ||

(AVParis_22,4.1)     yonisaMkarasaMkIrNe mahAn doShaH prapadyate | sa yaj~nas tAmaso nAma phalaM tatra na vidyate ||
(AVParis_22,4.2)     piNDe tv ayanaviShuvau pR^ithutve R^itavaH sthitAH | ardhamAsAsh ca dIrghatve kAlash cAtra pratiShThitaH ||
(AVParis_22,4.3)     yajamAno 'raNir iti vadanty eke vipashcitaH | tatpradhAnAH kriyAH sarvA yaj~nash cApi tathaiva hi ||
(AVParis_22,4.4)     prathame mUlaShaDbhAge pAdau jaN^gheti kIrtyate | dvitIye jAnunI UrU tR^itIye shroNir ucyate ||
(AVParis_22,4.5)     caturthe jaTharaM sAN^gaM grIvA caiva tu paJNcame | ShaShthe shiraH samAkhyAtam aN^gAny etAni nirdishet ||

(AVParis_22,5.1)     mathite pAdajaN^ghe ca pishAcaH saMprajAyate | jAnunosh ca tathA corvo rAkShastvaM prayAti hi ||
(AVParis_22,5.2)     shroNyAM ca sarvakAmA[H] syur jaThare kShut tathA smR^itA | urasy amitrA grIvAyAM mR^ityuH shirasi vedanA ||
(AVParis_22,5.3)     shroNyAm evAta aicchanti nirdoShA kIrtitA yataH | tathA vittapashUn putrAn svargam AyuH priyaM sukham ||
(AVParis_22,5.4)     prathamaM manthanaM shroNyAm AdhAne ca visheShataH | itarANi yatheShtaM hi grIvAM sarvatra varjayet ||
(AVParis_22,5.5)     trINy aN^gulAni tyaktvAdau tathA catvAri cAntataH | madhye devAH sthitAs tasmAd vahniM tatraiva manthayet ||

(AVParis_22,6.1)     anulomA bhaved yoniH pArshvabhedo na vidyate | Anulomyena mathitaH sarvAn kAmAn prayacchati ||
(AVParis_22,6.2)     mUlAd aN^gulam utsR^ijya trINitrINi ca pArshvayoH | devayonis tu vij~neyA tatra mathyo hutAshanaH ||
(AVParis_22,6.3)     [mUlAt tyaktvAN^gulAny aShTau agrAt tu dvAdashaiva hi | antare devayoniH syAt tatra mathyo hutAshanaH] ||
(AVParis_22,6.4)     vedA yaj~nAya saMbhUtA yaj~nA agnau pratiShThitAH | araNyor jAyate cAgnis tayos tasmAt pradhAnatA ||
(AVParis_22,6.5)     araNyardhena caiva syuH khAdirau cAtrapIDakau | netraM tu ShaDguNaM cAtrAd uttaro 'ShTAN^gulaH smR^itaH ||

(AVParis_22,7.1)     aShTAN^gulaH pramanthaH syAc cAtraM syAd dvAdashAN^gulam | ovIlI dvAdashAN^gulA eSha yaj~navidhiH smR^itaH ||
(AVParis_22,7.2)     vyAmamantraM vadanty eke anye hastatrayaM viduH | trivR^itaM muShTisaMyuktaM yaj~navR^ikShajavalkalaiH ||
(AVParis_22,7.3)     cAtre ca bhAskarAH proktA uttare vasavas tathA | netre devagaNAH sarve viShNush caiva tu pIDake ||
(AVParis_22,7.4)     araNir yA dvitIyA tu uttarA sA prakIrtitA | tatraikadeshaM saMgR^ihya uttaraH sa ca kIrtitaH ||
(AVParis_22,7.5)     prAÇmukhodaÇmukho vApi bhrAmakaH pashcimAmukhaH | pANibhyAM pIDanaM shubhram uttarAgraM pragR^ihya tu ||

(AVParis_22,8.1)     mUle mUlaM tu saMyojya cAtrasyaivottarasya ca | araNyupari saMsthApya pIDakena tu pIDayed ||
(AVParis_22,8.2)     netreNa bhrAmayec cAtraM yAvad vahniH prajAyate | sarvair hi devaiH saMpannas tena sarvasukhaH smR^itaH ||
(AVParis_22,8.3)     brahmAdyair daivataish caiva vidvadbhish ca tapodhanaiH | eSha yantraprayogas tu dR^iShTo yaj~nArthahetubhiH ||
(AVParis_22,8.4)     yajamAnena manthavyaH svashAkhAshrotriyeNa vA | tanmantrena dvijAgryair vA smR^itam etad dhi manthanam ||
(AVParis_22.9.1)     (atha) yady araNI jIrNe syAtAM jantubhir manthanena vA || samAnIte nave araNI AhR^itya shve bhUte darshenAShTvA tasmin pUrve shakalIkR^itya gArhapatye prakShipyopary agnau dhArayan japati ||
(AVParis_22,9.2)     ud budhyasvAgne pra vishasya yonyAM devayajyAyai voDhave jAtavedaH | araNyor araNI saM carasva jIrNAM tvacam ajIrNayA nir Nudasvety
(AVParis_22,9.3)     AjyaM saMskR^ityAhavanIye manasvatIM juhoti || [putrArthI shrAvayet] ||
(AVParis_22,9.4)     mano jyotir juShatAm Ajyasya vichinnaM yaj~naM sam imaM dadhAtu | yA iShTA uShaso yA aniShTAs tAH saM cinomi haviShA ghR^itena svAheti agnaye 'gnimate 'ShTAkapAlaM puroDAshaM nirvapati || sharAv odanaM sadakShiNaM dadAti || sA prakR^iteShtiH saMgR^ihyate ||

(AVParis_22,10.1)     prasaN^genaiva kathitam agnimanthanam atra vai | araNyosh cAN^gasaMbhUtaM netraM cAtraM ca pIDakaH ||
(AVParis_22,10.2)     ya idaM dhArayiShyati araNyor iha lakShaNam | na tasya durlabhaM kiM cid loke paratra ca ||
(AVParis_22,10.3)     putrArthI shrAvayen nityam acirAl labhate sutam | shrutashIlaM vR^ittavantaM dIrghAyur vipulAM prajAm ||
(AVParis_22,10.4)     etad evaM samAkhyAtaM pippalAdena dhImatA | dvijAnAM bAlavR^iddhAnAM purashcaraNam uttamam ||
(AVParis_22,10.5)     adhItyaitac ca dehAnte paraM brahmAdhigacchati | na tasya mR^ityur na jarA nidrA vyAdhir na caiva hi | kShutpipAsAbhayaM nAsti brahmabhUtaH sa tiShThati ||

(ParishiShTa_23. yaj~napAtralakShaNam)

(AVParis_23,1.1)     om athAto yaj~napAtrANAM lakShaNaM yonir eva ca | rUpaM tathA pramANaM ca kramenaiva prakathyate ||
(AVParis_23,1.2)     camasagrahapAtrANi homapAtrANi yAni ca | yaj~navR^ikShAs tathA shAkhA brahmavede pradarshitAH ||
(AVParis_23,1.3)     pitR^ipiNDeShu darvyAdyam agniShvAttaM ca yAj~nikam | sAyaMhomeShu nityAni tathA naimittikAni ca ||
(AVParis_23,1.4)     bilvAkR^itish caruH proktas tAmro vA mR^inmayo 'pi vA | grIvAyAM mukhavistIrNash carusthAlIti kIrttitaH ||
(AVParis_23,1.5)     kushasyAmrasya vA parNair veNor vA balbajasya vA | catuShkoNArdhavItaM ca loke shUrpaM tad ucyate ||

(AVParis_23,2.1)     asiH khaDgaM ca nistriMshaH paryAyAH parikIrttitAH | tadAkR^iTy eva yad rUpaM yaj~ne sphyaM ca vadanti tam ||
(AVParis_23,2.2)     idhmocchrayam ardhakhAtaM khAtenaiva tu vistaraH | madhye hInaM tathordhvAgraM vAraNaM tad ulUkhalam ||
(AVParis_23,2.3)     sthUlatvAn muShTimAtraM ca skandhamAtraM pramANataH | vAraNaM musalaM caiva adhastAl lohaveShTitam ||
(AVParis_23,2.4)     sruvas tu mUladaNDash ca bilaM cAN^guShThaparvaNaH | samavete pR^ithagbhUte bilArdhe daNDavR^ittatA ||
(AVParis_23,2.5)     vaikaN^katI dhruvA proktA sarvayaj~neShu yA smR^itA | tathAgnihotrahavaNI sruvash cApi tathA smR^itaH ||

(AVParis_23,3.1)     mUladaNDA tvagbilA ca puShkaraM caturaN^gulam | puShkarAd dviguNaM cAgraM gajoShThaM paripaThyate ||
(AVParis_23,3.2)     [netrAdikaraNair hInaM nAsikAbhyAM dvijais tathA | dvyaN^gulaH khAtA ca bilAd aN^gulaM caiva piNDikA | vR^ittA vA caturashrA vA sAdhastAc chobhanA smR^itA] ||
(AVParis_23,3.3)     ardhAN^gulaM pR^ithutvena bilabAhyaM samantataH | bilaM vR^ittaM sruco madhye daNDasthaulyaM bilArdhataH ||
(AVParis_23,3.4)     caturviMshatyaN^gulaM daNDaM vadanty eke manIShiNaH | saptatriMshad aN^gulAni sA sruk caiva prakIrtitA ||
(AVParis_23,3.5)     bhinnA vishIrNA vakrA ca klinnA ca sphuTitA tathA | suShirA granthibhir yuktA cakShurAdivinAshinI ||

(AVParis_23,4.1)     dagdhasheShe 'rdhashuShke ca vidyutA caiva pAtite | unmUlye patite bhagne manasApi na cintayet ||
(AVParis_23,4.2)     shubhanakShatrAtithiShu shubhAM gatvA dishaM budhaH | sruvArthaM pAtayed vR^ikShaM prAtaH prAgraM ca saumyavAk ||
(AVParis_23,4.3)     mR^igo hariNarurush ca kR^iShNapR^iShThashiras tathA | yat tasya carma tvak caiva tat kR^iShNAjinam ucyate ||
(AVParis_23,4.4)     vAmamuShTigR^ihItAs tu prachidyante sakR^it kushAH | parashunAsinA vA tat sakR^idAchinnam ucyate ||
(AVParis_23,4.5)     aN^guShThaparvAgramukhaM darvyAkR^iti tu mekShaNam. vaikaN^kate pAlAshe vA prAdeshas tu pramANataH ||

(AVParis_23,5.1)     alAbu vaiNavaM vApi dArvyaM vaiNavam eva vA | akShAv amaNDalau proktau yathA dR^iShTaM pura rShibhiH ||
(AVParis_23,5.2)     cakrAbhyAM kAShThasaMghAtaiH shilpibhish caiva yat kR^itam | loke prasiddhaM shakaTam agniShThaM yAj~nike vidhau ||
(AVParis_23,5.3)     AjyaM ghR^itaM vijAnIyAn navanItaM susaMskR^itam | sauvIrAdy aJNjanaM caiva atha vA daivikaM tathA ||
(AVParis_23,5.4)     abhyaJNjanaM ca tat praktaM tilatailaM ca yad viduH | AsanaM kashipu proktaM kAyasthaM copabarhaNam ||
(AVParis_23,5.5)     yavodarair aShTabhis tu aN^gulaM paripaThyate | carutviMshatyaN^gulaM tu yAj~nikair hasta AkR^itaH ||

(AVParis_23,6.1)     hastamAtraM sruvaH khaDgaM sakR^idAchinnam eva ca | bAhumAtrA juhUH proktA dhruvA barhis tathaiva ca ||
(AVParis_23,6.2)     tAmrash caiva sruvaH proktaH khaDgaM khAdiram eva ca | pAlAshI ca juhUH kAryA idhmAsh caiva visheShataH ||
(AVParis_23,6.3)     grahAH pAtrANi camasA daNDayUpAsanAni ca | vR^ikSheShu yAj~nikeShu syur yathAlAbheShu nAnyataH ||
(AVParis_23,6.4)     samidhaH prAdeshamAtryo nityahome prakIrtitAH | samillakShaNadR^iShTAni pramANAni yathAkramam ||
(AVParis_23,6.5)     shamy ashvattha[H] palAshash ca khAdiro 'tha vikaN^kataH | kAshmaryodumbaro bilvo yaj~navR^ikShAH prakIrtitAH ||

(AVParis_23,7.1)     eShAm alAbhe vR^ikShANAm anye grAhyAs tu yAj~nikaiH | yaj~nAN^gakArye draShTavyAH samidarthaM visheShataH ||
(AVParis_23,7.2)     yavavrIhimahAvrIhiprayaN^gUNAM hi taNDulAH | shyAmAkataNDulatilA AsAdyAH shruticoditAH ||
(AVParis_23,7.3)     sAyaMhomeShu yad dravyaM prAtarhomeShu tad bhavet | bhinnadravyahutaM yat tu na hutaM tasya tad bhavet ||
(AVParis_23,7.4)     udite 'nudite caiva samayAdhyuShite tathA | kShudhAkAle tathApy keke pakShahomaM tu kArayet ||
(AVParis_23,7.5)     yAyAvarANAM munibhiH pakShahomas tu taiH smR^itaH | yathA kathaM cid vacanaM shrutyuktaM dvija AcAret ||

(AVParis_23,8.1)     AturaH pathikash caiva rAjopadravapIDitaH | pakShahomaM tadA kuryAn nistIrya satataM caret ||
(AVParis_23,8.2)     caturdashagR^ihItaM tu sakR^id unnayate haviH | ekA samit sakR^id dhomaH so 'rdhamAsAya kalpate ||
(AVParis_23,8.3)     caturdashaguNaM kR^itvA srucA pAtreNa pUrvavat | evaM gArhapatye ca dakShiNAgnau ca juhvati ||
(AVParis_23,8.4)     pUrvA hutvAhutIH sAyaM vyuShTAyAm apare 'hni | etenaiva vidhAnena juhvati prAtarAhutIH ||
(AVParis_23,8.5)     R^iShibhish ca purA dR^iShTam ApatkAleShu sarvataH | araNyosh ca samAropya shrutidR^iShTena karmaNA ||

(AVParis_23,9.1)     homArtheShv etad draShTavyam AhitAgnigR^iheShv api | tatprayojanamAtraM tu na doShaH sUtakeShu ca ||
(AVParis_23,9.2)     sadyaHshaucAdikaM proktaM sUtakaM ca dvijAtibhiH | svayaMhomIti vacanAn na doShaH shruticodanAt ||
(AVParis_23,9.3)     vratinAM sattriNAM caiva mahArAjAhitAgnayaH | eShAM doSho na vidyeta sAyamprAtaH kriye sthite ||
(AVParis_23,9.4)     pAlAshyaH samidho 'doShA nityaM home prakIrtitAH | atha vA kaushikoktAnAM yaj~niyAnAM mahIruhAm ||
(AVParis_23,9.5)     aN^gulatrayam Avartya ucchraye 'py aN^gulatrayam | puroDAshapramANaM tu sarvatra kathitaM nR^iNAm ||

(AVParis_23,10.1)     ShoDashAN^gulam Avartya tribhAgaM cottaram R^iju | dakShiNasyAM dishi sthAnaM dakShiNAgneH prakIrtitam ||
(AVParis_23,10.2)     aShTAviMshaty aN^gulAni gArhapatyaM prakIrtitam | AhavanIyam [catur]viMshatish caturashraM tu kArayet ||
(AVParis_23,10.3)     aN^gulAni tu ShaTtriMshad dhnvAkR^ityA tu kArayet | dakShiNAgnes tu vai kuNDaM vidvadbhij parikathyate ||
(AVParis_23,10.4)     IshAnyAM dishi sabhyasya gArhapatyavidhAnataH | sabhyaM necchanti shAlAgnau mAhakiH kaushikas tathA ||
(AVParis_23,10.5)     maudAyanAs tathecchanti shaunakeyAs tathaiva ca | mantAd eva tathA proktaM dravyaM yatra na dR^ishyate ||
(AVParis_23,10.6)     AjyaM tatra vijAnIiyAd dhomas tatra sruveNa ca | abhyukShaNaM haviHkarma kartavyaM vajrapANinA ||
(AVParis_23,10.7)     kushahastena kartavyA japahomapitR^ikriyAH | yaj~ne caiva aN^gabhUtAsh ca pAtramantrahavirdvijAH | carutbhish ca kriyAH sarvAsh cAturhotraM tad ucyate ||

(AVParis_23,11.1)     yAj~nikAs tu vadanty anye caturbhir yac ca hUyate | brahmaNAdhvaryuhotR^ibhyAM tribhir agnicaturthakaiH ||
(AVParis_23,11.2)     durbhikShe cAkule bhaN^ge R^itvijAM cApy asaMbhave | ekash cAturhotraM kuryAd Apastambe prapaThyate ||
(AVParis_23,11.3)     R^itvijAM ca7apy asAmnidhye adhvaryus tat paThet svayam | asthAnapaThite kuryur R^itvig ityAdi coditam ||
(AVParis_23,11.4)     khAte lUne tu yac coktaM saMskArashrutihetubhiH | dravyANAM yaj~nakLptyarthaM kuryAt pUrveNa saMgraham ||
(AVParis_23,11.5)     pAtrAsAdaM dvitIyaM ca prokShaNena vivarjitam | ubhayosh caiva kurvIta pAkayaj~neShTikarmavat ||

(AVParis_23,12.1)     kR^iShNAjinaM tilA darbhA mantrA AjyaM dvijottamAH | doSho na vidyate hy eShAM yathArthaM saMniyojayet ||
(AVParis_23,12.2)     AjyaM dhUmahavir jvAlA paripAkaH sphuliN^gakaiH | dAvAgnikAShThasaMsparshe agner doSho na vidyate ||
(AVParis_23,12.3)     japAdhyAyatapodAnaiH sopavAsaiH sahomakaiH | shrAddhAdipitR^ikAryais ca na doShaH parivedane ||
(AVParis_23,12.4)     pitR^ibhrAtR^isapatnaish ca patitonmattaShaNDhakaiH | jAtyandhamUkabadhirair na doShaH parivedane ||
(AVParis_23,12.5)     atyantakAminA caiva patnIhInena caiva hi | eShAm anuj~nAm AdAya kuryAd vaitAnikI[H] kriyAH ||

(AVParis_23,13.1)     raudrarAkShasapaishAcAn AsurAMsh cAbhicArikAn | mantAMsh ca pitR^ikarmaivaM kR^itvAlabhyodakaM spR^ishet ||
(AVParis_23,13.2)     sruk sruvash ca dhruvA khaDgaM musalolUkhalaM caruH | udakenaiva soShNena saMprakShAlya vishudhyati ||
(AVParis_23,13.3)     pAtraM grahAsh ca camasA haviH shUrpaM kushAsanam | somaspR^iShTaM ca yad bhANDaM vArishaucena shudhyati ||
(AVParis_23,13.4)     vedoktaM sarvamantoktaM shaunakena mahAtmanA | avashyaM tad dvijaiH kAryaM shreyaskAmais tu nityashaH ||
(AVParis_23,13.5)     pAtrAnAM tu prasAN^gena yad anyat parikIrtitam | sAyaM prAtas tu homAN^gaM purA dR^iShTaM maharShibhiH ||

(AVParis_23,14.1)     guruNA bhAShitenaiva yAj~nikAnumatena ca | sadApadiShTadravyANAM lakShaNaM parikIrtitam ||
(AVParis_23,14.2)     nityaM ye 'nusmariShyanti yaj~napAtreShu lakShaNam | rAjasUyAshvamedhAbhyAM phalaM prApsyanti te dhruvam ||
(AVParis_23,14.3)     pippalAdena mahatA samAkhyAtam idaM shubham | brAhmaNAnAM hitArthAya putrashiShyahitAya ca ||
(AVParis_23,14.4)     niShkAmo vA sakAmo vA vedoktaM yaH samAcaret | niShkAmasya tu muktiH syAt sakAmaH phalam ashnute ||
(AVParis_23,14.5)     niShkAmeNa tu yat kiM cit kartavyam iti vaidikam | tat sarvaM muktidaM j~neyaM parAparaparaM sukham ||
(AVParis_23,14.6)     na shokas tasya no vyAdhir na mR^ityur na jarA tathA | na kShudhA na pipAsA ca amR^itAtmA sa tiShThati ||
