(ParishiShTa_24. vedilakShaNam [+ agnivarNalakShaNam])

(AVParis_24,1.1)     om atha rShiputrikAyAM tu sphutaM sarveShu karmasu | lakShaNaM hy agnivarNAnAM pravakShyAmi yathAkramam ||
(AVParis_24,1.2)     vAstukarmaNy athotpAte pater nIrAjane vidhau | sarvanakShatrahomeShu grahAtithyavidhau tathA ||
(AVParis_24,1.3)     yAtrodyAne vivAheShu cUDopanayaneShu ca | sarveShu cAgnihomeShu vahnivarNAn nibodhata ||
(AVParis_24,1.4)     mAnenAdhyardhashIrsaNyA trimadhyA ShaNmukhA smR^itA | caturashrA cakartavyA vediH shAntIShTikarmasu ||
(AVParis_24,1.5)     eShA vai viparItA ca kAryA ghoreShu karmasu | karmaNAm anurUpAM tu vediM vakShyAmy ataH param ||
(AVParis_24,1.6)     yathAvartanagocarmacakratalpeShu saMmitA | saMmR^ijya prokShya saMstIrya vidhivac copashobhayet ||
(AVParis_24,1.7)     shlakShNAH samAhitAH sarvAH prAgudakpravaNAH shubhAH | saMmR^ijya prokShya saMstIrya vidhivac copashobhayet ||
(AVParis_24,1.8)     dakShiNena tu yA vakrA yAj~nikaM sA vinAshayet | yA ca vakrottareNa syAd yajamAnaM vinAshayet ||
(AVParis_24,1.9)     purastAt pR^iShThato vApi madhyato viShamA ca yA | puram antaHpuraM cApi nAyakaM ca hinasti sA ||
(AVParis_24,1.10)     eShA saMkShepataH proktA vediH sAmAnyalakShaNA | visheShatas tu teShv eva karmasv evAbhidhAsyate ||

(AVParis_24,2.1)     prAcIM saMshodhayed bhUmiM yaj~navAstu yathoditam | samitkushAgnivarNAnAM lakShaNaj~no bhaved guruH ||
(AVParis_24,2.2)     tatas tu yatnavAn samyag agnAv upasamAhite | agnivarNAn parIkSheta yathovAcoshanAH kaviH ||
(AVParis_24,2.3)     shabdaM varNaM ca gandhaM ca rUpaM snehaM prabhAM gatim | sparshaM cApi parIkSheta agnAv iti vinishcayaH ||
(AVParis_24,2.4)     svAhAkArAvasAne tu svayam utthAya pAvakaH | havir yAtrAbhilaShati tad vidyAd arthasiddhaye ||
(AVParis_24,2.5)     vR^iShavAraNameghaughanemidundubhiniHsvanaH | mR^iNAlapadmadUrvAbhakumudotpalagandhamuk ||

(AVParis_24,3.1)     tathA mahAtmA stanayan vAhakumbhanibhadyutiH | saMhitajvAlanikaraH pAvakaH pApanAshanaH ||
(AVParis_24,3.2)     kuraNTAkR^itigokShIrahemAruNataDitprabhaH | protphullotpalakundendukumudAbhotpaladyutiH ||
(AVParis_24,3.3)     huto 'pi saMjvalaty eva snigdho viprasya dakShiNaH | lelihAnaH pramuditaH kR^iShNavarNo 'rthasidhaye ||
(AVParis_24,3.4)     vishAlamUlo hy amalo nIlaH pR^ithulamadhyamaH | pradIptAgro 'malatato jvAlAmAlAkulo 'nalaH ||
(AVParis_24,3.5)     pradakShiNaH prasannArcir arciShmAn arcitadyutiH | arcanIyash ca nR^ipater arcito havyavAhanaH ||

(AVParis_24,4.1)     paristaraNayogAc ca yaj~nakANDaparicchadam | shAntiveshmArdhvadIptArcir R^itvijash cAnulimpati ||
(AVParis_24,4.2)     prahasann iva shabdena dyotayann iva tejasA | kR^itapuNyasya nR^ipater hUyamAno hutAshanaH ||
(AVParis_24,4.3)     karmaNo 'vabhR^ithe yasya haviSho 'nte ca pArthivam | sugandhAbhir adhUmAbhiH shikhAbhiH saMspR^ishann iva ||
(AVParis_24,4.4)     arcibhir jvAlabhAraish ca pradahan dviShatAM dishaH | vidhUmaH kuNDalI yaH syAd anulomash ca siddhaye ||

(AVParis_24,5.1)     kuraNTahemAruNashaN^khakundamuktAvalIndupratime hutAshe | samasvane siMhavR^iShair gajendrabalAhakaughasvanadundubhInAm ||
(AVParis_24,5.2)     vishAlamUle pR^ithule ca madhye j~neyAnale saMprati pIDitAgre | mR^iNAlapadmAnilatulyagandhe trisAgarAntA vasudhA nR^ipasya ||
(AVParis_24,5.3)     AtaptapadmAnilatulyagandhe trisAgarAntA vasudhA nR^ipasya | tasyArthabAndhavavatI sakalA mahIyaM vIryAMshujAlavivarAhatarAjashabdA ||
(AVParis_24,5.4)     vibhrAjate tv akhilarAgayuto hutAsho hastAvR^itaM kathayatIva jayaM nR^ipasya | sUryAMshubhiH kR^itavighaTTanahemapadmakiMjalkacUrNanikarAruNatAmalAMshuH ||
(AVParis_24,5.5)     kShIrodashuktipuTagarbhavikIrNamuktAsaMghAtapANDurarajo rathanemighoShaH | dAtA nR^ipAya vasudhAM tu himAMshumaulijyotsnAvikAshitasamudrajalAM hutAshaH ||

(AVParis_24,6.1)     lakShmIpradoharamR^iNAlakapAlashubhrasnigdhAnuvR^ittashikharaprakR^itish ca yatra | vaishvAnaro jvalati yasya vishuddhamUrtiH sa prApnuyAn nR^ipashatAdhipatAM narendraH ||
(AVParis_24,6.2)     bAlArkabodhitasaroruhagarbhagandhas toyAvalambijaladastanitAbhirAmaH | rAj~no dadAti vasudhAM hutabhug gajendradantAgrakampitamahArNavavIcivR^ikShAm ||
(AVParis_24,6.3)     yasyAM vasantaravimaNDalatulyabimbo vedyAM nR^ipasya paripUrNamarIcijAlaH | tasyAnalAkalitasAgaratoyavastrA mrAgaikShavenir avanir vasham abhyupaiti ||
(AVParis_24,6.4)     yasyAnalo jvalati kAJNcanatulyagauro prajvAlyamAnavapur utpalakoshagandhaH | AyAti tasya bhavanaM hy alidIptimAlA savrIDasUryakiraNA kShitipAlalakShmIr iti ||

(ParishiShTa_25. kuNDalakShaNam)

(AVParis_25,1.1)     oM shaunakaM tu sukhAsInaM bhArgavaH paripR^icchati | kuNDaM kasmin bhavet kIdR^ik kasyAM vA dishi kiM phalam ||
(AVParis_25,1.2)     sa tasmA upasannAya AcaShTe bhArgavAya tu | kuNDaM yasmin bhaved yAdR^ig yasyAM vA dishi yat phalam ||
(AVParis_25,1.3)     caturashraM shaphAkR^ityA ardhacandraM trikoNakam | vartulaM paJNcakoNaM ca padmAbhaM saptakoNakam ||
(AVParis_25,1.4)     kuNDAny etAni pUrvAdidikShu aShTasu vinirdishet | digdevatAnAM cAShTAnAM karmaNi svamsvam Adishet ||
(AVParis_25,1.5)     caturashraM tu pUrvasyAm aindreShv api ca karmasu | shaphAkR^iti tadAgneyyAm AgneyeShv api karmasu ||
(AVParis_25,1.6)     ardhacandraM tu yAmyAyAM yAmyeShv api ca karmasu | nairR^ityAM ca trikoNaM syAd abhicAravidhau shubham ||
(AVParis_25,1.7)     vAruNyAM vartulaM j~neyaM vAruNyeShv api karmasu | vAyavyAM paJNcakoNaM tu vAyavyeShv api karman ||
(AVParis_25,1.8)     uttarasyAM tu padmAbhaM saumyeShv api ca karmasu | aishAnyAM saptakoNaM tu raudreShv api yathoditam ||
(AVParis_25,1.9)     sarvakarmasu vij~neyaM kuNDaM padmanibhaM tu yat | caturashraM tu sarvatra samaM syAd vijayAvaham ||
(AVParis_25,1.10)     sarvashAntikaraM kuNDaM padmAkAraM visheShataH | shAntike caturashraM ca pauShTike vartulaM tathA ||
(AVParis_25,1.11)     abhicAre trikoNaM ca vashyAdau cArdhacandrakam | ShaTkoNaM mAraNAdau ca vidveShe cAShTakoNakam ||
(AVParis_25,1.12)     mekhalA sarvakuNDeShu dvAdashAN^gulam iShyate | caturaN^gulamAnena pUrvApUrvasamucchritA ||

(AVParis_25,2.1)     na cet purastAd dhInaM syAt sukhaM yaj~naH samApyate | yat tu dakShiNato 'hInaM tad rAj~nas tv abhayapradam ||
(AVParis_25,2.2)     yathAhInaM pashcimena bhavet tat siddhidaM shubham | uttareNa samamyat syAt tad rAj~no rAjyavardhanam ||
(AVParis_25,2.3)     madhye samaM ca sukhadaM digvidikShu samaM tu yat | tad rAjajanasaMpatkR^it sarvAMsh cArIn vinAshayet ||
(AVParis_25,2.4)     na cet purastAd ityAdi ya eSha kathito vidhiH | maNDapAnAM gR^ihANAM ca mAne shAntikaraH smR^itaH ||
(AVParis_25,2.5)     hastakuNDaM sadAhome ayute dvikaraM smR^itam | lakShahome catuShpANi koTyAm aShTakaraM smR^itam ||

______________________________________________________________________


(ParishiShTa_26. samillakShaNam)

(AVParis_26,1.1)     oM samidhAM saMpravakShyAmi pramANaM lakShaNaM shubham | tathAshubhaM ca tattvena yathAphalavibhAgataH ||
(AVParis_26,1.2)     yaj~nakarmaNi kartavyA[H] shAntike pauShTike tathA | prAdeshamAtrIH samidhaH proktAH sarveShu karmasu ||
(AVParis_26,1.3)     tiryag yavodarANy aShTAv UrdhvA vA vrIhayas trayaH | aN^gulasya pramANena prAdesho dvAdashAN^gulaH ||
(AVParis_26,1.4)     ata UrdhvaM na kartavyA nApi hrasvA na cordhvataH | na vakrA caiva kartavyA nApi granthisamanvitA ||
(AVParis_26,1.5)     Urdhvatas tu yato vakrA citradadruvicarcikAH | karoti yAge kShipraM tu tasmAt tAM parivarjayet ||

(AVParis_26,2.1)     dviphalA piNDavarjApi triphalA vApi yA bhavet | ShaTphalA saptaphalA yA caturaN^gaM vinashyati ||
(AVParis_26,2.2)     sapattrapuShpasamidhaH kalpayitvA vicakShaNaH | pauShTikaM karma kurvIta sidhyate nAtra saMshayaH ||
(AVParis_26,2.3)     pattrapuShpayutA yAs tu shAntadrumasamudbhavAH | samidho goShThamadhye tu prashastAH parikIrtitAH ||
(AVParis_26,2.4)     [athAparaM pravakShyAmi samidhAM caiva lakShaNam] ||
(AVParis_26,2.5)     vishIrNA dvidalA hrasvA vakrA caiva dvidhAgrataH | kR^ishA ca dIrghA sthUlA ca karmasiddhivinAshinI ||
(AVParis_26,2.6)     [yad yatra lakShaNaM proktaM yasmin kAle yathAvidhi | tatra tenaiva siddhiH syAd viparIte tathA bhayam] ||
(AVParis_26,2.7)     samAhR^itAnAM samidhAM tAsAM caiva phalaM shR^iNu ||
(AVParis_26,2.8)     vishIrNAyuHkShayaM kuryAd dvidalA rogadA bhavet | abhimukhagatamAtrA sadyo hrasvA nivartayet ||

(AVParis_26,3.1)     durbhagaM kurute vakrA sthAnabhraMshaM dvidhAgrataH | kR^ishA sarvavinAshAya dIrghA nAshayate shriyam ||
(AVParis_26,3.2)     sthUlA tu kurute vighnaM sarvakArye dvijasya tu | ataH pramANaM vividhaM phalaM cApi tathA shR^iNu ||
(AVParis_26,3.3)     latApallavasaMjAtA dvAdashAN^gulakalpitA | kShIrAktA shAntike home hotavyA tu visheShataH ||
(AVParis_26,3.4)     kevalaM muktisiddhyarthaM ghR^itAktA[m] homayeddvijaH | dashAN^gulapramANAM hi homayen mantrakarmaNi ||
(AVParis_26,3.5)     navAN^gulA tu kartavyA tailAbhyaktAbhicArike | aShTAN^gulA vibhUtyarthe ghR^itadadhnA tu homayet ||

(AVParis_26,4.1)     kevalaM madhusaMyuktA saptAN^guladalIkR^itA | uccATane prashastA sA dvidalA ca na shAntaye ||
(AVParis_26,4.2)     vidveShe kaTutailAktA dvidalA tu ShaDaN^gulA | sarvato granthihInA tu viprANAM syAt samic chubhA ||
(AVParis_26,4.3)     avakrAgranthisaMyuktA kShatriyANAM jayAvahA | madhye tu granthisaMyuktA vaishyAnAM bhUtisAdhanI ||
(AVParis_26,4.4)     trayANAm api vakShyante yA grAhyAH samidhaH smR^itaH | nAtyArdrA nAtishuShkA vA naiva coSharasaMbhavAH ||
(AVParis_26,4.5)     na dagdhA na kR^imidaShTAH sarvadoShavivarjitAH | samidhAm indhanAnAM ca tulyAn vR^ikShAn bravImy ataH ||
(AVParis_26,4.6)     shuShukair yA indhanaiH pUrvaM yaj~navR^ikShamayaiH shubhaiH | ArdrANi homayec caiva shuShkaiH kalahakarmaNi | shuShkANi hIndhanAni syuH samidhas tu yathoditAH ||

(AVParis_26,5.1)     puShTikAmaH palAshasya gR^ihNIyAc chAntikarmaNi udumbarasya vittArthI vaTAshvatthasya rAjyadhIH ||
(AVParis_26,5.2)     shrIkAmo bilvavR^ikShasya kadambasya tathaiva ca | vidveShaM kaTukaiH kuryAt kaNTakair maraNaM bhavet ||
(AVParis_26,5.3)     kakubhaM kaTabhaM vR^ikShaM kauvirAlaM tu kauhakam | vaMshaM vibhItakaM shigruM vidyAd uccATane hitAn ||
(AVParis_26,5.4)     stambhane sarvasainyAnAM vijayArthe jayaM dishet | apAmArgeNa saubhAgyam AyuShkAmo hi dUrvayA ||
(AVParis_26,5.5)     punnAgacampakau vR^ikShA ye cAnye kShIriNaH shubhAH | yad yatra lakShaNaM proktaM yasmin kAle yathAvidhi ||
(AVParis_26,5.6)     tatra tenaiva siddhiH syAd viparIte tathA bhayam | arkaH palAsho madhuko nyagrodhodumbaras tathA ||
(AVParis_26,5.7)     plakSho 'shvattho gomayAnikushAsh ca samidhaH kramAt | yathAkrameNa samidha AdityAdigraheShu ca ||
(AVParis_26,5.8)     shataM sahasraM lakShaM vA gAyatryA paramAhutiH | hUyamAnaM tu yat kiM cit kR^itAnnaM yadi vA tilAH ||
(AVParis_26,5.9)     grahanakShatrapIDAyAM sAvitryApi hutaM hutam | eShabhedo mayAkhyAtaH shubhasya tv ashubhasya ca ||
(AVParis_26,5.10)     yathoktam etad yaH kuryAt sa sarvaphalam ApnuyAd iti ||

(ParishiShTa_27. sruvalakShaNam)

(AVParis_27,1.1)     oM sauvarNarAjatais tAmraiH kAMsyair draumais tathAyasaiH | sruvaiH sarvaguNopetaiH karma kuryAd yathAkramam ||
(AVParis_27,1.2)     sauvarNai rAjatair yaj~ne tAmraiH shAntikapauShTike | kAMsyena rudhiraM mAMsaM nAnyaj juhuvIta kiM cana ||
(AVParis_27,1.3)     sarve yaj~ne prayoktavyA varjayitvAyasaM sruvam | AyasaM khAdiraM caiva abhicAre prayojayet ||
(AVParis_27,1.4)     adhunvaMsh caiva juhuyAt sruveNAsphuTitAhutim | dhunvan hi hanti putrAn tu rAkShasA sphuTitAhutiH ||
(AVParis_27,1.5)     nAnyat kiM cid abhidhyAyed uddhR^ityAnyata Ahutim | tad daivatam abhidhyAyed Ahutir yasya hUyate ||

(AVParis_27,2.1)     sruve pUrNe japen mantram uttAnaM shAntike karam | shAntike pauShTike caiva varjayet tu kanInikAm ||
(AVParis_27,2.2)     nAtidIrgho nAtihrasvo nAtisthUlaH kR^ishas tathA | aShTAviMshatyaN^gulaH syAt kaniShThAgrapramANataH ||
(AVParis_27,2.3)     dIrgho hinasti rAjAnaM hrasva rtvijaM vinAshayet | sthUlaH sasyopaghAtAya kR^ishaH kShayakaraH smR^itaH ||
(AVParis_27,2.4)     gopucchAgrAkR^itir daNDo maNDalAgra[m] shiro viduH | aN^guShThAgrapramANena nimnaM shirasi khAnayet ||
(AVParis_27,2.5)     etal lakShaNam uddiShTaM sruvasya phalabhedataH | gopathena yathAshAstram uddhR^itaM shruticodanAt | sruveNa kurute karma hastenApi tathA shR^iNu ||

(ParishiShTa_28. hastalakShaNam)

(AVParis_28,1.1)     oM yadA juhoti hastena dakShiNenetareNa vA | tadA vakShye vidhiM tasya shreyasI syAd yathAhutiH ||
(AVParis_28,1.2)     yathA nashyati caivAsya karma guhyam ajAnataH | tathAhaM saMpravakShyAmi gopathaH pATham icchatAm ||
(AVParis_28,1.3)     kushabalbajamauJNjAM vA kR^itvA veShTim anAmikAm | homakarma tataH kuryAt spR^iShTvA vAmena dakShiNam ||
(AVParis_28,1.4)     na riktapANir juhuyAn nAnipAtitajAnukaH | anipAtitajAnosh ca haranty AhutI rAkShasAH ||
(AVParis_28,1.5)     uddhR^itya samidho 'nnaM vA paJNcabhir juhuyAd budhaH | shanaish ca nirvaped annaM madhye 'gnau susamAhitaH ||

(AVParis_28,2.1)     gR^ihakarmaNi yaj~ne vA tathA paJNcabhir eva tu | shAntike pauShTike vaiva varjayet tu kanInikAm ||
(AVParis_28,2.2)     tisR^ibhir juhuyAd annaM na tilAn naiva taNDulAn | yadAbhicArikaM kiM cit tasmin kAle prayojayet ||
(AVParis_28,2.3)     vAmenAbhicAran nityaM tribhir aN^gulibhiH samaiH | nirdiShTaM tisR^ibhiH shUlaM tena shatruM nipAtayet ||
(AVParis_28,2.4)     apasavyena hastena savyaM yadi juhoti tat | savyena cApasavyaM tu [savyaM yadi juhoti tat] ||
(AVParis_28,2.5)     abhicAras tu tat proktaH....SharvashAntiM gamiShyati ||

(ParishiShTa_29. jvAlAlakShaNam)

(AVParis_29,1.1)     oM bR^ihaspatiM sukhAsInam AtmavidyAparAyaNam | praNipatya mahartvijaM nAradaH paripR^icchati ||
(AVParis_29,1.2)     kathayasva mahAprAj~na sarvashAstravishArada | ashubhaM yac chubhaM vApi lakShaNaM pAvakasya tu ||
(AVParis_29,1.3)     sa pR^iShTas tena tat sarvam AcacakShe mahAmatiH ||
(AVParis_29,1.4)     hUyamAnoyadA vahnir R^ijujvAlaH pradR^ishyate | snigdhash ca kiMshukAbhash ca siddhis tatra vinirdishet ||
(AVParis_29,1.5)     yatra bAlArkavarNAbhaH karmaNy agniH pradR^ishyate | shAntiM labhete tatrAshu yajamAnapurohitau ||
(AVParis_29,1.6)     ashokakusumAbho 'pi kAJNcanAbhas tathaiva ca | shAntiM karoty AkAlena hUyamAno hutAshanaH ||

(AVParis_29,2.1)     adhUmo jvalate kShipraM kR^itvAvartaM pradakShiNam | tadA shAntiM vijAnIyAd viparIte tathA bhayam ||
(AVParis_29,2.2)     shvaste garjate caiva visphuliN^gAH samantataH | prAyashcittiM tadAkuryAd yad uktaM kaushikena tu ||
(AVParis_29,2.3)     athApi AliN^gate bhUmiM bhramate ca samantataH | ashubhaM kathayet tatra hotre 'sau pAvakaH svayam ||
(AVParis_29,2.4)     kapilaH piN^galas tAmro raktaH kAJNcanasaprabhaH | shubhakR^it pAvako j~neyo viparIto bhayAvahaH ||
(AVParis_29,2.5)     yadAgnau lakShaNaM kiM cid ashubhaM tu pradR^ishyate | hotA klesham avApnoti shAntiM tatra prayojayet ||

(ParishiShTa_30. laghulakShahomaH)

(AVParis_30,1.1)     oM shaunakaM tu sukhAsInaM gautamaH paripR^icchati | lakShahomasya yat puNyam AhutInAM ca devatAH ||
(AVParis_30,1.2)     tasmai yathAvad AcaShTe shaunako j~nAnalocanaH | shR^iNuShvAvahito bhUtvA lakShahomaM yathAvidhi ||
(AVParis_30,1.3)     agnyAgArasya yA bhUmis tAM pravakShyAmy asheShataH | shuddhAkShArA samA snigdhA yA ca pUrvottaraplavA ||
(AVParis_30,1.4)     abhasmAsthyaN^gAratUShA prashastA parikIrtitA | pramANaM bAhumAtraM tu jaN^ghAmAtraM dviratnikam ||
(AVParis_30,1.5)     caturashraM catuShkoNaM tulyaM sUtreNa dhArayet | brAhmANA vedasaMpannA brahmakarmasamAdhayaH ||
(AVParis_30,1.6)     upoShya caikarAtraM ca gAyatryA ayutaM japet | upoShya caiva gAyatryA japeyur ayutaM budhAH ||

(AVParis_30,2.1)     te shuklavAsasaH snAtAH sragbhir gandhair alaMkR^itAH | nirAhArAs tathA dAntAH saMtuShTAH sajitendriyAH ||
(AVParis_30,2.2)     kausham Asanam AsInAH prayuJNjyur homam uttamam | ullikhya cAdbhir abhyukShya saMskR^itya vidhipUrvakam ||
(AVParis_30,2.3)     agne praihy agninA rayim ity upasthApya pAvakam | kuryAd upasamAdhAya samAs tvAgne samAhitaH ||

(AVParis_30,3.1)     lakShahoma kute pUrNe dhenuM dadyAt payasvinIm | anaDvAn kAJNcanaM vastraM tuShyeyur yena vA dvijAH ||
(AVParis_30,3.2)     yavais tu vipulAn bhogAn dhAnyair AyuShyam eva ca | tilair hutvA tu tejasvI AyuH kIrtiM ca vardhate ||
(AVParis_30,3.3)     Adityaloko 'rkamayI pAlAshI soma Apyate | AshvatthI viShNulokasya brAhma audumbarI tathA ||
(AVParis_30,3.4)     anenaiva vidhAnena hUyate 'tra hutAshanaH | hutvaitAMsh caturo lakShAn brahmalokaM sa gacchati ||
(AVParis_30,3.5)     yAvaj jIvati kartAsau tAvat putrAn dhanaM shriyam | pUrNe kAle vimAnena nIyate paramaM padam ||

______________________________________________________________________


(ParishiShTa_30b. bR^ihallakShahomaH)

(AVParis_30b,1.1)     om atha kAN^kAyano bhagavantam atharvANaM papraccha || bhagavan kena vidhAnena koTihomaM lakShahomam ayutahomaM vA prArambhamANaH katham R^itvijo vR^iNIte kathaM ca kuryus tasmai sa hovAca ||
(AVParis_30b,1.2)     brAhmaNo vA rAjA vA vaishyo vA grAmo vA janapado vA shrIkAmaH shAntikAmaH koTihomaM lakShahomam ayutahomaM vAhaM kariShyAmIti tasyA samApter bhavadbhir amAMsAshibhir brahmacAribhir haviShyabhugbhir bhavitavyam
(AVParis_30b,1.3)     tais tatheti uktaH kuNDam ekahastaM dvihastaM caturhastam aShTahastaM vA [samastahastaM vA dIrghaM vA] dashahastaM khAnayet tathA ca bAdariH ||
(AVParis_30b,1.4)     lakShahome tu kartavyam aShTahastaM na saMshayaH | dvihastaM vA prakurvIta caturhastam athApi vA ||
(AVParis_30b,1.5)     kuNDaM vA dashahastaM tu dvivistAraM tathottaram | na cet purastAd dhInaM syAt sukhaM yaj~naH samApyate ||
(AVParis_30b,1.6)     atha dakShiNato hInaM yajamAnabhayaMkaram | pashcimena vihInaM syAd yaj~nasyAsiddhidaM dhruvam ||
(AVParis_30b,1.7)     uttareNa vinirdiShTaM rAj~no rAjyaharaM bhR^isham | madhye vihInaM yad kuNDaM prajAkShayakaraM viduH ||
(AVParis_30b,1.8)     sraktihInaM tu yat kuNDaM tad apy ashubhadaM bhavet | dvAdashAN^gulamAnena mekhalAkShetram ucyate ||
(AVParis_30b,1.9)     mekhalAtrayam uddhiShTam ubhayaM caturaN^gulam | caturaN^gulamAnena pUrvApUrvasamucchritA ||
(AVParis_30b,1.10)     prathamA sAttvikI proktA dvitIyA rAjasI smR^itA | tR^itIyA tAmasI j~neyA mekhalA vR^iShabhadhvajaH ||
(AVParis_30b,1.11)     caturdashAN^gulAM tatra yoniM kurvIta sAdhakaH | aShTAN^gulaM bhaved vR^ittaM nirvAhas tu ShaDaN^gulaH ||
(AVParis_30b,1.12)     gajoShThasadR^ishAkAra prAjApatyA ca sA ciduH | evaM kR^itvA vidhAnena kuNDaM lakShaNalakShitam ||
(AVParis_30b,1.13)     sarvalakShaNasaMpUrNaM sarvatas tu samAhitaH | kuNDaM siddhikaraM j~neyam AyuHkIrtivivardhanam ||
(AVParis_30b,1.14)     tasmAd yatnena kuNDaM khAtvAdbhir abhyukShya purastAd agner AdityAdIn grahAn pratiShThApyottarataH kR^ittikAdIni nakShatrANi svAsu dikShu lokapAlAn sarvAsu kuNDasraktiShv agnyAdidevAn ratiShThApya
(AVParis_30b,1.15)     teShAM pratimantram AvAhanAdikaM kR^itvA vilInapUtam AjyaM gR^ihItvA sruvaM srucaM ca saMmR^ijya pratapyedhmam upasamAdhAyAnvArabdhAya vAstoShpatyAdibhish caturbhir gaNaiH shAntyudakaM kR^itvA tataH kartAram AcAmayati ca saMprokShati ca ||
(AVParis_30b,1.16)     atha samidho ghR^itAktAs tilAn vA svAhAkAravatIH saMkhyAvatyo gAyatryA mahAvyAhR^itibhir vA sarva R^itvijo juhvati ||
(AVParis_30b,1.17)     shrIparNamishrAH shrIkAmasya shamIparNamishrAH shAntikAmasya karIrasaktumishrA vR^iShTikAmaysa badarAdiphalamishrAH pashukAmasya ||

(AVParis_30b,2.1)     aharahaH karmaNo 'pavargAd atha pUrNAyAM koTyAM lakShe vAyute vAnvArabdhe yajamAne nishi mahAbhiShEkaM kR^itvA vasor dhAraM juhvati ||
(AVParis_30b,2.2)     audumbarIM srucaM shuraHpramANAM brAhmaNasya lalAtapramANAM kShatriyasya skandhapramANAM vaiShyasyApramANAM janapadasya
(AVParis_30b,2.3)     teShAm ante saraNArthaM nimnaM khAnayitvoShNodakena prakShAlyAjyam AnIya vasor dhArAM vaishvAnaraM prApnoti ||
(AVParis_30b,2.4)     tad yad AjyadhAnIM ca vaishvAnaraM prApnoti athoccArayati ||
(AVParis_30b,2.5)     ojash ca me kShatraM ca me ye agnayo amo devavadhebhyo bhavAsharvau mR^iDataM prANAya nama iti hutvA arghaM pradAya vastraM lodhraM mAlyaM phalAdIni bhAjane kR^itvA namas te astu pashyata iti svAhAkAreNAgnau prakShipya yamyaM kAmaM kAmayate so 'smai kAmaH samR^idhyate ||
(AVParis_30b,2.6)     samR^iddhihomAdi samAnaM svastyayanAni japet puNyAhaM vAcayed gobhUtilasuvarNaM vAsash ca rtvigbhyaH saMpradAya praNipatya visarjayet ||
(AVParis_30b,2.7)     tasminn ahani vyatIte yadi strI mAlyahastA shvetacandanAniliptA shvetapuShpANy AdAya prayacched gaurasarShapAn pANyAdhAre vA gR^ihItvA prAsAdam Arohayet kuJNjaraM vA pramattam ashvaM shvetaM vA parvataM govR^iShaM vA yAnaM yuktaM vAjibhir yady Arohet svapnakAle samastasiddhiM vidyAn manaso yAm abhIShTAm ||
(AVParis_30b,2.8)     tasmAt tAM rAtrIM prayataH svapet || svapnaM dR^iShTvA rtvigbhyo nivedayet || paro 'pehi yo na jIbo 'si vidma te svapna yathA kalAM yathA shapham iti rAjamukham abhimantrya yathAgataM gaccheyus tad api shlokAH ||
(AVParis_30b,2.9)     divyAntarikShabhaumeShu adbhuteShu na saMshayaH | koTihomaM viduH prAj~nA lakShaM vAyutam eva vA ||
(AVParis_30b,2.10)     avij~nAtaM ca yat pApaM sahasA caiva yat kR^itam | tat sarvaM lakShahomasya karaNAd dhi vinashyati ||
(AVParis_30b,2.11)     tasmAt sarveShu kAryeShu shAntikeShu visheShataH | yaH kuryAt prayato nityaM na so 'narthAn samashnute ||

(ParishiShTa_31. koTihomaH)

(AVParis_31,1.1)     oM devAsh ca R^iShayash caiva pIDyamAnA mahAsUraiH | mR^ityunA vyAdhibhish caiva brahmANam idam abruvan ||
(AVParis_31,1.2)     karmaNA kena devesha mR^ityur vyAdhish ca jIyate | aishvaryaM prApyate vApi sthAnaM ca paramaM prabho ||
(AVParis_31,1.3)     evam ukto mahAtejA brahmA lokapitAmahaH | pratyuvAceshvaraH sarvAn viprAn devagaNaiH saha ||
(AVParis_31,1.4)     shR^iNudhvaM prayatAH sarve prApyate yena karmaNA | aishvaryam Ayur ArogyaM putrA vijaya eva ca ||
(AVParis_31,1.5)     savyAhR^itiM sapraNavAM gAyatrIM shirasA saha | ye japanti sadA tebhyo na bhayaM vidyate kva cit ||

(AVParis_31,2.1)     tayA homash ca kartavyaH satataM siddhim icchatA | yavais tilaiH samidbhish ca vrIhibhiH sarShapais tathA ||
(AVParis_31,2.2)     atha cen mahatIM siddhiM prArthayedhvaM surottamAH | purodhasA kArayadhvaM koTihomaM mahAphalam ||
(AVParis_31,2.3)     yAdR^ishaM kR^itavAn pUrvam atharvA tryambakasya tu | tAdR^ishena vidhAnena koTihomaH prayujyate ||
(AVParis_31,2.4)     mahattvaM prArthayamAnaH sharvo 'tharvANam abravIt | kuruShva mama tat karma mahattvaM yena labhyate ||
(AVParis_31,2.5)     aishvaryam Ayur ArogyaM sthAnaM ca paramaM prabho | putrA lakShmIr yasho medhA balaM pauruShyam eva ca ||

(AVParis_31,3.1)     evam ukto mahAtejA atharvA mantradarshavit | gAyatrIM tapasA yuktAm R^icaH padam itIti ha ||
(AVParis_31,3.2)     [R^icaH padaM mAtrayeti mantre vij~nAyate hi sA |] gAyatrI vai tripAd brahma vishvarUpA ca saMsthitA ||
(AVParis_31,3.3)     prANadA sarvabhUtAnAM dhAraNI yApi nityashaH | iti nishcitya manasA koTihomaM prayojayat ||
(AVParis_31,3.4)     samidbhiH shAntavR^ikShasya gAyatryA susamAhitaH | tato mahattvam agamad aisharyaM paramaM tathA ||
(AVParis_31,3.5)     mahAdeva iti cAsya nAma lokeShu vishrutam | upadravAsh ca ye ke cid upaghAtAs tathaiva ca | sarve 'sya prashamaM yAtAH skandaM putraM ca labdhavAn ||

(AVParis_31,4.1)     tataH prItas tu bhagavA¤ shaMkaraH paryapR^icchata | atharvANaM mahAprAj~naM koTihomasya ko vidhiH ||
(AVParis_31,4.2)     caturviMshAkSharaM brahma tripAdaM lokadhAraNam | sAvitraM tena homo 'yaM kR^ito me koTisaMmitaH ||
(AVParis_31,4.3)     vidhiM cAsya pravakShyAmi sarvalokahitAya vai | yatprayogAd bhavec chAntir vR^iddhish ca paramA nR^iNAm ||
(AVParis_31,4.4)     upadraveShu bhUtAnAm Apatsu vividhAsu ca | koTihomaH prayoktavyaH ketUnAM darshane tathA ||
(AVParis_31,4.5)     upasargabhaye caiva paracakrabhaye tathA | anAvR^iShTibhaye caiva koTihomaM prayojayet ||

(AVParis_31,5.1)     ArambhaM tasya kurvIta shukle cApi tithau shubhe | muhUrte vijaye caiva tithichidrANi varjayet ||
(AVParis_31,5.2)     rohiNyAM vaiShNave tvAShTre pauShNe maitrottareShu ca | abhijitpuShyasaumyeShu kuryAt puNyeShu vA budhaH ||
(AVParis_31,5.3)     atha cet tvarate kartuM koTihomaM mahAphalam | puNyAhaM vAcayitvAsya ArambhaM kArayed budhaH ||
(AVParis_31,5.4)     aShTahastaM tu nirdiShTaM koTihomasya khAtakam | tasyaivArdhapramANena lakShahome vidhIyate ||
(AVParis_31,5.5)     trirAtropoShito brahmA kR^itvA shAntiM caturgaNIm | prokShayet karmasiddhyarthaM vAstu shAntyudakena tu ||
(AVParis_31,5.6)     mahAshAntividhAnena nirmathyAgniM samAhitaH | tAvat kuryAd budhaH sarvaM yAvan no nairR^itaM kR^itam ||

(AVParis_31,6.1)     tataH prabhAte bahusha uddhR^ityAgniM samAhitaH | nirmathya hAvayet tatra samidho brAhmaNAn bahUn ||
(AVParis_31,6.2)     shataM sahasraM koTiM vA viMshatir dasha vA dvijAH | juhuyuH shAntavR^ikShasya samidho ghR^itasaMyutAH ||
(AVParis_31,6.3)     svayaM vApi yajed brahmA savitAraM dinedine | pAkayaj~navidhAnena mantrash cAtra viShAsahim ||
(AVParis_31,6.4)     shAntikAmo yavaiH kuryAt tilaiH pApApanuttaye | samidbhiH sarvakAmas tu bilvaiH prApnoti kAJNcanam ||
(AVParis_31,6.5)     labhate shriyam agryAM tu padmais tejo ghR^itena tu | dadhnA tu labhate putrAn payasA brahmavarcasam ||

(AVParis_31,7.1)     haviShyabhojino dAntAH shuklAmbaradharAs tathA | hAvakA niyatAH sarve bhaveyur brahmacAriNaH ||
(AVParis_31,7.2)     AraNyam upayuJNjAnaH payasA vApi vartayet | phalAhAro 'pi vA brahmA koTihomaM samAcaret ||
(AVParis_31,7.3)     pratyekaM caiva hotÌNAM dAtavyA dakShiNA tataH | niShko ashvo gaur vAsash ca hiraNyaM vApi shaktitaH ||
(AVParis_31,7.4)     yash caivApi bhaved brahmA prayoktA sarvakarmaNAm | sarvasvaM tasya deyaM syAd dhiraNyaM vApi tatsamam ||
(AVParis_31,7.5)     koTihome samApte tu yajed grahagaNAn budhaH | kArayed amR^itAM caiva ghR^itakambalam eva ca ||

(AVParis_31,8.1)     kAryAmR^itA mR^ityubhaye ghR^itakambalasaMyutA | paracakrAgame tv aindrI ghR^itakambala[m] eva ca ||
(AVParis_31,8.2)     raudrI sarvAdbhutotpattau ghR^itakambalasaMyutA | [salilA salilakShaye ghR^itakambala eva ca ||]
(AVParis_31,8.3)     ghR^itakambalapR^iShThA ca salilA salilakShaye | yenayena tu kAmena koTihomaM prayojayet ||
(AVParis_31,8.4)     AmnAtaM tatra yat karma tad ante kArayed budhaH | eSha eva vidhir dR^iShTo abhicAre vidhIyate ||
(AVParis_31,8.5)     pratilomayAtra homaH sAvitryA tilasarShapaiH | ArambhaM tasya ghoreShu nakShatreShu dineShu ca ||
(AVParis_31,8.6)     kArayet kR^iShNapakShasya tithichidreShu sarvadA | maghAshleShA tathA mUlaM revaty ArdrA ca sarvadA ||

(AVParis_31,9.1)     darbhArthe tu sharAn kuryAd ghR^itArthe tailam ucyate | svAhAkAre tu phaTkAro veNyAdyAH syush caturdasha ||
(AVParis_31,9.2)     cANDAlAgnau citAgnau vA sUtikAgnAv athApi vA | hAvayed ghoravR^ikShANAM samidhas tailasaMyutAH ||
(AVParis_31,9.3)     raktoShNIShI raktavAsAH kR^iShNAmbaradharo 'pi vA | juhuyAd vAmahastena samidho dakShiNAmukhaH ||
(AVParis_31,9.4)     khAdirAgnau madhUcchiShTe kR^itvA pratikR^itiM ripoH | tApayet pratilomAM tu sAvitrIM manasA japet ||
(AVParis_31,9.5)     kaNThe shUlArpitAM kR^itvA tApayet tu dinedine | yAvac chatrur vashaM yAti vilInAyAM vinashyati ||

(AVParis_31,10.1)     evaMproktavidhAnena koTihomasya shaMkaraH | prItimAn ucyate yena tac chubhaM bhautikaM dadau ||
(AVParis_31,10.2)     atharvA bhautikaM labdhvA shiShyebhyas tat punar dadau | shubhaM mokShakaraM puNyaM priyaM pashupater vratam ||
(AVParis_31,10.3)     etaj j~nAtvA tu yaH samyak koTihomaM prayojayet | sarvAn kAmAn avApnoti brahmalokaM sa gacchati ||
(AVParis_31,10.4)     yas tv imaM shrAvayed vidvAn paThate caiva sarvadA | koTihomaphalaM labdhvA rudraloke mahIyate ||
(AVParis_31,10.5)     gopathAt pANineyAya madhye nÌNAM pramodinAm | hitArtham uddhR^ito granthaH koTihomas tu vishrutaH ||

(ParishiShTa_32. gaNamAlA)
(AVParis_32,1)     oM bhUs tat savituH shaM no devIH shAntA dyauH shaM na indrAgnI shaM no vAto vAtu uShA apa svasus tama iti shAntigaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,2)     kR^ityApratiharaNo dUShyA dUShir asi IshAnAM tvA samaM jyotir uto asy abandhukR^id ye purastAt suparNas tvA yAM te cakruH pratIcInaphalo yad duShkR^itam ayaM pratisaro yAM kalpayantIti kR^ityApratiharaNAni || iti kR^ityAgaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,3)     cAtanaH stuvAnam idaM havir ye 'mAvAsyAm upa prAgAn niHsAlAm arAyakShayaNaM shaM no devI pR^ishniparNy A pashyati tAnt satyaujAs tvayA pUrvaM purastAd yukto antardAve juhuta prAgnaye rakShohaNam ity anuvAkash cAtanAni || iti cAtanagaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,4)     mAtR^inAmA divyo gandharva A pashyatImaM me agne yau te mAteti mAtR^inAmAni || iti mAtR^igaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,5)     vAstoShpatIya AshAnAm AshApAlebhya ihaiva dhruvAm R^idhaÇmantro yonim uta putraH pitaram indrasya gR^iho 'sIti catasro dive svAhAshamavarma me pR^ithivyai shrotrAyeti dhanvAnIti dve UrjaM bibhrad iti ShaTsatyaM bR^ihad ity anuvAko vAstoShpatIyAni || iti vAstugaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,6)     pApmahA vi devA jarasAvR^itam apa naH shoshucad agham ava mA pApmann iti pApmahA || iti pApmahA gaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,7)     takmanAshano jarAyujaH prathamo yad agnir ud agAtAM dashavR^ikSha muJNca kShetriyAt tvA hariNasya raghuShyado muJNcAmi tvA bhavAsharvau manve vAM yo giriShu dive svAhAgnis takmAnam agner ivAsyAva mA pApmant sR^ijAva jyAm iva varaNo vArayAtA imaM yavaM vidradhasya balAsasya namo rUrAyeti dve shIrShaktiM shIrShAmayam iti takmanAshanAni || iti takmanAshanagaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,8)     duHsvapnanAshanAni dauShvapnyaM daurjIvityaM paro 'paihi yo na jIvo 'si pary Avarte duShvapnyAd yat svapne annam ashnami yo na stAyad dipsati yo naH suptAM jAgrato yan me manso duShvapnyaM kAma svapnaM suptvA vidma te svapneti trayaH paryAyA duHsvapnanAshanAni || iti duHsvapnanAshanagaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,9)     AyuShyo yathA dyauH prANApAnAv ojo 'si tubhyam evAkShIbhyAM te muJNcAmi tvota devA Avatas ta upa priyam antakAya mR^ityava A rabhasva prANAya namo viShAsahim ity AyuShyANi || iti AyuShyagaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,10)     varcasyo ye triShaptA asmin vasu prAtar agniM hastivarcasaM siMhe vyAghre yasho havir yashasaM mendro girAv aragarATeShu yathA somaH prAtaHsavane yac ca varco akSheShu yena mahAnaghnyA jaghanam iti varcasyAni || iti varcasyagaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,11)     svastyayano amUH pAre pAtaM na indrApUShaNA tvaShTA me daivyaM yena soma namo devavadhebhyo 'bhayaM mitrAvaruNAv upa prAgAt sahasrAkSho 'namitraM no adharAd yamomR^ityur bR^ihaspatir naH pari pAtu tyam U Shu trAtAram indraH sutrAmA sa sutrAmA A mandrair indra marmANi te varma me dyAvApR^ithivI aindrAgnaM varma girayas te yat te madhyaM yAs te prAcIr mA naH pashcAd iti svastyayanAni || iti svastyayanagaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,12)     abhayaH svastidA vishAM brAhmaNena paryuktAsi na tA arvA reNukakATo abhayaM mitrAvaruNAv abhayaM dyAvApR^ithivI asmai grAmAya hataM tardaM pUShemA AshA indraH sutrAmA maitaM panthAM svastidA vishAM patir nama te ghoShiNIbhya A te rAShTram idam uc chreyo yata indra bhayAmaha ity abhayAni || ity abhayagaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,13)     aparAjito vidmA sharasya mA no cidann adArasR^it svastidA saMshitaM me tvayA manyo yas te manyo etA devasenA avamanyur nirhastaH pari vartmAny abhibhUr indro jAyaty abhi tvendrety aparAjitAni || ity aparAjitagaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,14)     sharmavarmA yaH sapatna itash ca yad amutash cApendra dviShato yUyaM naH pravata imam agna AyuShe tisro devIr uruvyacA no indrasya sharmAsIti uttamAM varjayitvA yena devA asurANAm anaDudbhyas tvam iti dve tanUSh Te vAjin vAjasya nu prasave devAnAM patnIr adhi brUhi rakShohaNaM vAjinaM ye srAktyaM varma me dyAvApR^iThivI aindrAgnaM varma bahulaM varma mahyam ayaM mitraH pR^ithivyod akrAmad aspatnaM purastAd iti sharmavarmA || iti sharmavarmA gaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,15)     devapurA ye purastAd brahma jaj~nAnaM sahasradhAra evAgnir mA pAtu agniM te vasuvantaM mitraH pR^ithivyod akrAmad apa ny adhuH pauruSheyaM vadhaM jitam asmAkam iti devapurIyaH || iti devapurIyagaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,16)     rudro ye 'syAM prAcI dig itirudragaNaH || iti rudragaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,17)     raudro rudra jalAShabheShaja ye 'syAM prAcI dig ud itas trayo akraman bhavAsharvau manve vAM brahma jaj~nAnam anAptA ye sahasradhAra eva grIShmo hemanto anaDudbhyas tvaM mahyam Apo vaishvAnaro yamo mR^ityur yAM te rudra yo agnau rudro bhavAsharvau mR^iDataM bhavAsharvAv idaM brUmo yas te sarpo vR^ishcikas tasmai prAcyA disho antardeshAd iti raudragaNaH || iti raudragaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,18)     citrAgaNo mA no vidann adArasR^it svastidA vishAm amUhoAre aghadviShTA agne yat te tapa iti paJNca sUktAni rudra jalAShabheShaja ye 'syAM prAcI dig vi devA uta devA agner manva itiprabhR^itIni mR^igArasUktAny uttamaM varjayitvApa naH shoshucad aghaM pR^ithivyAm agnaye mamAgne vrahma jaj~nAnam anAptA ye sahasradhAre savitA prasavAnAM nava prANAn pAtaM nas tvaShTA me yena soma namo devavadhebhyo 'bhayaM mitrAvaruNAv upa prAgAt sahasrAkShaH siMhe vyAghre 'bhayaM dyAvApR^ithivI grIShmo hemanto 'naDudbhyas tvaM mahyam Apo vaishvAnaro yamo mR^ityur abhi tvendra vishvajit trAyamANAyai imaM me agne viShANA pAshAn shakadhUmaM somArudreti dve bR^ihaspatir nas tyam U Shu trAtAram indraH sutrAmA A mandrair indra marmANi te antakAya mR^ityavA A rabhasvAyaM pratisaro 'yaM me varaNo bhavAsharvau mR^iDataM prANAya namo 'gniM brUma ity arthasUktaM satyaM bR^ihad iti dve prathame girayas te yat te madhyaM yAs te prAcIr mA naH pashcAd grIShmas te bhUme varShANy upasthAs te bhUme mAtaH sahasrashR^iN^go vR^iShabho jAtavedA mA pra gAma patho yo yaj~nasya tasmai prAcyA disho antardeshAd iti paryAyash citrAgaNaH || iti citrAgaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,19)     patnIvanto aditir dyauH sinIvAli kuhUM devIm iti trINi sUktAni patnIvantaH || iti patnIvantagaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,19b)     svasti mAtra indra juShasvAyA viShThA shive te stAM pAdAbhyAM te saM te shirShNo vatso virAja ity ekA uccA patantam iti dve bhUyAn indro viShAsahiM sahamAnam ity AdityagaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,20)     shaM no devI shaM na indrAgnI shaM no vAto vAtu shAntA dyauH pippalAdishAntigaNaH || iti pippalA[di]shAntigaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,21)     gane yad iti paJNca sUktAni paJNcApatyAni bhavanti pAJNcajanyAni bhavanti pAJNcApatyo gaNaH || iti paJNcApatyagaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,22)     ambayo yanti shambhumayobhubhyAM brahma jaj~nAnam asya vAmasya yo rohita ud asya krtavo mUrdhAham iti dve sUkte viShAsahim iti salilagaNaH || iti salilagaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,23)     ye triShaptA iti vishvakarmA gaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,24)     aghadviShTA devajAtA shaM no devI varaNo vArayA[tai] pippalI vidradhasya yA babhrava iti gaNakarmA gaNo bhaisajyash ca bhavati || iti bhaiShajyagaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,25)     ayaM te yonir A no bhara dhItI vA ya ity arthasUktam utthApano gaNaH || ity utthApanagaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,26)     ambayo yanti shambhumayobhU hiraNyavarNA niHsAlAM ye agnayo brahma jaj~nAnam ity ekaita devA mR^igArasUktAny uttamaM varjayitvApa naH shoshucad aghaM punantu mA sasruShIr himavataH pra sravanti vAyog pUtaH pavitreNa shaM ca no mayash ca no 'naDudbhyas tvaM mahyam Apo vaishvAnaro rashmibhir yamo mR^ityur vishvajit saMj~nAnaM no yady antarikShe punar maitv indriyaM shivA naH shaM no vAto vAtu agniM brUmo vanaspatIn iti shAntigaNaH || iti sarvaiH sUktaiH kaushikoktabR^ihacchAntigaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,27)     ambayo yanti shambhumayobhU hiraNyavarNA uta devA yady antarikShe punar naitv indriyaM shivA naH shaM no vAto vAtv agniM brUmo vanaspatIn iti shAntAtIyo laghushAntigaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,28)     ye triShaptA mamAgne varcaH prAtar agniM girAv aragarATeShu divas pR^ithivyA hastivarcasaM siMhe vyAghre yasho havir yas te gandha iti tisR^ibhir varcasyagaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,29)     yA asurA manuShyA mA no vidan namo devavadhebhya ity abhayagaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,30)     bhUto bhUteShv iti rAjAnam abhiShekagaNaH ||
(AVParis_32,31)     [ya] AshAnAm AshApAlebhyo agner manva iti sapta sUktAni yA oShadhayaH somarAj~nIr vaishvAnaro na A gamac chumbhanI dyAvApR^ithivI yad arvAcI[na]m agniM brUmo vanaspatIn iti muJNcantu nA bhavAshArvA yA devIr yan mAtalI rathakrItam ity etAsh catasro varjayitvA aMholiN^gagaNaH ||

(ParishiShTa_33. ghR^itakambalam)

(AVParis_33,1.1)     oM brahmaNe brahmavedAya namaskR^itvA svayaMbhuve | ghR^itakambalaM pravakShyAmi brahmaNo nigado yathA ||
(AVParis_33,1.2)     bR^ihaspatir mahendrAya cakAra ghR^itakambalam ||
(AVParis_33,1.13)     athendro ha vA asuraiH parAjitash cintAm Apede
(AVParis_33,1.4)     taM savitAbravIt prAyashcittaM kuruShvApratiruddho bhaviShyasIti
(AVParis_33,1.5)     tam indro 'bravIt || bhagavan tvam evApratiruddhaH prAyashcittaM kurv iti ||
(AVParis_33,1.6)     sa prAyashcittam akarot
(AVParis_33,1.7)     puNye nakShatre bArhaspatye muhUrte 'bhijity audumbaraM kumbhaM droNena sADhakena pUrayitvA tasminn eva vAsaprabhR^itayaH oShadhayo darbhaprabhR^itayash ca bilvagaurasarShapAsh cety etAn saMbhArAn saMbhR^itya ghR^itakumbhaM barhiShy AdhAyaitair gaNair AjyaM juhuyAt ||
(AVParis_33,1.8)     pra pateta ity ekenAN^gAdaN^gAc chamalam avalikhya sapatnaM bhrAtR^ivyaM hR^idaye imarmaNi vAsinAvidhya gomayena kAShAyeNa vAcchAdya shAnter apratighAtakaM karma tato jyeShThaM ghR^itakambalaM brahmaNaH putram akarot
(AVParis_33,1.9)     tasya ha vA etasya ghR^itakambalasya sAvitrIgaNasharIrasya shantAtIyaH shiraH triShaptIyo mukhaM rudraraudrau cakShuShI ghR^italiN^ga AsyaM nairR^ito jihvA dantoShThAv abhayAparAjitau kR^ityAdUShaNacAtanau shrotre sharmavarmasvastyayanau bAhU mAtR^inAmavAShToShpatyau pAdau....pAyush ca bhaiShajyaM nyAyaH prANApAnAv iti mImAMsata ity
(AVParis_33,1.10)     eSha ha vai jyeShTho ghR^itakambalo brahmaNaH putro 'parAjitagaNeneShTvendro 'surAn ajayan mR^ityum alakShmIm arAtiM duHsvapnadurbhUtAny ajayad
(AVParis_33,1.11)     yathA caivaMvidvAn ghR^itakambalaM kurute sarvakAmAn Apnoti sarvavyAdhirahito bhavati brahmalokam avApnotIti brAhmaNam ||

(AVParis_33,2.1)     yadA sarvam idaM vyAptam asurair nAvasheShitam | sthAtuM devAH parAbhUtAs te 'tharvANam upAgatAH ||
(AVParis_33,2.2)     karmAdy ekaM kuruShva tvaM yad bhR^igvaN^girasor matam | asurANAM vadhArthAyety uktaH kartAtha so 'bhavat ||
(AVParis_33,2.3)     paracakropasR^iShTasya rAj~no vijayam icchataH | pratiruddhasya vA bhUyaH shrIkAmasyecchataH shriyam ||
(AVParis_33,2.4)     prAdurbhAvAdbhutAnAM ca grahANAM vigrahe tathA | shaN^kamAno 'bhicArAd vA kArayed ghR^itakambalam ||
(AVParis_33,2.5)     ghR^itamAtrA tu vij~neyA mAgadhaprasthasaMmitA | shatAni paJNca droNAnAM palaikashatam eva vA ||

(AVParis_33,3.1)     [sarvapApapraNAshAya sarvakAmArthasiddhaye | sarvarogakShayArthAya prayojyo ghR^itakambalaH] ||
(AVParis_33,3.2)     ghR^itapramANaM vakShyAmi mAShakaM paJNcakR^iShNalam | mAShakANi catuhShaShTiH palam ekaM vidhIyate ||
(AVParis_33,3.3)     dvAtriMshatpalakaM prasthaM mAgadhaiH parikIrtitam | ADhakaM tu catuHprasthaM caturbhir droNam ADhakaiH ||
(AVParis_33,3.4)     droNapramANaM vij~neyaM brahmaNA nirmitaM purA | dvAdashAbhyadhikair nityaM palAnAM paJNcabhiH shataiH ||
(AVParis_33,3.5)     [ghR^itamAtrA tu vij~neyA mAgadhaprasthasaMmitA | shatAni paJNca droNAnAM palAnAM vA shatottare] ||
(AVParis_33,3.6)     ghR^itadroNashatenokta eko droNavaras tathA | yathAshakti prayuJNjIta ghR^itaM kR^itvAtha bhAgashaH ||
(AVParis_33,3.7)     caturbhAgo 'bhiShekAya caturbhAgas tu hUyate | bhAgo deyaH sadasyebhyaH kartA bhAgena yujyate ||

(AVParis_33,4.1)     puShye prayogaM kurvIta prAjApatye 'tha mArute | vaiShNave pUShadaivatye uttareShv atha vA triShu ||
(AVParis_33,4.2)     taptakR^ichrAvasAne vA sarvakR^ichrasya cAntataH | yasmin vA snAtakA brUyus tatra kuryAd vicakShaNaH ||
(AVParis_33,4.3)     pAkayaj~navidhAnena kR^itvopakramaNaM budhaH | nishAkAle bahirgrAme kuryAd agniniveshanam ||
(AVParis_33,4.4)     yajeta nirR^itiM tatra kR^iShNavAsAsh catuShpathe | yathoktaM nairR^itair mantrair havirbhish ca yathAkramam ||
(AVParis_33,4.5)     tR^itIyena tu sUktena nivedya balim antataH | yathAvyAvartane caiva yad uktaM tat samAcaret ||

(AVParis_33,5.1)     tataH snAtaH shuklavAsAH prAshya shAntyudakaM shuciH | paryukShyopasamAdhAya ghR^itasaMskAra iShyate ||
(AVParis_33,5.2)     pUrvaM mahAvyAhR^itibhiH sAvitryA tadanantaram | shAntish ca brahma jaj~nAnaM brahma bhrAjad itIti ca ||
(AVParis_33,5.3)     agne gobhir agne 'bhyAvartinn agne jAtavedaH saha rayyA punar Urjeti ||
(AVParis_33,5.4)     agnim ILe purohitam agna A yAhi vItaye | bR^ihaspatir na ity ekA bR^ihaspate yuvaM tathA ||
(AVParis_33,5.5)     etair AjyaM ca juhuyAt saMpAtAn Anayed ghR^ite | kR^ityAdUShaNamantraish ca kuryAc chAntyudake vidhim ||
(AVParis_33,5.6)     saMpAtAn Anayet tatra cAtanair mAtR^inAmabhiH | vAstoShpatyair vAShToShpatAv Anayet samadUShaNam ||
(AVParis_33,5.7)     nidhAya havir AsAdya ghR^itakumbhaM susaMskR^itam | ghR^itabhAgau tu yAv anyau pUrveNAgner nidhApayet ||
(AVParis_33,5.8)     darbhAdIn tu vAsAdIMsh ca saMbhArAn gaurasarShapAn | bilvaM ca kumbhe nidhAyApareNAgner nidhApayet ||

(AVParis_33,6.1)     sAvitraH shantAtIyash ca kR^ityAdUShaNa eva ca | abhayAparAjitAyuShyA varcasyash ca tataH paraH ||
(AVParis_33,6.2)     saMsaktIyaH suShuptIyaH svastyayanaH sharmavarma ca | cAtano mAtR^inAmAni bhaiShajyaM nyAya eva ca ||
(AVParis_33,6.3)     ghR^italiN^gau tathA raudrau saMpAtAn Anayed ghR^ite | gaNAnteShu yathAshakti brAhmaNAn svastivAcayet ||
(AVParis_33,6.4)     yo 'sminn akShIbhyAM te sahasrAkShaM brahma jaj~nAnam | brahma bhrAjad ud agAd idam Apas tathApash ca ||
(AVParis_33,6.5)     abhiShiJNcet sarvamantrair AyuShyair abhayais tathA | mR^iNmayash cAtra bhavati dveShyasya ca parAkR^itiH ||
(AVParis_33,6.6)     abhiShiJNcet sarvamantrair AyuShyair abhayais tathA | mR^iNmayash cAtra bhavati dveShyasya ca parAkR^itiH ||
(AVParis_33,6.7)     tasyopariShTAd abhiShicya kuryAn mAtrAtalekhanIm | aN^gAdaN^gAd athAnyena pra pateti catasR^ibhiH ||
(AVParis_33,6.8)     bhrAtR^ivyaham iti vaishvAnaroyanty avasAnena | dyAvAdinA paryAyeNa samalaMkR^iTam ullikhet ||
(AVParis_33,6.9)     dviShantaM me parAvad vi dviShantaM nir dahantu me | bhrAtR^ivyatAn iti dvAbhyAM paryAyAsh ca trayaH parAH ||
(AVParis_33,6.10)     anvAlabhya tu kartAram upaviShTa udaÇmukhaH | svapnatakmAShTanayanaiH saubhAgyair varmabhis tathA ||
(AVParis_33,6.11)     rudraraudraparair mantrair Ajyahomo vidhIyate | srAktyaM vA yadi vAshvattham audumbaram athApi vA ||
(AVParis_33,6.12)     shaN^khaM ca maNim Abadhya pratisarair abhimantrayet | anvArabhyAbhiShekaM tu raudrAbhyAM juhuyAt tataH ||

(AVParis_33,7.1)     yat te vAsa [iti] paridhAnaM yathoktaM paridhApayet | rocanA guggulu ghR^itam abhyaJNjanam athAJNjanam ||
(AVParis_33,7.2)     tata etair alaMkR^itya IkShayetAdarShe mukham | dasha gA dakShiNAM dadyAd vR^iShabhaM ghR^itam eva ca ||
(AVParis_33,7.3)     brAhmaNAn svastivAcyAtha prAÇmukhaH saMvishet tataH | rakShohaNam [ity] anuvAkaM japet kartAtha R^itvijaH ||
(AVParis_33,7.4)     sharmavarmaitad uktaM snAtasya rakShobhyo 'bhayaMkaram iti ||
(AVParis_33,7.5)     na rAkShasA na gandharvA na pishAcA na cAsurAH | krUrAH puruShamarmaj~nA na hiMsanti ghR^itArcitam ||
(AVParis_33,7.6)     siddhAbhiSheko naishash ca ghR^itakambalam eva ca | lakShaH puShyAbhiShekash ca pradhAnAvabhR^itas tathA ||
(AVParis_33,7.7)     mahAshAntitrayastriMshat tatra ShaT prastaraiH saha | niyatAnyevadR^ichAyA kartavyA bhUtim icchatA ||

(ParishiShTa_34. anulomakalpaH)
(AVParis_34,1.0)     oM namo 'tharvavedAya ||

(AVParis_34,1.1)     akSharAni vilomAni na svaraM pratilomayet | pratyArambhanighAteShu sthAnAny anyAni nirdishet ||
(AVParis_34,1.2)     yakAras tu takArAnto antyasvaritasaMj~nitaH | sa tUdAttaH sa evAdau dakAraH shiShyate guruH ||
(AVParis_34,1.3)     dakArAt svaryate nIcam upodAtte pra yojayet | anyAni tu yathApUrvam udAttapracitAni tu ||
(AVParis_34,1.4)     prathamo 'ShTAkSharo 'rdharco dvitIyaH ShoDashAkSharaH | AdAv ante ca vij~neyA vyAhR^itish cApy atharvaNAm ||
(AVParis_34,1.5)     raktavarNA vilomA ca yamena parikIrtitA | sarvashatruvinAshAya sarvakarmArthasiddhaye ||
(AVParis_34,1.6)     mR^ityush ca devatA cAsyA nichannaM chanda ucyate | svAhAkAre tu phaTkAraH koTihome vidhiH smR^itaH ||
(AVParis_34,1.7)     anulomAM vilomAM vA gAyatrIM yaH paThet sadA | sarvArthAs tasya sidhyanti na cAnarthAn samashnute ||
(AVParis_34,1.8)     t yA da co pra naH yo yo dhi || hi ma dhI sya va de rgo bha yam NI re rva tu vi tsa ta t ||

(ParishiShTa_35. AsurIkalpaH)

(AVParis_35,1.1)     oM kaTuke kaTukapattre subhage Asuri rakte raktavAsase | atharvaNasya duhite aghore aghorakarmakArike ||
(AVParis_35,1.2)     amukaM hanahana dahadaha pacapaca mathamatha | tAvad daha tAvat paca yAvan me vasham Anayasi svAhA ||
(AVParis_35,1.3)     shayyAvasthitAyAs tAvaj japed yAvat svapiti || prasthitAyA gatiM daha svAhA || upaviShTAyA bhagaM daha svAhA || suptAyA mano daha svAhA prabuddhAyA gR^idayaM daha svAheti ||
(AVParis_35,1.4)     athAta AsurIkalpam upadeshAd atharvaNaH | nAsyAs tithir na nakShatraM nopavAso vidhIyate ||
(AVParis_35,1.5)     ghR^itAdidravyasarveShu AsurI shatajApitA | pattrAdyavayavash cAsyA jikaiShA cAnuyAyinI ||
(AVParis_35,1.6)     hantukAmo hi shatrUMsh ca vashIkurvaMsh ca bhUpatIn | AsurIshlakShNapiShTAjyaM juhuyAd AkR^itiM budhaH ||
(AVParis_35,1.7)     arkendhanAgniM prajvAlya chittvAstreNAkR^itiM tu tAm | pAdAgrato 'ShTasahasraM juhuyAd yasya vashy asau ||
(AVParis_35,1.8)     ghR^itAktayA strI vashinI pAlAshAgnau dvijottamAH | guDAktayA kShatriyAs tu vaishyAs tu dadhimishrayA ||
(AVParis_35,1.9)     shUdrAs tu lavaNamishrai rAjikAM piShTayed budhaH | A saptAhAt sarva ete AsurIhomato vashAH ||
(AVParis_35,1.10)     kaTutailena trisaMdhyaM kulocchedaM karoti hi | shunAM tu lomabhiH sArdham apasmArI tribhir dinaiH ||
(AVParis_35,1.11)     nivR^ittiH kShIramadhvAjyair lavaNena tu sajvarI | arkaidhaHsamidagnau tu kAryo visphoTasaMbhavaH ||
(AVParis_35,1.12)     teShAm upashamaM vidyAt surAshvaryA ghR^itena ca | arkakShIrAktayAR^ikAgnAv akShiNI sphoTayed dviShaH ||
(AVParis_35,1.13)     gatAsumAMsaM tasyaiva nirmAlyaM citibhasma ca | eShAM cUrNena saMspR^iShTo hAsyashIlo 'bhijAyate ||
(AVParis_35,1.14)     ajAkShIrAktayA homAt tasya mokSho vidhIyate | tagaraM kuShThamAMsI ca tasyAH pattrANi caiva hi ||
(AVParis_35,1.15)     etaiH shlakShNais tu saMspR^iShTaH pR^iShThataH paridhAvati | tasyAH phalAni mUlAni surabhIhastimedasA ||
(AVParis_35,1.16)     sUkShmAt taddravyasaMsparshAd anudhAvaty acetasaH | achidrapattrANy asita ushIraH sarShapAs tathA ||
(AVParis_35,1.17)     etacshUrNAt pUrvaphalaM ghR^ite caivAparAjayaH ||

(AVParis_35,2.1)     kusumAni manahshilApriyaN^gutagarANi ca | gajendramadasaMyuktaM kiM kurvANas tv akR^id varam ||
(AVParis_35,2.2)     yAsh ca striyo 'bhigacchanti tA vashAH padAlepataH | sapuShpAM tAM samAdAya aJNjanaM nAgakesharam ||
(AVParis_35,2.3)     anenAktAbhyAm akShibhyAM yamyaM pashyet sa kiMkaraH | aJNjanaM tagaraM kuShThaM devIjaM kAShTham eva ca ||
(AVParis_35,2.4)     mANsI ca sarvabhUtAnAM saubhAgyasya tu kAraNam | tatsamidhAM lakShahomAn nidhAnaM pashyate mahat ||
(AVParis_35,2.5)     sarpirdadhimadhvaktapattrANAM vR^iddhaputrI sahasrataH | rAjyaM tu labhate vashyaM tatpattratrisahasrataH ||
(AVParis_35,2.6)     svarNasahasrasyAptis tu tatpuShpANAM tu lakShataH | sahasrajApAc ca tadvad udake kShIrabhakShiNaH ||
(AVParis_35,2.7)     vAripUrNe 'tha kalashe lokeshIpallavAn kShipet | snAnAd alakShmyA mucyeta sauvarNakalashe 'pi tu ||
(AVParis_35,2.8)     vinAyakebhyaH snAnato daurbhAgyAc caiva durbhagAt | pR^iShThatash cAnudhAvanti saMspR^iShTa udakena tu ||
(AVParis_35,2.9)     ushIraM tagaraM kuShThaM mustA tatpattrasarShapAH | cUrNenAbhihatas tUrNam Ishvaro 'pi vasho bhavet ||
(AVParis_35,2.10)     tulasIbhUmahAdevIcUrNaspR^iShTas tathA vashI | rAjAbhayaM sureshvarImArjanAd bhAraNAt tathA ||
(AVParis_35,2.11)     na syAt tasyAdbhutaM kiM cin na kShudropadravas tathA | nAnaishvaryaM nAprajatvaM yasya devy AsurI gR^ihe ||

(ParishiShTa_36. ucchuShmakalpaH)

(AVParis_36,1.1)     oM nama ucchuShmebhyaH
(AVParis_36,1.2)     ....shikhAM devIM prapadye shaMkarAyaNIM | sarvArthasAdhanIM vibhvIM sarveshIM brahmacAriNIm ||
(AVParis_36,1.3)     te iShTakAkArakarAlam aticaturmukham || caturvidhais tu rUpaM dhyAnam ||
(AVParis_36,1.4)     shive jaTile brahmacAriNi stambhani jambhani mohani huM phaT namaH svAhA ||
(AVParis_36,1.5)     AtmarakShA ||
(AVParis_36,1.6)     prAcyAM dishIndro rAjA devAnAm AdhipatyaM kurute | taM devaM bhagavantaM sagaNaM sAnucaraM saparivAraM sashirAH praNipatya vij~nApayati | vajreNa praharaNenemAM dishaM vidishaM ca sarvakalikaluSham ashubhaM prashamayoM namaH svAhA ||
(AVParis_36,1.7)     dakShiNasyAM dishi yamo rAjA pretAnAm Adhipatyam iti | daNDena praharaNeneti ||
(AVParis_36,1.8)     pratIcyAM dishi varuNo rAjApAm Adhipatyam iti | pAshena praharaNeneti ||
(AVParis_36,1.9)     udIcyAM dishi kubero rAjA yakShANAm Adhipatyam iti | gadayA prahareNeti ||
(AVParis_36,1.10)     dhruvAyAM dishi vAsukI rAjA nAgAnAm Adhipatyam iti | daMShTrayA praharaNeneti ||
(AVParis_36,1.11)     UrdhvAyAM dishi somo rAjA nakShatrANAm AdhipatyaM kurute | taM devaM bhagavaM sagaNaM sAnucaraM saparivAraM sashirAH praNipatya vij~nApayati || tejasA praharaNenemAM dishaM vidishaM ca sarvakalikaluSham ashubhaM prashamayoM namaH svAhA ||
(AVParis_36,1.12)     athocchuShmahR^idayam || dyurudyuru daradara vidArayavidAraya milimili namaH svAhA ||
(AVParis_36,1.13)     ucchuShmashikhA || shive jaTila iti prathamaH ||
(AVParis_36,1.14)     kurukuru murumuru mahA muJNca mahA muJNca viduvidu namaH svAhA || iti kavacam ||
(AVParis_36,1.15)     oM namo mahApiN^galAya siMhanAdanAdine namaH svAhA || ity astramantraH ||

(AVParis_36,2.1)     eShAm ucchuShmarudrANAm ataH kalpo nigadyate | atharvavedodbhavAnAM tithyR^ikShAdyayogataH ||
(AVParis_36,2.2)     grAme vAthApy araNye vA pracareta yathAvidhi | sadyaHsiddhikarA hy ete ucchuShmAH parikIrtitAH ||
(AVParis_36,2.3)     AtmarakShAM dishAM bandhaM shikhAbandhaM ca sarvadA | etair eva yathAyogam Adau kuryAd vicakShaNaH ||
(AVParis_36,2.4)     khadirasyodumbarasya tathA bilvapalAshayoH | dadhisarpirmadhuyujAM shAntAnAM vApi bilvataH ||
(AVParis_36,2.5)     samitsahasratritayaM hutvA shAntir gavAM bhavet | tIkShNAsR^igviShayuktAnAM phaTkArash ca vinAshane ||
(AVParis_36,2.6)     prayogAd apy asiddhish cet tatkarmedaM samArabhet | ucchuShmarUpI bhakShayaMs tIkShNaH saktUdakAni tu ||

(AVParis_36,3.1)     abhIShTAM vA striyaM gatvA dhyAtvA vA reta utsR^ijet | mUtrAM purIShaM cotsR^ijya gokaN^kAlAdhirohaNam ||
(AVParis_36,3.2)     kR^itvA mantraM nishi japed yAvad goshR^iN^gatash caret | jvAlAbhaN^gaM tatas tasya karmasiddhiM samAdishet ||
(AVParis_36,3.3)     [dadhimadhughR^itAktAnAm iti sheShaH] ||

(AVParis_36,4.1)     saptakShIrAJNjaligrAsaH sruvo hy asmin prashasyate | kShIraM tenAtha juhuyAd dhanakAmasya nityashaH ||
(AVParis_36,4.2)     ghR^itena tejaskAmasya AyuHkAmasya dUrvayA | kukusaM tumbaraM vApi vidyAd uccATakarmaNi ||

(AVParis_36,5.1)     brAhmaNaM tu vashIkartuM shAlipiShTamayIM tanum | kR^itvA catuShpathaM gatvA gR^ihItvA shastram uttamam ||
(AVParis_36,5.2)     aShTottarasahasreNa kR^itvA tadabhimantraNam | aShTAN^gaM tena tAM chitvA mantrato vasham Anayet ||
(AVParis_36,5.3)     aShTottarasahasraM vA prakR^ite juhuyAd budhaH | brAhmaNIM tu vashIkartuM kuryAn mAShamayIM tanum ||

(AVParis_36,6.1)     sarpirdadhimadhvaktAnAM lAjAnAm AhutIH shubhAH | kanyAkAmo 'ShTasahasraM hutvA kanyAm avApnuyAt ||
(AVParis_36,6.2)     api vA piShTamayyAH prAg juhuyAt saMdhyayAhutIH | darbheShIkAM vAbhimantrya tadgR^ihe nishcalAM nyaset ||
(AVParis_36,6.3)     tAvad udvejayet sA tu vajrabhUtA hi tadgR^iham | kanyAyAH sAdhanIyAyAs [tu] yAval lAbhas tato bhavet ||

(AVParis_36,7.1)     pradhAnam anyaM vA kiM cid vashIkartuM narottamam | samidhaH khadirAdInAm audumbaryash ca homayet ||
(AVParis_36,7.2)     shmashAnakhaTvAN^gamayIM homayen mantrasAdhane | palANDulashunaprasthaM hutvA mastaM na saMshayaH ||
(AVParis_36,7.3)     shirIShAN^gamayIM rAj~no balis trimadhureNa tu | brAhmaNe pAyasamayIM kShatriyasya viShANikAm ||
(AVParis_36,7.4)     vaishyasya sAdhane homyAsh cUrNaiH surabhisaMskR^itAH | catuShpathe tu shUdrasya padminyutkaraNena tu ||

(AVParis_36,8.1)     likhitvA nAma saMgR^ihya karAgrAN^gulipIDitAm | shiraHpIDA jvaraH shUlaM vimatiH svastyasaMgatiH ||
(AVParis_36,8.2)     balyAdyA vA prayoktavyA brAhmaNAdicatuShTaye | evaM saty abhicArash ca caturNAm api darshitaH ||
(AVParis_36,8.3)     liN^gaM vA rAjasarShapaiH samAlikhyAtha dhUpayet | gaurair arghaM tathA dadyAn mriyate sApy asaMshayam ||
(AVParis_36,8.4)     abhakShabhakSho hy asvAsthyaM sarvarogaprakopanam | niHsaMj~natA piNDapAto japAvR^ittyA bhavanti hi ||
(AVParis_36,8.5)     ekAdashaM na japtavyaM kulotsAdas tato bhavet ||

(AVParis_36,9.1)     oM namo mahApiN^galAya trivR^ite trivR^ite namaH svAhA ||
(AVParis_36,9.2)     namaH sarAntitevatevasu trivR^ite trivR^ite triparvaNe trishIrShAya namaH svAhA ||
(AVParis_36,9.3)     namaH kaTavikaTakaNTemATe pATale vikale asauryAsau asauryAsau pR^ithivIShTakA iShTakAjinAtyUnyo saugaluMtigaluMtekaTamasi kaTapravR^ite pradviSha rudra raudreNAveshayAveshaya hanahana dahadaha pacapaca mathamatha vidhvaMsayavidhvaMsaya vishveshvara yogeshvara maheshvara namas te 'stu mA mA hiMsIH huM phaT namaH svAhA ||

(AVParis_36,10.1)     eShAM krameNa kR^ityAni vakShyamANAni yojayet | aShTasahasrAbhijaptam anyad dravyaM tu homataH ||
(AVParis_36,10.2)     shatror nAmnA lavaNasya sahasram aShTakAdhikam | hutvA dhanAyuShor hAnir jvareNa sa ca shuShyati ||
(AVParis_36,10.3)     kShipraM shAntir bhavet tasya kShIrahomAt tu tAvataH ||

(AVParis_36,11.1)     kaNaiH puttalikAM kR^itvA goshR^iN^geNArghadhUpabe | aShTasahasrAbhijaptaM madanasya tu kaNTakam || tenAShTAdashavedhAt tu mUlakShIrAn nivartanam ||

(AVParis_36,12.1)     dadhnA ca madhusarpirbhyAM ttrivarNaiH sarShapair hutaiH || gaurair aShTasahasreNa japtair Aveshayed ripUn ||

(AVParis_36,13.1)     dadhyAdyabhyaktalAjAnAM homAd aShTasahasrataH || nAshayet satatajvaraM dvitIyAdiM ca dUrataH ||

(AVParis_36,14.1)     parijapya darbheShIkAM kumbhakArAdiveshmasu | nyastvA pAkaM surApAkaM kaivartAdi vinAshayet ||

(AVParis_36,15.1)     akShatais taNDulaiH kR^itvA pratidehaM sushobhanam | saMsthApya dhAnyarAshau taM candanAduru dAhayet | baliM trimadhuraM dattvA syAt sa rAshish caturguNaH ||

(AVParis_36,16.1)     khAdiraM kIlakaM tIkShNaM tailAktaM dvAdashAN^gulam | parijaptaM grAmamadhye nikhanet sadya udvaset ||
(AVParis_36,16.2)     mahApAtakadoSheNa grAmI nirdhanatAM vrajet | kShIreNa kIlakasnAnAt kuryAt tuShTas tu shAntikam ||
(AVParis_36,16.3)     kShIrasyAShTasahasraM ca juhuyAt tadanantaram ||

(AVParis_36,17.1)     kalApamantrAM guTikAM tannAmnA gavyamAMsataH | mahApAtakasaMbandhAj jAyate 'sya dhanakShayaH ||

(AVParis_36,18.1)     trivarNasarShapair homAt saha trimadhureNa tu | saMpadyate sutas tasya medhAvI shrutadhArakaH | taddhomAt ke cid icchanti unmattatvaM na saMshayaH ||

(AVParis_36,19.1)     tilA dUrvA trimadhuraM homato vyAdhinigraham | taNDulaprakShepash ca ||

(AVParis_36,23.1)     dugdhAktAn sarShapAn hutvA tasmAd bhasma mukhe kShipet | sarveShu vyavahAreShu sa bhavaty aparAjitaH ||

(AVParis_36,24.1)     shastraM japtam upAdAya raNe grasto na jIyate | khanakhanAyeti mantraH pUrvasevArtha ucyate ||
(AVParis_36,24.2)     uttarasyA visheShAd vA cedAnIm ata uttaram | khAdiratryaktasamidhAM pUrvasevA sahasrataH | atasIsamidhAm evaM medhAvI viduShAM prabhuH ||

(AVParis_36,25.1)     gocarmamAtraM sthaNDilaM gomayenopalepayet | tatrAgniM trikapAleShu jvAlayitvA praNamya ca ||

(AVParis_36,25.3)     damShTrAghaNTAninAdAs tu jvAlAmukhabhayAnakAH | yat tvaM kAmayase putra tat sarvaM dadmahe vayam ||

(AVParis_36,26.1)     lakShajApottaraM gatvA nadIm udadhigAminIm | vAlukAsthaNDile liN^gaM tanmayaM tajjasadmani ||
(AVParis_36,26.2)     padmAShTashatam AhR^itya pUjayitvA vidhAnataH | udake nAbhimAtre ca suprabhAtaM punar japet ||
(AVParis_36,26.3)     tato mANDaliko rAjA dInArANAM gavAM shatam | praNamya shraddhayA tasmai dadyAd uddhara mAm iti ||

(AVParis_36,27.1)     lakShajapAd abAdhyas tu pashUnAM damShTrishR^iN^giNAm | itareShAM pashUnAM tu lakShatritayavardhanam ||

(ParishiShTa_37. samuccayaprAyashcittAni) [resembles in form the 13th adhyAya of the KaushikasUtra]

(AVParis_37,1.1)     oM bhR^igvaN^girorUpadhAriNe shivAya namaH || atha yatraitad apahanyamAne musalaM patati tad ghoraM bhavati tad apy etad R^icoktam ||
(AVParis_37,1.2)     ulUlhalAn musalaM patitaM hinasti patnIMkule jyeShTham | kR^iShIH prajAH pashavaH saMvisheante yathendrasR^iShTaM prapateta vajram iti ||
(AVParis_37,1.3)     tad vajraM shAntyudakena saMprokShya arAtIyor ity ullikhya yat tvA shikva iti prakShAlya barhiShy AdhAya juhoti ||
(AVParis_37,1.4)     vajraH patitas tu varaM hinasti taM tvA vayam apahanma ghoram | sa naH shivo 'stu dviShatAM vadhAya sapatnAn me dviShato hantu sarvAn ||
(AVParis_37,1.5)     yadvat prajAH papanayad dhastAd yadi volUkhalAt | sapatnAn me paripAhi mAM tv evaM paripAhi naH ||
(AVParis_37,1.6)     yady antarikShe yadi vAsi soccair vajraH sR^iShTo yadi vA pArthivair uta | mantrAH prayuktA vitatA mahAnto 'ghoro vajro musalaprapAtaH ||
(AVParis_37,1.7)     vajro 'si sapatnaheti tisraH ||
(AVParis_37,1.8)     vajro 'si sapatnahA tvayAdya vR^itraM sAkShIya | tvAm adya vanaspate vR^ikShANAm ud ayuShmahi ||
(AVParis_37,1.9)     sa na indrapurohito vishvataH pAhi rakShasaH | abhi gAvo anUShatAbhi dyumnaM bR^ihaspate ||
(AVParis_37,1.10)     prANa prANaM trAyasvAso asave mR^iDa | nirR^ite nirR^ityA naH pAshebhyo muJNca iti ||
(AVParis_37,1.11)     tyam U Shu trAtAram indraH sutrAmA sa sutrAmA A mandrair indra marmANi te varmaNA chAdayAmIti ulUkhalamusale saMpAtAn AnIya saMsthApya homAn ulUkhalam annenaiva pUrayitvA pratipravartayed ulUkhalamusalaM vasanaM ca gAM ca kartre dadyAt sA tatra prAyashcittiH ||

(AVParis_37,2.1)     atha yat kAko 'bhimR^ishati tan mR^ityum AshaN^kyaM bhavati || tad apy etad R^icoktam ||....antakAya mR^ityava A rabhasva prANAya nama iti svAheti agnau hutvA sA tatra prAyashcittiH ||

(AVParis_37,3.1)     athAta AjyasthAlI cyavate pracalati vA kA tatra prAyashcittiH || saMnatimahAvyAhR^itisAvitrIkUShmANDyaH sa sarvAbhir juhuyAt sA tatra prAyashcittiH ||

(AVParis_37,4.1)     atha pavitram <cet> praNashyeta karmamadhyAt pramAdataH | anyac chittvA mantrayeta karmasheSham upakramet | AtmendriyasamAyuktaM tena mantreNa kArayet ||
(AVParis_37,4.2)     vAyoH pUtaH pavitreNa yan me chidraM punar maitv indriyaM mA na Apo medhAM mA no medhAM mA naH piparid ashvineti saMnatibhir AjyaM juhuyAd vyAhR^itibhish ca gAM ca kartre dadyAt sA tatra prAyashcittiH ||

(AVParis_37,5.1)     atha yasyAsamApte karmaNi barhir AdIpyeta tatas tan nirvApya juhuyAt ||
(AVParis_37,5.2)     yad agnir barhir adahad vedyA vAso apAM tataH | tvam eva no jAtavedo duritAt pAhi tasmAt ||
(AVParis_37,5.3)     nirdagdhA no amitrAs tu yathedaM barhis tathA | amitrANAM shriyaM bhUtiM tAm eShAM pari nir jahi ||
(AVParis_37,5.4)     yatkAmAs te juhumas tan no astu vishAmpate | ye devA yaj~nam AyAnti te no rakShantu sarvataH ||
(AVParis_37,5.5)     avadagdhaM duHsvapnyam avadagdhA arAtayaH | sarvAsh ca yAtudhAnyaH ||
(AVParis_37,5.6)     mA tvA dabhan yAtudhAnA mA bradhnaH shamyum icchata | darbho rAjA samudriyaH pari naH pAtu vishvataH ||
(AVParis_37,5.7)     ato 'nyad barhir upakalpyodakena saMprokShya punaH stR^iNAti ||
(AVParis_37,5.8)     idaM barhir amR^iteneha siktaM hiraNmayaM haritaM te stR^iNAmi | tad vai purANam abhinavaM stR^iNIShva vAsaH prashastaM prati me gR^ihANety anyena ca barhiShAbhiprachAdaye ||

(AVParis_37,6.1)     AhutyAM tu gR^ihItAyAM hutocchiShTaM pramAdataH | tam AhutiM pratiShThApya shaM no devIr ity Acamya brahmAparam ity ardharcenemAM hutvA brahmajyeShTheti hutvA sA tatra prAyashcittiH ||

(AVParis_37,7.1)     keshakITAvapannA cec chaMbhuvAya svAheti bhasmani hutvA havir utpUyAnyAM juhuyAt sA tatra prAyashcittiH ||

(AVParis_37,8.1)     atha cec calitadantaM patitadantaM vopanayet tatra prAyashcittam Aha gR^ihe vA barhiH [vA] pitA vAcAryo vA dvAdasharAtraM dIkSheyAtAM kartA trirAtraM gaurasarShapasarpiHpayobhiH snAtaH prayataH shuciH shuklavAsAH paurNamAsaM tantram AjyabhAgAnte sAvitrIm anuyojayet tena shAntyudakenainam AcAmayati saMprokShati ca ||
(AVParis_37,8.2)     sAvitrI shAntir brahma jaj~nAnaM ye triShaptA agniM brUma AyuShyavarcasyasvastyayanAbhayAparAjitasharmavarmabhir juhuyAt taM saMpAtya yaH shramAt tapaso yo vetasaM yo bhUtam UrdhvA asyedAvatsarAya yady antarikShe punar maitv indriyam ity AplAvayati sA tatra prAyashcittiH ||

(AVParis_37,9.1)     nashyec cen madughamaNiH shAmyed vAgnir vivAhajaH | atyadbhutaM dvayam idaM dampatyos tu vinAshanam ||
(AVParis_37,9.2)     pUtudArumaNis tatra bandhyo mantrAsh ca mAdughAH | pUtudAru na vindyAc ced yavaM tatra niyojayet ||
(AVParis_37,9.3)     AyuShmantau suprajasau suvIrau dhAtA pUShA draviNe nau dadhAtu | vimuJNcatAM shamalaM kilbiShaM nau dIrgham Ayush ca savitA kR^iNotv iti shAntyudakenAN^guliM saMprokShya badhnIyAt
(AVParis_37,9.4)     samidho 'bhyAdadhyAd upatiShTeta saMnatibhir vyAhR^itibhir juhuyAd gAM ca kartre dadyAt sA atra prAyashcittH ||

(AVParis_37,10.1)     om atha yasya tantre 'praNIto 'huto 'gnir upashAmyati || punas tvAdityA ity agniM prANIya saMnatibhir vyAhR^itibhiH samAs tvAgne 'bhy arcateti ca sUktAbhyAM juhuyAt parisaMkhyAhomAMsh ca ||

(AVParis_37,11.1)     atha yatraitad vivAhagnir upashAmyati agnipraNayanamantraiH prAjApatyaM praNIya prAktantraM praNIya yad devA yad vidvAMso 'pamityam apratItaM yad dhastAbhyaM yad adIvyann ity etaiH sUktair AjyaM juhuyAt samidho 'bhyAdadhyAd upatiShTheta vAsaH kartre dadyAt ||

(AVParis_37,12.1)     atha yatraitat kAlAtItAsu kriyAsv atIta uttarAyaNe AjyabhAgAnte yan me skannaM yad asmR^itIty anumantrayet tasmai prAcyA disho antardeshAd iti paryAyAn ekaviMshatiM juhuyAt saMskArAtIte ca karmaNi ||

(AVParis_37,13.1)     atha yatraitat prANIto 'gnir upashAmyati || yady antarikShe punar maitv indriyaM punas tvAdityA ity agniM praNIya prajvAlya mamAgne varca iti samidham AdhAya sheShaM karma samApayet ||

(AVParis_37,14.1)     atha yasyopayAmo 'vapated dhastAt sa yan me upayAma ity AdadIta, 
(AVParis_37,14.2)     yan me upayAmo 'patad dhastAd ya AyuShA pariShkR^itaH | tam ahaM punar Adade ||
(AVParis_37,14.3)     punar indraH punar bhagaH punar me brahmaNaspatiH | brahma jIvitu dAd ity [AdadIta]
(AVParis_37,14.4)     yan me chidraM yad asmR^itIti juhuyAt ||

(AVParis_37,15.1)     yan me sruvo 'patad dhastAd ity upayAmena vyAkhyAtam ||

(AVParis_37,16.1)     mekhalAdIni cet plaveran punar upanayeta || vimocanIyAn homAn hutvAnyaM brAhmaNam anUcAnam upaveshyodapAtraM cAparAjitena niShkramya vAso yaj~nopavItAdi dattvAbhyukShyAcamyApAM sUktaiH pavitraish ca saMprokShya priyaM mA kR^iNu deveShv iti yaj~nopavItaM dattvA vimR^igvarIM mA naH pashcAd iti dvAbhyAM prAÇmukha upavishya mahAvyAhR^itibhiH sAvitrI shAntisUktaM brahma jaj~nAnaM yad asmR^ity anumatiH sarvam iti juhuyAd abhyAtAnaish ca ||

(AVParis_37,17.1)     atha yatraitan mekhalA prapatati jIrNA vA syAt tAM sAvitryoddhR^ityAntaM kR^itvA shAntyudakena saMprokShya mahAvyAhR^itibhiH sAvitrI shAntisUktaM brahma jaj~nAnaM ye triShaptA idAvatsarAya ghR^itena tvAgniM brhUma iti ||

(AVParis_37,18.1)     caturthyAm ahutAyAM yadi ghaTodakaM nashyeta tathaiva punar AnIya shaM no devIr iheta devIr ity anumantryAmbayo yanty Apo hi ShThA shaM no devIr iti saMpAtya vyAhR^ityA saMnatyA ca juhuyAt Apo bhR^igvaN^girorUpam apAM puShpam ity udakumbham abhimantrayet || vAso dakShiNA ||

(AVParis_37,19.1)     atha yasyAsasamApte karmaNy udapAtraM pravarteta tad anumantrayate
(AVParis_37,19.2)     yad udapAtraM pravartate brahmaNAsthApitaM mahat | sthAnAc cyutaM pravartitaM tan me vahatu kilbiSham || ity AsthApayati ||
(AVParis_37,19.3)     pUraNena pUrayitvA punaH pUrNam ity etayA | 
(AVParis_37,19.4)     punaH pUrNam idaM pAtaM brahmaNAsthApayAmasi | vishvais [tad] devair abhiShTutam ||
(AVParis_37,19.5)     UrjaM puShTaM dadhAtu no rAyas poShaM shriyam AyuH | mayi karma samR^idhyatAm iti ||

(AVParis_37,20.1)     atha cet prabhajyeta bhUmir bhUmim agAd ity anumantryAnyataram AhR^itya yady antarikShe punar maitv indriyam ity anumantrya vaishvAnaro na Utaya ud enaM vaishvAnaro rashmibhir iti juhuyAt sA tatra prAyashcittiH ||

(ParishiShTa_38. brahmakUrcavidhiH)

(AVParis_38,1.1)     oM brahmakUrcavidhiM puNyaM saMkShepAd vacmy asaMshayam | pAvanAnAM paraM yo hi pAvanaM tapasAM tapaH ||
(AVParis_38,1.2)     snAtvA shuciH shucau deshe gomayenAvasecite | vastreNa saMhite cApi sitapuShpaiH prapUjite ||
(AVParis_38,1.3)     ahorAtrositaH kShAntaH pavitrAtmA prapAvanaH | shuklavAsAH sugandhiH prAg upaviShTaH kushAsane ||
(AVParis_38,1.4)     gomUtraM gomayaM kShIraM dadhi sarpiH kushodakam | Aharet tAmrapAtre tu shakR^in mUtraM tv abhUgatam ||
(AVParis_38,1.5)     gomUtraM nIlavarNAyAH kR^iShNAyA gomayaM tathA | payas tu tAmravarNAyAH shvetAya Ahared dadhi ||
(AVParis_38,1.6)     kapilAyA ghR^itaM grAhyam alAbhe syAt tu paJNcamam ||

(AVParis_38,2.1)     gomUtraikapalaM dadyAd aN^guShThAgraM tu gomayam | kShIrasya sapta dadhnas tu trINy ekaikaM ghR^itAmbhasoH ||
(AVParis_38,2.2)     gAyatryAhR^itya gomUtraM gandhadvAreti gomayam | A pyAyasveti ca kShIraM dadhikrAvNeti vai dadhi ||
(AVParis_38,2.3)     tejo 'si shukram ity ajyaM devasya tvA kushodakam | saptapattrAs tu ye darbhA achinnAgrAH samAyutAH ||
(AVParis_38,2.4)     taiH samuddhR^itya hotavyaM devatAbhyo yathAkarmam | agnaye svAhA somAya prajApataya ity api ||
(AVParis_38,2.5)     bR^ihaspate ati yad idaM viShNur itIti ca | mAnastokena gAyatryA etaish ca juhuyAt tataH ||
(AVParis_38,2.6)     praNavena praNavenaiva pibec ca praNavena tu | hotavyaM praNavenaiva pibec ca praNavena tu ||

(AVParis_38,3.1)     madhyamena palAshasya padmapattreNa vA pibet | api vA tAmrapAtreNa hutasheShaM vishuddhaye ||
(AVParis_38,3.2)     yat tvagasthigataM pApaM dehe tiShThati dehinAm | brahmakUrco dahet sarvaM pradIpto 'gnir ivendhanam ||
(AVParis_38,3.3)     trayodashyAdicaturShu triHsnAnAkShArabhojanam | paJNcadashyAM paJNcagavyaM sopavAsaM mahAphalam ||
(AVParis_38,3.4)     abhojyAbhakShyashUdrAnnabhakShaNe vedavikraye | pratigrahe kAlamantrahIne home dyumaithune ||
(AVParis_38,3.5)     bAlatve yat kR^itaM caiva yuvA vR^iddhavayAs tathA | mAtApitR^ikR^itaM caiva tat kShaNAd eva nirdahet ||
(AVParis_38,3.6)     mAsemAse prayuJNjAnodevalokam avApnuyAt | ardhamAseardhamAse ca R^iShINAM lokam uttamam ||
(AVParis_38,3.7)     ShaDrAtre caiva ShaDrAtre brahmalokam anAmayam | aharahaH prayuJNjAnaH paraM brahmAdhigacchati ||
(AVParis_38,3.8)     anena vidhinaiveShTvA devatarpaNapUrvakam | brahmaNA nirmitaM hy etat pavitraM paramaM hitam ||

(ParishiShTa_41. saMdhyopAsanavidhiH)

(AVParis_41,1.1)     om athAtaH saMdhyopAsanavidhiM vyAkhyAsyAmaH ||

(AVParis_41,1.3)     suprakShAlitapANipAdavadanaH prAg vIrAsanenopavishya jIvA sthety AcamyApo hi ShThety abhyukShya prANAyAmAn kR^itvAcamyottiShThan dakShiNahastasthA Apo ayojAlA ity apa utsR^ijed bahudhA ||
(AVParis_41,1.4)     hariH suparNa iti prAtar

(AVParis_41,2.1)     athordhvajAnur AsIna iti vIrAsanI

(AVParis_41,2.5)     gAyatraM chandaH savitA devatA vishvAmitra R^iShir

(AVParis_41,2.13)     sahasrakR^itvaH prayuktAgniShTomAptoryAmAdInAM kratUnAM phalam avApnoti ||

(AVParis_41,3.1)     ato yathAkAmaM japitvA pashyema sharadaH shatam indra jIvety AshiShaH prArthayate ||
(AVParis_41,3.2)     stutA mayA varadeti visR^ijyodIrANA uta sUryasyAvR^itam asapatnaM purastAd yasmAt koshAd iti yathArtham upatiShThate ||
(AVParis_41,3.3)     ya imAM na vindanti nAdhIyate saMdhyAkAle nopAsate te hy ashrotriyA bhavanty anupanItAH kriyAhInAsh chedanabhedanabhojanamaithunAny abhicarantaH ||
(AVParis_41,3.4)     saMdhyAkAle hy ajapantaH shvasUkarasR^igAlakukkuTasarpayoniShu varShasahasrANi jAyante ||
(AVParis_41,3.5)     samAs tasyaivopajAyante ||

(AVParis_41,3.8)     sAyaM saMdhyAm upAsIta kR^itavIrAsano dvijaH | kR^itottAnas tathA prAtaH prAJNjaliH susamAhitaH ||
(AVParis_41,3.9)     etad vIrAsanaM sthAnaM brahmaNA nirmitaM purA | dvijAnaM bAlavR^iddhAnAM purashcaraNam uttamam ||
(AVParis_41,3.10)     sAyaM prAtas tu yaH saMdhyAm askannAm upatiShThate | sa tayA pAvito devyA brAhmahaH pUtakilbiShaH ||
(AVParis_41,3.11)     na sIdet pratigR^ihNAnaH pR^ithvIm api sasAgarAm | ye cAsya viShamAH ke cid divi sUryAdayo grahAH ||
(AVParis_41,3.12)     te cAsya saumyA jAyante shivAH sukhakarAH sadA | sthAnaM vIrAsanaM caeShAM pR^ithivI ca pradakShiNA | agnihotraM hutaM caiShAM ye vai saMdhyAm upAsate ||

(AVParis_41,4.1)     ardhAstamita Aditye ardhodite divAkare | gAyatryAs tatra sAMnidhyaM saMdhyAkAlaH sa ucyate ||
(AVParis_41,4.2)     bhUmyAdityAntaraM yas tu chAdayec caturaN^gulam | tAM tu saMdhyAM parAM vidyAc chAyAsaMbhedane pare ||

(AVParis_41,5.6)     akSharadaivataM vyAkhyAsyAmaH

(ParishiShTa_42. snAnavidhiH)

(AVParis_42,1.1)     atha snAnavidhiM puNyaM vakShyamANaM nibodhata | yena snAtA divaM lokaM prApnuvanti dvijottamAH ||
(AVParis_42,1.2)     saritsu vA taDAge vA devakhAte hrade 'pi vA | gartaprasravaNe vApi puNyaM snAnaM samAcaret ||
(AVParis_42,1.3)     pArakye tu tADAge hi snAnaM naiva vidhIyate | taDAgakartur duShkR^itair lipyate snAnam AcAran ||
(AVParis_42,1.4)     saritAM sarasAM caiva aprAptau nirjharasya ca | uddhR^itya caturaH piNDAn snAyAt tu parakhAtake ||
(AVParis_42,1.5)     anvIkShyamANaH pArshvAni kushahastaH samAhitaH | dvijo madhyaMdinAd arvAg arogI snAnam Acaret ||
(AVParis_42,1.6)     yat te bhUma iti mR^idaM saMgR^ihya rcA samAhitaH | yas te gandha iti tribhir mR^idhir AtmAnam Alabhet ||
(AVParis_42,1.7)     aghadviShTeti sUktena dUrvAM shirasi vinyaset | agramagram ity etayA gomayenAnulepayet ||
(AVParis_42,1.8)     agramagraM carantInAm oShadhInAM vanevane | yan me rogaM ca shokaM ca tan me tvaM nuda gomaya ||
(AVParis_42,1.9)     praNavAdyA vyAhR^itIs tu gAyatrIM ca shiroyutAm | paThet trir anavAnaM hi prANAyAmaH sa ucyate ||
(AVParis_42,1.10)     ambayo yantIty AdIni trINi sUktAni hi kramAt | hiraNyavarNA yad ado vAyoH pUtaH punantu mA ||

(AVParis_42,2.1)     vaishvAnaro rashmibhish ca tathApsu ta iti smR^itam | etaiH saMplAvayet sUktais tato 'ghamarShaNam ||
(AVParis_42,2.2)     apo divyAsh ca saM mAgne idam ApaH shivena mA | yad Apo naktam iti ca etat syAd aghamarShaNam ||
(AVParis_42,2.3)     yad Apo naktaM mithunaM cakAra yad vA dudroha duritaM purANam | hiraNyavarNAs tata ut punantu pra mA muJNcantu varuNasya pAshAt ||
(AVParis_42,2.4)     sarasvatIM gayAM gaN^gAM naimiShaM puShkarANi ca | smR^itvA tIrthAnipuNyAtni avagAhej jalaM tataH ||
(AVParis_42,2.5)     gacchataH snAnakAryAya pitaraH saha daivataiH | pR^iShThataH tv anugacchanti tatsamIpaM jalArthinaH ||
(AVParis_42,2.6)     AshAM tyaktvA nivartante vastraniShpIDanena tu | tasmAn na pIDayed vastram akR^itvA pitR^itarpaNam ||
(AVParis_42,2.7)     utsAhaM varuNaH snAne agnir hotuH shriyaM haret | AyuShyaM bhuJNjato mR^ityus triShu maunam atash caret ||
(AVParis_42,2.8cd)     snAnavastre mR^idas tisraH pradadyAc chuddhihetunA | 8ab | snAtvA paryukShya vAso 'nyac chodhye jaN^ghe mR^idA punaH ||
(AVParis_42,2.9)     vastraniShpIDatoyena apavitrIkR^ite hi te | uttirya vastraM niShpIDya japed AdhyAtmikAni tu ||
(AVParis_42,2.10)     adhyAtmam asyavAmIyaM kautsaM kauShmANDikaM tathA | japtvAtharvashirash caiva bhavAsharvIyam eva ca ||
(AVParis_42,2.11)     prANAsh ca bhagavAn kAlaH puruSho manyur eva ca | ucchiShTo rohito vrAtya etAny AdhyAtmikAni tu ||
(AVParis_42,2.12)     saMvatsareNa yat pApaM kR^itaM ghoram avistaram | japtvaitAni tataH pApAn mucyate nAtra saMshayaH ||
(AVParis_42,2.13)     viShAsahiM manasA hi japtvA gAyatrIM ca tathA tridivaM prAyAti | paribhraShTas tridivAt tapaHkShaye jAtismaratvaM punar eva vindate ||

(ParishiShTa_47. varNapaTalam)

(AVParis_47,1.1)     oM varNAn pUrvaM vyAkhyAsyAmaH prAkR^itA ye ca vaikR^itAH | shrutinirvacanAt sarve vivadante vivR^ittiShu ||
(AVParis_47,1.2)     vR^ittiH karaNaM varNAnAM karNayos tu shrutir yathA | shrutipradeshAd vimatas tad yathA varNa ucyate ||
(AVParis_47,1.3)     samAnasaMdhyakSharANi sparshA antaHsthA UShmANaH | etair anye na dR^ishyante etAvAn varNasaMcayaH ||
(AVParis_47,1.4)     [yeShAM ca shrutisaMhitAyAM vibhAge asadR^ishI syAt || tAn eva varnAn virudrAdaye ca pradise kR^itaH] ||
(AVParis_47,1.5)     ye varNAbhyAM shrUyante ca yeShAM nAsti vibhAgataH | mAnasAMsh cApi saMgrAhyAn upadeshena vartayet ||
(AVParis_47,1.6)     krAntAn bahir nidhAnasya yamAMsh cAnanunAsikAn | savyAkShepaM tato varNAn upadeshena vartayet ||
(AVParis_47,1.7)     iti varNAH svarAH proktAs teShAm AdyAsh caturdasha | samAnAkSharANy ucyante sheShaH saMdhyakSharANi tu ||
(AVParis_47,1.8)     anavarNasvaro nAmi kAdayo vyaJNjanaM smR^itam | paJNcaviMshatir AdyaiShAM sparshA vargAsh ca paJNcakAH ||
(AVParis_47,1.9)     catvAro yAdayo 'ntaHsthAH shAdir UShmAShTako gaNaH | ayogavAhA vartante teShAm AdyAH pR^ithagvidhAH ||
(AVParis_47,1.10)     visarjanIyo 'nusvAro jigvAmUlIya [ity adhaH] | upadhmAnIya ity ete catvAro 'tha pare yamAH ||
(AVParis_47,1.11)     nAsikyAbhinidhAnau ca vidyate yena pUraNam | paJNcaShaShTir iyAn vAco rAshir yo vedalokayoH ||
(AVParis_47,1.12)     mukhanAsike ye varNA ucyante te 'nunAsikAH | samAnAsyaprayatnA ye te savarNA iti smR^itAH ||
(AVParis_47,1.13)     hrasvo 'varNaparas tasya savarNasya ca vAcakaH | hrasvottaras tu dIrgho 'pi tasmAt tasmAt tasyaiva vAcakaH ||
(AVParis_47,1.14)     vargAntaras tu vargAdir vargasya grAhako mataH | vargANAM ca yathAsaMkhyaM prathamAditvam iShyate ||

(ParishiShTa_49. caraNavyUhaH)

(AVParis_49,1.1)     om athAtash caraNavyUhaM vyAkhyAsyAmaH ||
(AVParis_49,1.2)     tatra catvAro vedA bhavanti | R^igvedo yajurvedaH sAmavedo brahmavedash ceti ||
(AVParis_49,1.3)     tatra R^igvedasyArthashAstram upavedaH | yajurvedasya dhanurvedopavedaH | sAmavedasya gAndharvavedopavedaH | brahmavedasyAyurvedopavedaH | abhicArakArthashAstram ity ucyate ||
(AVParis_49,1.4)     R^igveda Atreyasagotro 'gnir devatA | yajurvedaH kAshyapasagotro vAyur devatA | sAmavedo bhAradvAjasagotro viShNur devatA | brahmavedo vaitAyanasagotro brahmA devatA ||
(AVParis_49,1.5)     athAta R^igvedaH pItavarNaH padmapattrAkShaH suvibhaktagrIvaH kuJNcitakeshashmashruH supratiShThitajAnujaN^ghaH | pramANena sa vitastayaH paJNca ||
(AVParis_49,1.6)     tatra R^igvedasya sapta shAkhA bhavanti | tad yathA | AshvalAyanAH | shAN^khAyanAH | sAdhyAyanAH | shAkalAH | bAShkalAH | audumbarAH | mANDUkAsh ceti ||
(AVParis_49,1.7)     teShAm adhyayanam | R^icAM dasha sahasrANi R^icAM paJNca shatAni ca | R^icAm ashItiH pAdash ca etat pAraNam ucyate ||

(AVParis_49,2.1)     tatra yajurvedasya caturviMshatir bhedA bhavanti || tad yathA | kANvAH | mAdhyaMdinAH | jAbAlAH | shApeyAH | shvetAH | shvetatarAH | tAmrAyaNIyAH | paurNavatsAH | AvaTikAH | paramAvaTikAH | hauShyAH | dhauShyAH | khADikAH | AhvarakAH | carakAH maitrAH | maitrAyaNIyAH | hAritakarNAH | shAlAyanIyAH | marcakaThAH | prAcyakaThAH | kapiShThalakaThAH | upalAH | taittirIyAsh ceti ||
(AVParis_49,2.2)     teShAm adhyayanam | dve sahasre shate nyUne vede vAjasaneyake | sakalaM parisaMkhyAtaM brAhmaNaM tu caturguNam ||
(AVParis_49,2.3)     aShTAdasha shatAni bhavanti | tAny eva triguNam adhItya kramapAro bhavati | saptasu vIrAsh ceti ||

(AVParis_49,4.1)     tatra brahmavedasya nava bhedA bhavanti | tad yathA | paippalAdAH | staudAH | maudAH | shaunakIyAH | jAjalAH | jaladAH | brahmavadAH | devadarshAH | cAraNavaidyAsh ceti |

(AVParis_49,4.4)     tatra brahmavedasyAShTAviMshatir upaniShado bhavanti | muNDakA prashnakA brahmavidyA kShurikA cUlikA atharvashiro atharvashikhA garbhopaniShan mahopaniShad brahmopaniShat prANAgnihotraM mANDukyaM nAdabindu brahmabindu amR^itabindu dhyAnabindu tejobindu yogashikhA yogatattvaM nIlarudraH paJNcatApinI ekadaNDI saMnyAsavidhiH aruNiH haMsaH paramahaMsaH nArAyaNopaniShad vaitathyaM ceti ||

(AVParis_49,4.9)     tatra dvAsaptatiH parishiShTAni bhavanti kaushikoktAni | kR^ittikArohiNI | rAShTrasaMvargaH | rAjaprathamAbhiShekaH | purohitakarmANi | puShyAbhiShekaH | piShTarAtryAH kalpaH | ArAtrikam | ghR^itAvekShaNam | tiladhenuH | bhUmidAnam | tulApuruShaH | AdityamaNDakaH | hiraNyagarbhaH | hastirathaH | ashvarathaH | gosahasradAnam | hastidIkShA | ashvadIkShA | vR^iShotsargaH | indrotsavaH | brahmayAgaH | skandayAgAH | saMbhAralakShaNam | araNilakShaNam | yaj~napAtralakShaNam | vedilakShaNam | kuNDalakShaNam | samillakShaNam | sruvalakShaNam | hastalakShaNam | jvAlAlakShaNam | lakShahomaH | kAN^kAyanokto bR^ihallakShahomaH | koTihomaH | gaNamAlA | ghR^itakambalam | anulomakalpaH | AsurIkalpaH | ucchuShmakalpaH | samuccayaprAyashcittAni | brahmakUrcavidhiH | paiThInasitaDAgavidhiH | pAshupatavratavidhiH | saMdhyopAsanavidhiH | snAnavidhiH | tarpaNavidhiH | shrAddhavidhiH | agnihotravidhiH | uttamapaTalam | varNapaTalam | nighaNtuH | caraNavyUhaH | candraprAtipadikam | grahayuddham | grahasaMgrahaH | rAhucAraH | ketucAraH | R^ituketulakShaNam | kUrmavibhAgaH | maNDalAni | digdAhalakShaNam | ulkAlakShaNam | vidyullakShaNam | nirghAtalakShaNam | pariveShalakShaNam | bhUmikampalakShaNam | nakShatragrahotpAtalakShaNam | utpAtalakShaNam | sadyovR^iShTilakShaNam | goshAntiH | adbhutashAntiH | svapnAdhyAyaH | atharvahR^idayam | bhArgavIyagArgyabArhaspatyoshanasAdbhutAni | mahAdbhutAni bR^ihatsarvAnukramaNI ceti ||
(AVParis_49,4.10)     tatra paJNcadashopaniShado bhavanti | muNDakA | prashnakA | brahmavidyA | kShurikA | cUlikA | atharvashiraH | atharvashikhA | garbhopaniShat | mahopaniShat | brahmopaniShat | prANAgnihotram | mANDUkyam | vaitathyam | advaitam | alAtashAntish ceti ||
(AVParis_49,4.11)     tatra brahmavede 'ShTAdasha vratAni cariShyan sAvitrIvratam | vedavratam | vedottaravratam | mailavratam | mailottaravratam | mR^igAravratam | rohitavratam | viShAsahivratam | yamavratam | shAntivratam | shikhivratam | gaNavratam | shirovratam | shikhAvratam | marudvratam | adhivratam | aN^girovratam | pAshupatavrataM caret ||

(AVParis_49,5.1)     yo vai brahmavedeShUpanItaH sa sarvavedeShUpanito
(AVParis_49,5.2)     yo vai brahmavedeShv anupanItaH sa sarvavedeShv anupanItaH ||

(ParishiShTa_51. grahayuddham)

(AVParis_51,1.1)     oM ke cid grahA nArarAn Ashrayante ke cid grahA [jyotiShi] saMgrahe ca | graho graheNaiva hataH kathaM syAd vij~nAya tattvaM bhagavAn bravItu ||
(AVParis_51,1.2)     evaM sa pR^iShTo munibhir mahAtmA provAca gargo grahayuddhatantram | parAjayaM caiva jayaM ca teShAM shubhAsubham(ashubham¤) caiva jagaddhitAya ||

(AVParis_51,1.5)     yasmin deshe tu yo jAtaH sa grahaH pIDyate yadA taM deshaM ghAtitaM vidyAd durbhikSheNa bhayena vA ||

(AVParis_51,2.1)     divAkarash caiva shanaishcaras tathA bR^ihaspatish caiva budhash ca nAgarAH | prajApatiH ketur athApi candramAs tathaiva rAhUshanasau ca yAyinaH ||
(AVParis_51,2.2)     yadA graho nagara eva nAgaraM vijeShyate yAyy atha vApi yAyinam | tadA nR^ipo nAgara eva nAgaraM vijeShyate vAyy atha vApi yAyinam ||
(AVParis_51,2.3)     ArohaNaM ca bhedash ca lekhanaM savyadakShiNam | rashmisaMsarjanaM caiva grahayuddhaM caturvidham ||
(AVParis_51,2.4)     prasavye vigrahaM brUyAt saMgrAmaM rashmisaMgame | lekhane 'mAtyapUDA syAd bhedane tu janakShayaH ||
(AVParis_51,2.5)     sarveShAM nabhasi samAgame grahANAm uktR^iShTo bhavati tathaiva rashmivAn yaH | snigdhatvaM bhavati tu yasya [sa graho graheNa] saMyukto bhavati [tu yaH] parAjayeta sheShaH ||

(AVParis_51,3.1)     shyAmo vA vyapagatarashmimaNDalo vA rUkSho vA vyapagatarashmivAn kR^isho vA | AkrAnto vinipatitas tato 'pasavyo vij~neyo hata iti sa graho graheNa ||
(AVParis_51,3.2)     budhash ca bhaumaH shanibhArgavAN^girAH pradakShiNaM yAti yadA nishAkaram | anamayatvaM triShu saukhyam uttamaM viparyaye cApi mahA¤ janakShayaH ||
