(AVParis_51,3.5)     parasparaM virudhyante kShudbhayaM cApi dAruNAm | anAvR^iShTibhayaM ghoraM vidyAt somaviparyaye ||

(AVParis_51,4.1)     traigartAH kShitipatayaH sayodhamukhyAH pIDyante girinilayAgnijIvinash ca | saMgrAmAH sarudhirapAMsuvarShamishrA durbhikShaM bhavati dharAsutasya ghAte ||
(AVParis_51,4.2)     sAgaranilayAH paurAH kShayam upayAnti narA vaNikpradhAnAH | bhavati tu [rAjA] vijayI prayAyI budhabandhane prapatanti cAtra sobhyAH ||
(AVParis_51,4.3)     daivaj~nAs tapasi ciraM sunishcitArthAH syur dAntA nR^ipatigaNaH purohitAsh ca | Agantur jayati vadhash ca nAgarANAM trailokyam <ca> bhayam upaiti guros tu ghAte ||
(AVParis_51,4.4)     yo rAjA prathitaparAkramaH pR^ithivyAM vaN^gAN^gAdiShu madadhAH sashUrasenAH | ye yodhAH samaraNabhumilabdhashabdAs te sainyaiH kShayam upayAnti shukraghAte ||

(AVParis_52,10.1)     prabhAsash candrabhAsash ca tathAgastyaH pratApavAn | dR^iDhavratas trishaN^kush ca ajau vaishvAnare mR^iDaH ||

(ParishiShTa_53. rAhucAraH)

(AVParis_53,1.1)     om upetya yash candramasaM raviM vA gR^ihNAti sUnor asurasya putraH | nibodhataitasya shubhAshubhAni grahasya mR^ityoH praticeShTitAni ||
(AVParis_53,1.2)     yadA tu rAhuH shashino raver <vA> [grahe] grahItukAmo bhavati prasahya | tadA karoty adbhutadarshanAni yair j~nAyate rAhur upaiShyatIti ||

(AVParis_53,1.5)     saMdhyayor ubhayosh colkA gavAM prakShIyate payaH | kShIriNAm aiva vR^ikShANAM tad ahar nashyate payaH ||

(AVParis_53,2.1)     apsu snigdhAni dR^ishyante kAkAbadhnanti maNDalam | UrdhvaM vadati gomAyur yadA rAhuH pradR^ishyate ||

(AVParis_53,2.3)     udito gR^ihyamANas tu hanti vedavido janAn | bAlAMsh ca jaTilAn hanti ye ca kAShAyavAsasaH ||
(AVParis_53,2.4)     yauvanasthAMsh ca pUrvAhNe hanti yaj~navido janAn | audakAni ca sarvANi nAgendrAsh cAtra duHkhitAH ||
(AVParis_53,2.5)     atha madhyapathaM prAptaH shUdrAn hanti ca taskarAn | parivR^ikto nR^ipaM hanti candrash caraNacAraNAn ||

(AVParis_53,3.1)     pralambaH pramadAn hanti kShatraM rAShTraM ca sarvashaH | traigartAsh cAtra pIDyante ye ca daNDabhR^ito janAH ||
(AVParis_53,3.2)     uparakto yadodeti yadA vA pratitiShThati | ayogakShemam Adishyet triShu lokeShu dAruNam ||
(AVParis_53,3.3)     shAradaM trINi varShANi sasyaM jAtaM na pacyate | naidAghenAtra jIvanti prajA mUlaphalena vA ||
(AVParis_53,3.4)     sarvaM saMgrasate jyotish ciram antardadhAti vA | hanti sphItAni rAShTrANi pradhAnaM ca mahIpatim ||
(AVParis_53,3.5)     yadi <tu> rAhur ubhau shashibhAskarau grasati pakSham anantaram antataH | puruShashoNitakardamavAhinI bhavati bhUr na ca varShati mAdhavaH ||

(AVParis_53,4.1)     gR^ihItvA bhAskaraM pUrvaM gR^ihNAti shashinaM yadi | taM tu somottaraM nAshas tatra rdhyante hi devatAH ||
(AVParis_53,4.2)     vayasAM maraNaM chidre prakIrNe rakShasAM vadhaH | nAgAnAM tu mahAnAge chidre devo na varShati ||
(AVParis_53,4.3)     shveto varNo brAhmaNAnAM kShatriyANAM tu lohitaH | vaishyAnAM pItako varNaH shUdrANAM kR^iShNa ucyate ||
(AVParis_53,4.4)     eteShAM yena varNena rAhush carati bhAskare | yA jAtis tasya varNasya tAM sa pIDayate grahaH ||
(AVParis_53,4.5)     shyAmo bhavati vAtAya draukSho bhavati vR^iShTaye | haridraH sarvadhAnyAnAM kopaM sR^ijati dAruNam ||

(AVParis_53,5.1)     tAmro bhavati shastrAya shastrAya rUkSho bhavati mR^ityave | bahvAkAras tu bhUtAnAM ghoraM janayate jvaram ||
(AVParis_53,5.2)     dhUmavarNo 'gnivarNo vA grAmeShu nagareShu vA | agnyutpAtAn gR^ihasthAnAM karotIha mahAgrahaH ||
(AVParis_53,5.3)     nIlalohitaparyanto rAhush carati bhAskare | amAtyo hanti rAjAnaM rAjA vAmAtyam Atmaha ||
(AVParis_53,5.4)     yasya rAj~nash ca nakShatre svarbhAnur uparajyati | rAjyabhraMshaM suhR^innAshaM maraNaM cAtra nirdishet ||

(ParishiShTa_57. maNDalAni)

(AVParis_57,1.1)     vishAkhe kR^ittikAH puShyaH pUrvau proShThapadau tathA | bharaNyash ca maghAsh caiva phalgunyau prathame tathA ||
(AVParis_57,1.2)     yady atra calate bhUmir nirghAtolkAsta eva vA | asharIrAsh ca nardante kampante daivatAni ca ||
(AVParis_57,1.3)     Adityo vAtra gR^ihyeta somo vApy uparajyate | AgneyaM tad vijAnIyAd durbhikShaM cAtra nirdishet ||
(AVParis_57,1.4)     alpakShIrAs tathA gAvo agner vyAdhish ca jAyate | purANi deshA grAmAsh ca pIDyante hy agninA tadA ||
(AVParis_57,1.5)     pIDyante cAgnikarmANo agniveshAsh ca ye narAH | pittajvaras tathA shvAsaha prajAH pIDayate tadA ||
(AVParis_57,1.6)     akShirogAs tathA ghorAH puruShANAM visheShataH | ApagAsh cAtra shuShyanti na ca sasyavatI mahI ||
(AVParis_57,1.7)     tapyate ca tadA bhUmir na ca devo 'bhivarShati | nIlalohitaparyaktA aphalAH pAdapAs tathA ||
(AVParis_57,1.8)     durbhikShaM marako vyAdhiH paracakrabhayaM tathA | etai rUpais tu vij~neyam AgneyaM caladarshanam ||

(AVParis_57,2.1)     hasto 'shvinyau tathA citrA R^ikSham aryamadaivatam | brAhmaM mR^igashiraH svAtir vAyavyaM maNDalaM smR^itam ||
(AVParis_57,2.2)     yady atra calate bhUmir nirghAtolkAsta eva vA | asharIrAsh ca nardante kampante daivatAni ca ||
(AVParis_57,2.3)     Adityo vAtra gR^ihyeta somo vApy uparajyate | vAyavyaM tad vijAnIyAd akShemaM cAtra nirdishet ||
(AVParis_57,2.4)     pAMsuvarShaM tadA ghoraM kShIre sarpir na vidyate | prAsAdatoraNAdIni prapatanti mahItale ||
(AVParis_57,2.5)     madrakA yavanAsh caiva shakAH kAmbojabAlhikAH | gandhArAsh ca vinashyanti etaiH sArdhaM tathA kila ||
(AVParis_57,2.6)     gajA vAjina uShTrAsh ca vR^ikA nakulaceTakAH | pIDyante vyAdhinA sarve ye ca shastropajIvinaH ||
(AVParis_57,2.7)     pure shreShThA vinashyanti gaNeShu guNasaMmitAH | gR^ihANi ramaNIyAni vishIryante ca sarvashaH ||
(AVParis_57,2.8)     AyAsash colbaNas tatra shastrabhrAmaH samantataH | etai rUpais tu vij~neyaM vAyavyaM caladarshanam ||

(AVParis_57,3.1)     ArdrAshleShAs tathA mUlan pUrvAShADhAs tathaiva ca | vAruNaM revatI caiva sUryadaivatyam eva ca ||
(AVParis_57,3.2)     yady atra calate bhUmir nirghAtolkAsta eva vA | asharIrAsh ca nardante kampante daivatAni ca ||
(AVParis_57,3.3)     Adityo vAtra gR^ihyeta somo vApy uparajyate | vAruNaM tad vijAnIyAt subhikShaM cAtra nirdishet ||
(AVParis_57,3.4)     bahukShIrAs tathA gAvo nAgAsh ca phalinas tathA | shAntArayaH prajAH sarvA gomino jaN^galaM payaH ||
(AVParis_57,3.5)     jalopajIvinaH sarve prApnuvanty R^iddhim uttamAm | khecarAsh cAtra dR^ishyante snigdhavarNAH samantataH ||
(AVParis_57,3.6)     nyastashastrAsh ca rAjAno brahmakShatraM ca vardhate | etai rUpais tu vij~neyaM vAruNaM caladarshanam ||

(AVParis_57,4.1)     jyeShThAnurAdhA shravaNaH shraviShThAsh ca punarvasU | prAjApatyam AShADhAsh ca mAhendraM maNDalaM smR^itam ||
(AVParis_57,4.2)     yady atra calate bhUmir nirghAtolkAsta eva vA | asharIrAsh ca nardante kampante daivatAni ca ||
(AVParis_57,4.3)     Adityo vAtra gR^ihyeta somo vApy uparajyate | mAhendraM tad vijAnIyAt sukShemaM cAtra nirdishet ||
(AVParis_57,4.4)     gAvaH samagravatsAsh ca striyaH putrasamanvitAH | kITA vyAlA mriyante ca ye cAnye svedajantavaH ||
(AVParis_57,4.5)     vedAdhyayanayaj~neShu brAhmaNA niratAH sadA | viTkShatriyAH svakarmANaH shUdrAH shushrUShakArakAH ||
(AVParis_57,4.6)     viMshatishataM tv AgneyaM vAyavyaM navatiM calet | ashItiM calate tv aindraM vAruNaM saptatiM calet ||
(AVParis_57,4.7)     Agneyo bhUmikampo yaH sa dvimAsAd vipacyate | vAruNas tu phalaM sadyo vAyavyas tu trimAsikaH || mAhendrasya phalaM vidyAn mAsam ardhaM tathaiva ca ||

______________________________________________________________________


(ParishiShTa_58. digdAhalakShaNam)

(AVParis_58,1.1)     om ata UrdhvaM ca digdAhAn kIrtyamAnAn nibodhata | yathA dishaH pradahyante tAsAM dAhaphalaM ca yat ||
(AVParis_58,1.2)     indro 'gnir marutash caiva pradahanti disho dasha | shubhAshubhAya lokAnAM kR^itAntenAbhicoditAH ||
(AVParis_58,1.3)     yadAstamita Aditye vahner jvAlA pradR^ishyate. dishAM dAhaM tu tad vidyAd bhArgavasya vaco yathA ||
(AVParis_58,1.4)     nAnArAgasamutthAnAM nAnAvidhaphalodayAH | pAMshuneva ca saMchannA digdAhAyogam AshritAH ||
(AVParis_58,1.5)     dishaH sarvAH pradahyante akShemAya phalAya ca | avadAhAd R^ite dAhaM yadi snigdhAH pradarshanAH ||
(AVParis_58,1.6)     tamodhUmarajaskA ye dIptadvijamR^igAvR^itAH | pradIptalakShaNAH satyAH sarva evAhitAvahAH ||
(AVParis_58,1.7)     tathA kanakakiMjalkataDitkalpAH shivAsh ca ye | rUkShAH kR^iShNAtha mAJNjiShThA bandhujIvakavac ca ye ||
(AVParis_58,1.8)     shvetA raktAsh ca pItAsh ca dAhAH kR^iShNAsh ca varNataH | brahmakShatriyaviTshUdravinAshAya prakIrtitAH ||
(AVParis_58,1.9)     raktAH shastrabhayaM kuryur pItA vyAdhiprakopanAH | agnivarNAs tathA kuryur agnishastrabhayaM mahat ||
(AVParis_58,1.10)     sapItaparuShashyAmA ye ca vAruNasaMnibhAH | sarva eva kShudhArogamR^ityushastrAgnikopanAH ||
(AVParis_58,1.11)     R^itau tu varShaM tIvraM syAt sainyavidravam eva ca | bhR^isham uddyotanI saMdhyA kurute vA grahAgamam ||
(AVParis_58,1.12)     dikShu dagdhAsu pIDyante yathAdig deshabhaktayaH | shakunaj~nAnanirdiShTA ye ca tatrAdhikArakAH ||
(AVParis_58,1.13)     yathoktA tu mahAshAntir yathoktavidhinA kR^itA | sarvaM digdAhajaM ghoraM shamayet sA sadakShiNA ||

(ParishiShTa_58b. ulkAlakShaNam)

(AVParis_58b,1.1)     om ulkAdayo hi nirdiShTA nirghAtAs tu purAtra ye | teShAm idAnIM vakShyAmi visheShAMs tu pR^ithakpR^ithak ||
(AVParis_58b,1.2)     aN^gAnAm AntarikShANAM yad aN^gam abhipUjitam | tad ulkAlakShaNaM shrImad aN^gaM kArtsnyena vakShyate ||
(AVParis_58b,1.3)     apradhR^iShyANi yAni syuH sharIrANIndriyair dR^iDhaiH | kShamAvanti vishuddhAni satyavratarAtAni ca ||
(AVParis_58b,1.4)     tAny etAni prakAshante bhAbhir vitimiraM nabhaH | samantAj jvalayantIha yasmAd asukaraM nabhaH ||
(AVParis_58b,1.5)     tAni bhAvakShayAd bhUyaH pracyutAni nabhastalAt | kShitau salakShaNAny eva nipatantIha bhArgava
(AVParis_58b,1.6)     teShAM nipatatAM tatra yatrayatropalakShyate | tatratatraiva vividhaM prajAnAM jAyate bhayam ||
(AVParis_58b,1.7)     rUpavarNaprabhAsnehapramaNAkR^itisaMgamaiH | teShAM balAbalaM j~nAtvA guNadoShaH pravakShyate ||
(AVParis_58b,1.8)     tArA dhiShNyAs tatholkAsh ca vidyuto 'shanayas tathA | vikalpAH paJNcadhA caiShAM parasparabalottarAH ||
(AVParis_58b,1.9)     tatra shabdenba mahatA visvareNa vikarShiNA | mahAcakram ivAgacchad AyatAkShA nabhastalAt ||
(AVParis_58b,1.10)     manuShyamR^igahastyashvavR^ikShAshmapathaveshmasu | patanty ashanayo dIptAH sphoTayantyo dharAtalam ||

(AVParis_58b,2.1)     sahasaivopapanneShu bhR^ishaM tadanuyAyinA | sattvavibhraMshinAtyarthaM shabdenodvegakAriNA ||
(AVParis_58b,2.2)     jvAlAbhAravisarpiNyaH prakR^ityA duHkhadarshanAH | vidyuto nipatanty Ashu jIveShu vanarAshiShu ||
(AVParis_58b,2.3)     tIkShNashUlavishAlAgrA patantI cApi vardhate | prakR^ityA pauruShI tUlkA tasyA bhedAn nibodhata ||
(AVParis_58b,2.4)     kR^ishA nArIva dIptA syAc chikhA sAN^gAravarShiNI | uddyotayantI gaganaM kAJNcanenaiva varmaNA ||
(AVParis_58b,2.5)     pItena pANDunA vApi dhUmadhUmAruNena vA | vishIryatA mahAbhreNa mahatA cAnuShaN^giNA ||
(AVParis_58b,2.6)     vaMshagulmanibhAsh cApi kAsh cid indradhvajopamAH | kAsh cid indrAyudhaprakhyAH kAsh cin maNDalasaMsthitAH ||
(AVParis_58b,2.7)     chattravac cApu dR^ishyante cakravan nipatanti ca | daNDavac cApi tiShThanti pradhAvanti ca sarpavat ||
(AVParis_58b,2.8)     prakIrNena kalApena khe gacchantIva barhiNaH | abhyucchritena pucchena yAti kA cid dharAtalam ||
(AVParis_58b,2.9)     tejAMsi vikiranty anyAH pradhAvanti ca golavat ||

(AVParis_58b,3.1)     pranR^ittapretamArjAtavarAhAnugatAs tathA | sasvanA niHsvanAsh cApi patanti dharaNItale ||
(AVParis_58b,3.2)     etAsAM phalam ulkAnAM pravakShyAmi pR^ithakpR^ithak | tantunaiva hi saMbaddhA uhyamAneva vAyunA ||
(AVParis_58b,3.3)     patantI dR^ishyate kA cit kA cid bhramati cAmbare | ulkAsaMghaiH parivR^itA kA cid yAti dharAtalam ||
(AVParis_58b,3.4)     sAmAnyaM tu phalaM tAsAM tat samAsena vakShyate | varAhapretashArdUlasiMhamArjAravArAiH ||
(AVParis_58b,3.5)     tulyA bhayAvahA ulkA nikR^iShTAhinibhA ca yA | shUlapaTTishashaktyR^iShTimudgarAsiparashvadhaiH ||
(AVParis_58b,3.6)     vR^iShTyAkAreNa tulyAsh ca vR^ikShAbhAsh ca vigarhitAH | padmashaN^khenduvajrAhimatsyadhvajanibhAH shubhAH ||
(AVParis_58b,3.7)     shrIvR^ikShasvastikAvArtahaMsadviradavarcasaH | jvalitAN^gArasaMkAshA jihmagA atha shIghragAH ||
(AVParis_58b,3.8)     vinA pucchAvakAshena hrasvenAtikR^ishena vA | dashAntarANi dhanuShaH pucchaM cApi pradR^ishyate ||
(AVParis_58b,3.9)     ulkAvikAro boddhavyo dhiShNya ity abhisaMj~nitaH | yas tu shuklena varNena vapuShA pelavena vA ||
(AVParis_58b,3.10)     padmatantunikAshena dhUmarAjInibhena vA | ulkAvikAraH so 'py uktas tArakA nAmanAmataH ||
(AVParis_58b,3.11)     evaM paJNcavidhA hy etAH shaunakena prakIrtitAH | svargacyutAnAM patatAM lakShaNaM puNyakarmaNAm ||

(AVParis_58b,4.1)     etAsAm indrashirasi patanaM nR^ipater bhayam | devatArcAsu patane rAjarAShTrabhayaM bhavet ||
(AVParis_58b,4.2)     puradvare purakShobha indrakIle janakShayaH | brahmAyatanaghAteShu brAhmaNAnAm upadravaH ||
(AVParis_58b,4.3)     caityavR^ikShAbhighAteShu satkR^ityAnAM mahad bhayam | dvAre cAyuHkShayaM vidyAd gR^ihe tu svAmino bhayam ||
(AVParis_58b,4.4)     goShTheShu gominAM vidyAt karShakANAM khaleShu ca | gR^iheShu rAj~nAM jAnIyAd bheShu tadbhaktinAM bhayam ||
(AVParis_58b,4.5)     AshAgrahopaghAteShu taddeshyAnAM tapasvinAm | adhomukhInR^ipaM hanyAd brAhmaNAn UrdhvagAminI ||
(AVParis_58b,4.6)     tiryaggA rAjapatnIM ca shreShThinaH pratilomanI | vaMshagulmanibhA rAShTraM nR^ipam indradhvajopamA ||
(AVParis_58b,4.7)     gajam indrAyudhaprakhyA puraM maNDalasaMsthitA | mantriNash cakrasaMsthAnA chattrAkArA purodhasam ||
(AVParis_58b,4.8)     mayUrapucchAnugatA kuryAd ulkA jalakShayam | vilIyamAnA nabhasi pibaty ulkA payodharAn ||
(AVParis_58b,4.9)     sphuliN^gAn visR^ijantyo yAH pradhAvanti samantataH | golavac ca pradhAvanti tAsu rAShTrabhayaM bhavet ||
(AVParis_58b,4.10)     ulkAsaMghaiH parivR^itA yAH patanti nabhastalAt | anusAriNya ulkAs tA rAjarAShTrabhayAvahAH ||
(AVParis_58b,4.11)     pretAnugatamArgAsh ca varAhAnugatAsh ca yAH | kravyAgnivyAlarUpAsh ca tA janakShayakArikAH ||
(AVParis_58b,4.12)     kSheveDitAsphoTitotkruShTA gItavAditranisvanAH | ulkApAteShu boddhavyA rAjarAShTrabhayAvahAH ||
(AVParis_58b,4.13)     sasvanA dAruNAH saMdhyAvAyosh ca pratilomagAH | nabho madhyaM ca yA yAnti yAsh ca kuryur gatAgatam ||
(AVParis_58b,4.14)     hinasti shuklA shirasA madhyena kShatajaprabhA | pArshvAbhyAM pItakA hanti kR^iShNolkA pucchayoginI ||
(AVParis_58b,4.15)     shuklA devanR^ipAn hanyAt kShatriyAn kShatajaprabhA | pItA vaishyopaghAtAya shUdrAn hanyAt sitetarA ||
(AVParis_58b,4.16)     patantyo nopalakShyante karma tAsAM prakAshate | kShitAv ashanayo yatra tatra nAsti bhayAgamaH ||
(AVParis_58b,4.17)     satArA nipatanty anyA mArutapratilomagAH | bhavanti vidyuto neShTA iShTAsh ca syur ato 'nyathA ||
(AVParis_58b,4.18)     tArA dhiShNyAsh ca boddhavyAsh cirAn mR^iduphalodayAH | tAsAm api ca bhUyiShThaM patanaM doShakArakam ||
(AVParis_58b,4.19)     yatoyato vikArAH syur nipatanty atimAtrashaH | tatastato nR^ipo yAyAd daivo mArgaH sa ucyate ||
(AVParis_58b,4.20)     nimitteShu mahAshAntim ulkAyAM ca visheShataH | kR^itvA siddhim avApnoti ulkAdoShAc ca mucyate ||

(ParishiShTa_59. vidyullakShaNam)

(AVParis_59,1.1)     ata UrdhvaM pravakShyAmi vidyullakShaNam uttamam | varNarUpavikArAMsh ca deshabhAgA¤ shubhAshubhAn ||
(AVParis_59,1.2)     caturthIM paJNcamIM caiva pratIkSheta sadA shuciH | AShADhashuddhe niyataM vidyuddarshanam adbhutam ||
(AVParis_59,1.3)     ativR^iShTim anAvR^iShTiM bhAvAbhAvau tathaiva ca | sarvasasyeShu niShpattir vidyuto darshane naraH ||
(AVParis_59,1.4)     aindryAM cet syandate vidyud aindrasthash cApi mArutaH | subhikShaM kShemam ArogyaM nirItiM ca vinirdishet ||
(AVParis_59,1.5)     AgneyyAM ced ubhau syAtAM bhayaM shastrAgnivR^iShTihtaH | yAmyAyAM viShamArish ca vyAdhimR^ityubhayaM tathA ||
(AVParis_59,1.6)     kanIyasI tu nairR^ityAM tathA bahvItikA samA | madhyamA sasyasaMpattir vAruNyAM vyAdhisaMkulA ||
(AVParis_59,1.7)     pataMgadaMshamashakA vAyavyAM madhyasapadaH | ativAribhayaM vidyAt saumyAyAM bhUrisaMpadaH ||
(AVParis_59,1.8)     nirItiH sasyasaMpat tu pradhAnAishyAM manoramA | pratilomeShu vAteShu ItibAhulyam Adishet ||
(AVParis_59,1.9)     anulomeShu vAteShu nirItiM tu samAdishet | shubhAyAM syandamAnAyAm aniShTA syandate yadi ||
(AVParis_59,1.10)     saMpadyate mahAsasyAn mahAMsh cet syAd avagrahaH | ashubhA syandate pUrvaM yadi pashcAc ca shobhanA ||
(AVParis_59,1.11)     suvR^iShTim eva tatrAhur na ca sasyaM samR^idhyati | yadA tu sarvAH syandante viShamAM vR^iShTim Adishet ||
(AVParis_59,1.12)     bahulAyAM vidyuti tu bahuvAribhayaM bhavet | savidyutaH sastanito darshayanti yadA shubhAm ||
(AVParis_59,1.13)     pUrvottarAM dishaM meghAH suvR^iShTiM tAM vijAnate | pUrvataH pUrvavarSheShu dR^ishyante yadi toyadAH ||
(AVParis_59,1.14)     pradakShiNAvartashubhAH suvR^iShTim iti nirdishet | AgneyeShv ativR^iShTiH syAt sasyaM cApi vipadyate ||
(AVParis_59,1.15)     viShamA vR^iShTir yAmyeShu vyAdhiM mR^ityuM ca nirdishet | bahvItikA nairR^iteShu samUlaphaladAyinI ||
(AVParis_59,1.16)     vAruNeShu payodeShu madhyamaM sasyam Adishet | vAyavyAM prathamaM varShaM yatra varShati vAsavaH ||
(AVParis_59,1.17)     tatrAtivR^iShTir bhavati svalpabIjAni vApayet | varNasnebhopapannAs tu pUrvavR^iShTyAM payodharAH ||
(AVParis_59,1.18)     saumyAM yatra pravarSheyus tatra sarvavR^iShTyAM payodharAH ||
(AVParis_59,1.19)     ity etat pUrvavarSheShu lakShaNaM vidyutAM sphuTam | varShArAvagataM sarvaM yathAvat parikIrtitam ||
(AVParis_59,1.20)     shubheShv api mahAshAntir avighAtAya vocyate | ashubheShu samarghAya tasmAt sarveShu shAntikam iti ||

______________________________________________________________________


(ParishiShTa_60. nirghAtalakShaNam)

(AVParis_60,1.1)     aShTau bhavanti nirghAtAs teShAm indraH prashasyate | pUrveNa vR^iShTiM sasyaM ca rAjavR^iddhiM ca nirdishet ||
(AVParis_60,1.2)     pUrvottare subhikShaM tu bhUmilAbhas tathottare | aparottare caurabhayaM vAjinAM cApy upadravaH ||
(AVParis_60,1.3)     pashcimAyAM bhayaM rAj~no jalajAtish ca pIDyate | nairR^ite sasyagostrINAM gaNAnAM ca mahad bhayam ||
(AVParis_60,1.4)     dakShiNe rAjapIDA syAd Ayush cAtra vinirdishet | Anartasya bhayaM vidyAd yadi syAt pUrvadakShiNaH ||
(AVParis_60,1.5)     sa yojanaparaH shabdo nirghAtasya vishAmyati | sarvatra ca bhayaM vidyAt tatra yatra vishAmyati ||
(AVParis_60,1.6)     bhaye raudrIM prakurvIta abhayAM vAbhayapradAm | tayA shAmyanti cotpAtAH sukhaM cAtyantikaM bhavet ||

______________________________________________________________________


(ParishiShTa_61. pariveShalakShaNam)

(AVParis_61,1.1)     om athAtaH pariveShANAM lakShaNaM caiva vakShyate | vR^iddhagargo yathA pUrvam uvAca mama suvrata ||
(AVParis_61,1.2)     svAyaMbhuvaniyogena vikAraM kurute 'malaH ||
(AVParis_61,1.3)     shvetaH shyAmo hariH kR^iShNa iti varNA vyavasthitAH | proktA megheShu catvAro vyaktAH snigdhAH supUjitAH ||
(AVParis_61,1.4)     snigdheShu pariveSheShu vaturShv eteShu nArada | saMdhyAyAm atra varNeShu vR^iShTiM teShv abhinirdishet ||
(AVParis_61,1.5)     kAcanIlAJNjanAriShTAshanisarpanibheShu ca | raupyadravasamAbheShu meghas triShv api varShati ||
(AVParis_61,1.6)     nimagnA tu yadA saMdhyA bhavaty etat suvR^iShTaye | ebhyash ca viparItA ye te 'vR^iShTibhayadA ghanAH ||
(AVParis_61,1.7)     varAhair makarair uShTrair vR^ikaiH kaN^kais tathA kharaiH | shashakAkR^itayaH kuryuH saMdhyAyAM jaladA bhayam ||
(AVParis_61,1.8)     hemapAvakavarNAsh ca vipulaM ca janakShayam | shabdaM shvakharagomAyugR^idhravAyasasaMsthitAH ||
(AVParis_61,1.9)     pUrvAparAsu saMdhyAsu saMgrAmaM prAhur unmukhAH | ashvasthA vAraNasthAsh ca yeShu yodhA narA iva ||
(AVParis_61,1.10)     megheShu saMpradR^ishyante ye pAshAN^kushasaMnibhAH | tathA savAraNAsh caiva vinighnantaH parasparam ||
(AVParis_61,1.11)     kravyAdbhir bhakShyamANAsh ca gR^idhragomAyuvAyasaiH | udyudhyante yadA yuktA rAJNjaH saMshayakArakAH ||
(AVParis_61,1.12)     mayUrATTAlapadmendukAshanIlanibhAni tu | saMdhyAsv abhrANi dR^ishyante tIvraM varSham upasthitam ||
(AVParis_61,1.13)     savidyut sadhanuShkash ca saghoShaH shikhisaMnibhaH | saMdhyAsv abhrANi dR^ishyante tIvraM varSham upasthitam ||
(AVParis_61,1.14)     nIlalohitaparyantaM kR^iShNagrIvaM savidyutam | vivarNaM parighaM dR^iShTvA vidyAd udakavAhakam ||
(AVParis_61,1.15)     trivarNe parighe vApi trivarNair vA balAhakaiH | udayAstamayam iyAd yadi sUryaH kadA cana ||
(AVParis_61,1.16)     pR^ithivyAM rAjavaMshyAnAM mahad bhayam upasthitam | lokakShayakaraM vidyAd yadi devo na varShati ||
(AVParis_61,1.17)     matsyarUpI sAdR^ishyena yady uttiShTheta bhAskaraH | sphuTarashmis tadAdityaH sa nirdahati medinIm ||
(AVParis_61,1.18)     etad dR^iShTvA mahad rUpam Aditye samupasthite | vispaShTaM jyotir vispaShTaM sadyovarShasya lakShaNam ||
(AVParis_61,1.19)     grahasaMchAdanaM cApi garjanaM pratigarjanam | paraspareNa kurvanti meghA vegasamIritAH ||
(AVParis_61,1.20)     tasmiMsh caturvidhe yuddhe meghAnAM vyomacArinAm | utpadyante trayo bhAvAs tan me nigadataH shR^iNu ||
(AVParis_61,1.21)     garjamAneShu megheShu vAraNaH pratigarjati | tAM dishaM yojayet snenAM garjanaM yatra mIyate ||
(AVParis_61,1.22)     vidyuto 'bhravikAreShu shakrAyudhanibhAyudhAH | sphoTitAshanighaNTAsh ca yAM dishaM meghavAraNAH ||
(AVParis_61,1.23)     saMghaTTeShu samudbhutAH parasparajighAMsavaH | tAM dishaM yojayet senAM rAjA jayati tAM disham ||
(AVParis_61,1.24)     grahaNAchAdane caiva garjane pratigarjane | evam eva vidhir j~neyaH sarvash caiva vinishcayaH ||
(AVParis_61,1.25)     parimANaM na shakyaM tat samIritum asheShataH | aparAbhravikArANAM ratnAnAm iva sAgare ||
(AVParis_61,1.26)     saMdhyA yojanabhAk proktA stanitaM tu dviyojanam | parighaH paJNcayojanyaH pratyAdityas triyojanaH ||
(AVParis_61,1.27)     nirghAtaH ShaT tathA vidyut pariveSho dviShaDyataH | dAhaM yojanakaM cApi ulkA tv amitabhAginI ||
(AVParis_61,1.28)     dashasaMsthA samAptAni shAyAN^gAni pramANataH | aN^gAni tv AntarikShANi vij~neyAni samAsataH ||

______________________________________________________________________


(ParishiShTa_62. bhUmikampalakShaNam)

(AVParis_62,1.1)     oM catvAro bhumikampAs tu gargaH provAca buddhimAn | agnir vAyus tathApash ca caturthas tv indra ucyate ||
(AVParis_62,1.2)     teShAM rUpaM vikArAMsh ca vyAkhyAsyAmo 'nupUrvashaH | yaj j~nAtvA buddhimAn dhIro nirdished vividhaM phalam ||
(AVParis_62,1.3)     prakampitAyAM bhUmau cet saptAhAbhyantareNA tu | [bhaveyur atra saMgrAmA rAj~nAM mR^ityubhayapradAH ||
(AVParis_62,1.4)     rAj~nAM virodho bhavati maraNAni bhavanti ca |] tAmraH sUryash ca candrash ca pItAsh ca mR^igapakShiNaH ||
(AVParis_62,1.5)     dishaH sarvA bhaveyush ca sUryodayasamaprabhAH | yad etallakShaNopetaM vidyAd agniprakampitam ||
(AVParis_62,1.6)     tasmin bhavati nirdeshaH shaunakasya vaco yathA | hiraNyaM ca suvarNaM ca yac cAnyad vidyate gR^ihe ||
(AVParis_62,1.7)     sarvam etat parityajya kartavyo dhAnyasaMgrahaH | rAShTrANi saMdahed agnir grAmAMsh ca nagarANi ca
(AVParis_62,1.8)     saMgrAmAsh cAtra vartante mAMsashoNitakardamAH | rAjAnash ca virudhyante devash cAtra na varShati ||
(AVParis_62,1.9)     evam etatprakampAnAM garhitam agnikampitam ||

(AVParis_62,2.1)     prakampitAyAM bhUmau ced iti ||
(AVParis_62,2.2)     atipracaNDo bahulo vAyur bhavati dAruNaH | sharkarAkarShaNash cApi dikShu caiva vidikShu ca ||
(AVParis_62,2.3)     tad etallakShaNopetaM vidyAd vAyuprakampitam | shastrair AvaraNaMkuryAt prAkAraM parikhAM tathA ||
(AVParis_62,2.4)     na tadA pravased grAmaM j~nAtvAtmAnaM tu gopayet | saMgrAmAsh cAtra vardhante mAMsashoNitakardamAH ||
(AVParis_62,2.5)     virudhyante ca rAjAno maraNAni bhavanti hi | rAjaputrasahastrANAM bhUmiH pibati shoNitam ||
(AVParis_62,2.6)     mAsaM viMshatirAtraM vA devas tatra na varShati | dvAbhyAM gatAbhyAM mAsAbhyAM paraM syAd bahulaM jalam ||
(AVParis_62,2.7)     daShTaM dUShayate cAtra kShatabaddhAni cAdhikam | eShAm eva tu kampAnAM garhitaM vAyukampitam ||

(AVParis_62,3.1)     prakampitAyAM bhUmau ||
(AVParis_62,3.2)     varShantas tu samAyAnti mahAmeghAH samantataH | nakrAsh ca shishumArAsh ca kUrmA makarasaMsthitAH ||
(AVParis_62,3.3)     abhrAkR^itiShu dR^ishyante grasantash candrabhAskarau | tad etallakShaNopetaM vidyAd ambuprakampitam ||
(AVParis_62,3.4)     parvateShu vaped bIjam UShare jAN^gale tathA | tatroptaM nandate bIjam anyatra bhuvi nashyati ||
(AVParis_62,3.5)     udajAni tu puShpANi mUlAni ca phalAni ca | gacchanti tatra vR^iddhiM ca sattvAny udakajAni ca ||
(AVParis_62,3.6)     [kShemaM subhikSham ArogyaM suvR^iShTiM cAtra nirdishet] ||

(AVParis_62,4.1)     prakampitAyAM bhUmau ||
(AVParis_62,4.2)     gambhIraM garjamAnas tu megha AyAti pArthivaH | snigdho hy aJNjanasaMkAshaH sumahatparvatopamaH ||
(AVParis_62,4.3)     vitrAsayan dishaH sarvA drutaM cApi pravarShati | indrAyudhaM bhavec cAtra vidyut stanitam eva ca ||
(AVParis_62,4.4)     suvR^iShTiM kShemam ArogyaM subhikShaM paramA mudaH | yaj~nodbhavais tu modante Anandair moditAH prajAH ||
(AVParis_62,4.5)     eteShAM bhUmikampAnAM prashastaM hIndrakampanam | jAnIyAl lakShaNair etaiH sarvam eva shubhAshubham ||
(AVParis_62,4.6)     eteShu triShu kampeShu atharvA shAstrakovidaH | mAhendrIm amR^itAM vApi kuryAc chAntiM sadakShiNAm ||
(AVParis_62,4.7)     indrakampe tu vidhivad aindrair mantrair vidhAnavit | tatohalasya pradhAnArthaM juhuyAc ca japet tathA ||

(ParishiShTa_63. nakShatragrahotpAtalakShaNam)

(AVParis_63,1.1)     om atha paraM pravakShyAmi vakShatreShu graheShu ca | pariveShAn bahuvidhAn nAnAvidhaphalodayAn ||
(AVParis_63,1.2)     aindravAruNakauberAn raktapANDuramecakAn | pANDUn babhrUMsh ca pItAMsh cAnIlAnalayamAtmanaH ||
(AVParis_63,1.3)     prAjApatyAMsh ca raudrAMsh ca nairR^ityAMsh cApi bhArgava | harishabalakApotAn pariveShAn uvAca ha ||
(AVParis_63,1.4)     navaite pariveShANAM varNA daivatayonayaH | bahutvam ete gacchanti anyonyaguNasaMshrayAt ||
(AVParis_63,1.5)     gR^ihItvAbhrarajaH sUkShmaM varNayog saMnipatya ca | pitAmahaniyogena mAturo maNDalIkR^itaH ||
(AVParis_63,1.6)     shubhAshubhArthaM lokAnAM jyotImShy avaruNaddhi saH | tasya rUpaM guNaM j~nAtvA guNadoShaH pracakShyate ||
(AVParis_63,1.7)     nakShatratArakANAM ca parato viShayasya ca niviShTo bhAva AgantuM pariveSha iti smR^itaH ||
(AVParis_63,1.8)     dhR^itatIkShNArkakiraNe prasannA mR^idumaNDale | prasnigdhe caikavarNe ca mAMsale vyaktalakShaNe ||
(AVParis_63,1.9)     lohitAkShau kShurakrAnte sarashmau pItamaNDale | A pradoShAd vimadhyAhnAd A nakShatrAntagAmini ||
(AVParis_63,1.10)     sahAbhrabhArastanite pariveShe prakAshini | anR^itAv api jAnIyAn mahad bhayam upasthitam ||

(AVParis_63,2.1)     kR^iShNanIhAratimire prakR^ityAkrAntamaNDale | vikArair nAbhasaiH kIrNe sphuliN^gopacite 'shubhe ||
(AVParis_63,2.2)     viShame vigatasnehe vidhvastakaluShAbhrake | triShu saMdhiShu bhUyiShThaM darshanaM copagacchati ||
(AVParis_63,2.3)     dvitrinakShatrage vApi nakShatrArdhagate 'pi vA | pradIptair vA rasadbhish ca vIkShyamANe mR^igadvijaiH ||
(AVParis_63,2.4)     pariveShe vijAnIyAn nR^ipAdyAnAm upasthitam | saptarAtrAd bhayaM ghoraM caurashastrAgnimR^ityubhiH ||
(AVParis_63,2.5)     dhUmakarburamAJNjiShTharaktapItAsitAkR^itiH | bhavaty ekatare pArshve rUpeNAvilamaNDalaH ||
(AVParis_63,2.6)     tanunA cAtra jAlena samantAt pariveShTitaH | muhurmuhush ca vilayaM saMsthAnaM cApi gacchati ||
(AVParis_63,2.7)     so 'pi vAyvAtmako j~neyo mR^idumandadivAkaraH | pariveSho 'lpaphalado vAtavR^iShTiH pravR^iMhate ||
(AVParis_63,2.8)     atha ced vAtavR^iShTis tu trirAtrAn nApajAyate | jalajvalanacaurANAM prAdurbhAvaH prajAyate ||
(AVParis_63,2.9)     pariveShagato 'lkA syAd dvimaNDalaparigrahe | dvAbhyAM senApatibhayaM yuvarAjabhayaM tribhiH ||

(AVParis_63,3.1)     maNDalaiH purarodhaH syAt tribhir abhyadhikair dhryvan | trANi yatrAvarudhyante nakShatragrahacandramAH ||
(AVParis_63,3.2)     tryahAd varShaM samAcaShTe sa mAsAd vigrahaM vadet | senApatikumArANAM senAyAsh cApi vidravaH ||
(AVParis_63,3.3)     lohitAN^gapariveShe shastrAgnyutpAta eva ca | sthAvarAH karShakAsh cApi kShudradhAnyaM ca pIDyate ||
(AVParis_63,3.4)     vAtavR^iShTiM ca janayet pariviShTaH shanaishcaraH | rAjyam eva hi garbhAMsh ca rAhuH pIDayate dhruvam ||

(AVParis_63,4.1)     rAjapatnIM caturdashyAM pajcadashyAM nR^ipasya ca | purohitAmAtyanR^ipA hanyur anyonyam eva tu ||
(AVParis_63,4.2)     purarodhaM vijAnIyAt pariviShTe bR^ihaspatau | mantriNo lekhakAsh cApi rudhyante sthAvarANi ca ||

(ParishiShTa_64. utpAtalakShaNam)

(AVParis_64,1.1)     oM yAn provAcAN^girAH pUrvaM yAMshca vedo 'shanAH kaviH | tAn ahaM saMpravakShyAmi utpAtAMs trividhAn api ||
(AVParis_64,1.2)     prakR^iter anyathAbhavo yatrayatropajAyate | tatratatra vijAnIyAt sarvam utpAtalakShaNam ||
(AVParis_64,1.3)     pArthivaM cAntarikShaM ca divyaM cotpAtalakShaNam | nakShatropadraveShUktaM yathAvidhi tathaiva tat ||
(AVParis_64,1.4)     teShUtpAtagaNeShu AhU rasAtalasamudbhavAn | nirghAtAn bhUmikampAMsh ca kIrtyamAnAn nibodhata ||
(AVParis_64,1.5)     vAruNAgneyavAyavyAH kampayanti vasuMdharAm | shubhAshubhArthaM lokAnAM rAtrau ahani cakravat ||
(AVParis_64,1.6)     teShAM vakShyAmi kampAnAM lakShaNAni phalAni ca | yatrovAcAushanAH khyAtAn nAradAya sma pR^icchate ||
(AVParis_64,1.7)     saptAhAbhyantare kampe bhaved vajradharAtmake | sasvanair AptaparyantaM svastikAbhraghanair nabhaH ||
(AVParis_64,1.8)     saindracApAyudhA kampAd vidyudgaNagavAkShakaiH | pAshorminagarAkArair naganAganibhair ghanaiH ||
(AVParis_64,1.9)     nabhaso 'ntaM ca sevinyo vidyutaH svArkasaMnibhAH | prAnte susaMvR^itAsh cApi shItAshItAsh ca mArutAH ||
(AVParis_64,1.10)     dhArAN^kuraparisrAvair nIlotpaladalaprabhaiH | svanadbhish chAdyate vyoma kampayed varuNaH svayam ||

(AVParis_64,2.1)     tArApAtair dishaM dAhair ulkApAtaish ca sasvanaiH | hAhAkR^itam ivAbhUti pradIpitapathaM nabhaH ||
(AVParis_64,2.2)     saptAhAbhyantare vApi kShitau vahniH prakupyate | sa Agneyo bhavet kampo rAjarAShtrabhayAvahaH ||
(AVParis_64,2.3)     niHprakAsham ivAkAshe bhAskaro nAtibhAskaraH | dishas tu na prakAshante duHkhAR^itA iva yoShitaH ||
(AVParis_64,2.4)     saghoShA mArutA rUkShA vAnti sharkarakarShiNaH | saptAhAbhyantare kampe mArute 'tibhayAvahe ||
(AVParis_64,2.5)     subhikShakShemadau kampau vij~neyAv aindravAruNau | vAyavyAgneyajau kampau rAjarAShtrabhayAvahau ||
(AVParis_64,2.6)     yasyAM yasyAM dishi dharA virauti vikR^itasvarA | tasyAM tasyAM dishi bhayM sArdhaM syAd adhikAridbhiH ||
(AVParis_64,2.7)     nirghAtA bhUmikampAsh ca sasamAsam udAhR^itAH | ataH paraM pravakShyAmi sheSham utpAtalakShaNam ||
(AVParis_64,2.8)     prAgyAmyAparasaumyAnAM gandharvanagaraM tathA | raktapItAshitaish caiva varNair dikShu pradR^ishyate ||
(AVParis_64,2.9)     rAj~naH senApatesh cApi yuvarAjapurodhasAm | vyasanaM maraNaM vApi vij~neyam anupUrvashaH ||
(AVParis_64,2.10)     varuNAmAN ca bhayaM j~neyaM yathAvarNaparigrahAt | vidikShu ca vivarNAsu pIDA j~neyA vivarNinAm ||

(AVParis_64,3.1)     satataM dR^ishyamAne ca rAjarAShTrabhayAvaham | AshAdhikArikANAM ca pIDA j~neyA yathAvidhi ||
(AVParis_64,3.2)     viruddhayonigamanam anyasattvaprasUtayaH | hastapAdAkShishirasAm adhikAnAM pradarshanam ||
(AVParis_64,3.3)     abhyaN^gatA ca saMyoge gatihInaM ca ceShTitam | viruddhAnAM ca sattvAnAm anyonyapratisaMgamam ||
(AVParis_64,3.4)     calatvam acalAnAM ca calAnAm acalakR^iyA | bhAShitaM cApi abhAShANAm ashabdAnAM ca bhAShaNam ||
(AVParis_64,3.5)     anagnau darshanaM cAgneH shItoShNasya viparyayaH | lohAdInAM plavash cApsu nodake cAmbhasAM sravaH ||
(AVParis_64,3.6)     akAlapuShpaprasavaH sasyAH paJNcacaturguNAha | saMyogo lAN^galAnAM ca prabhAnAM ceShTitAni ca ||
(AVParis_64,3.7)     vicitrair devatAsadbhir vR^ikShaprasravaNAni ca | disho dhUmAndhakArAsh ca dIptAsh ca mR^igapakShiNaH ||

(AVParis_64,3.10)     abhIkShNA mArutAsh caNDA vAnti sharkarakarShiNaH | saMhitA maNDalAnAM ca nIlalohitapItakAH ||

(AVParis_64,4.1)     dhvajastambhendrakIlAnAM shuShkacaityAdibhiH saha | chinne bhinne drumANAM ca skandhashAkhAN^kurodbhavaH ||

(AVParis_64,7.1)     maNDalAni samAjAshca sarvato mR^igapakShiNAm | kravyAdair Arasadbhishca vyAkulAH sarvato dishaH ||

(AVParis_64,7.8)     saMdhyAdaNDapariveShA rajoarkaparighAdayaH | maNDalAnAM samUhAshca dikShu pItAruNaprabhAH ||

(AVParis_64,7.10)     mlAyate mAlyam atyarthaM gandhAH kuNapagandhinaH | vastreShu bhakShabhojyeShu bhavati utpAtalakShaNam ||

(AVParis_64,8.1)     kShaudraM ghR^itaM ca dadhi ca prasravet prathitA drumAH | sArameyAH shmashAneShu rudanti viruvanti ca ||

(AVParis_64,10.2)     unmattAnAM ca yA gAthA bAlAnAM ceShTitaM ca yat | striyashca yat prabhAShante tatra nAsti vyatikramaH ||

(ParishiShTa_66. goshAntiH)

(AVParis_66,1.1)     oM bhagavan devadevesha surAsuranamaskR^ita | gavAM sarveShu rogeShu pratij~nAteShu vai prabho ||
(AVParis_66,1.2)     kathaM shAntiM dvijaH kuryAt kena mantreNa prokShaNam | homamantrAsh ca ke proktAH kasmiMs tantre prayojayet ||
(AVParis_66,1.3)     uvAca paripR^iShTaH san brahmA sarvajagatpatiH | shR^iNvantu R^iShayaH sarve goshAntiM mahaduttamAm ||
(AVParis_66,1.4)     athavavihitAM samyak sarvarogavinAshanIm | yAM shrutvA savarogAs tu vidravanti sahasrashaH ||
(AVParis_66,1.5)     goShThamadhye gR^ihe vApi govATe gokulAntile | AcAryas tu shucir bhUtvA kArayen maNDalaM shubham ||

(AVParis_66,2.1)     snAtash cAhatavAsAsh ca ahorAtroShitaH shuciH | caturashraM caturdvAram Alikhet tatra maNDalam ||
(AVParis_66,2.2)     tasya madhye tu deveshaM gomayena nidhApayet | tataH kShIraM ghR^itaM caiva gugguluM candanAgurum ||
(AVParis_66,2.3)     puShpANi ca sugandhIni tathA vai sarShapAMs tilAn | lAjAsh ca samidhash caiva samAhR^itya vicakShaNaH ||
(AVParis_66,2.4)     prANAMs tu tarpayet tatra dadhikShIraghR^itAdibhiH | tataH shAntiM prayuJNjita namaskR^itvA svayaMbhuvam ||
(AVParis_66,2.5)     AjyabhAgAntAjyatantram abhyAtAnAni caiva hi ||
(AVParis_66,2.6)     namo j~nAya sureshAya namas te vishvatomukha | namaH kAlAya tIkShNAya [jaTilAya] sarvabhUtahitAya ca ||

(AVParis_66,3.1)     tataH sarShapatilalAjA UrdhvAH samidhash ca dadhimadhughR^itAktA juhuyAt ||
(AVParis_66,3.2)     yajAmi || kAlAya svAhA || piN^galAya tIkShNAya jaTilAya babhrave oM bhUr oM bhuva oM svar oM bhUr bhuvaH svar jayavijayAya jayAdhipataye kapardine karAlAya vikaTAya kaTiramATarAyAN^girasabArhaspatyakakapilamaNDalamuNDajaTilakapAleshvarAdhipataye kapardine svAheti ||
(AVParis_66,3.3)     eSha kramasu tu goshAnteH saMsR^iShTa R^iShibhiH purA | proktA svayaMbhuvA caiShA goshAntis tu hitAya vai ||
(AVParis_66,3.4)     yo vipraH paThatImAM hi gokule cApi hitAya vai | gAvas tasya pravardhante mahatIM cAshnute shriyam ||

(ParishiShTa_67. adbhutashAntiH)

(AVParis_67,1.1)     oM puruShas putradAraM vA dhanadhAnyam atha api vA | nimittair yair vinashyeta shAntiM tatra nibodhata ||
(AVParis_67,1.2)     indrAyudhaM bhavet rAtrau dR^ishyate yasya kasya cit | darvI kare vA bhidyeta maNis kumbhas tathA eva ca ||
(AVParis_67,1.3)     chattraM shayyA AsanaM ca eva anyat vA api svayaM kva cit | strI hanyAt ca striyaM vA api gaur avaghret ulUkhalam ||
(AVParis_67,1.4)     shvA pidet gAm anaDvAhaM kalis saMpadyate kule | gajavAjino mriyante vivAdo rAjakIyakas ||
(AVParis_67,1.5)     kuTumbam ashubhaM sarvam aindrANi etAni nirdishet | shAmyanti yena sarvANi nirvapet pAyasaM carum ||
(AVParis_67,1.6)     samAvaoya ghR^itaM tatra AhutiM jihuyAt imAm | indram id devatAtaye sthAlIpAkasya homayet ||
(AVParis_67,1.7)     indras shacIpatis shakro vajrapANis sureAshvaras | sarvAdbhutAnAM shamano mahAvyAhR^itayas tathA ||
(AVParis_67,1.8)     hutvA sviShTakR^itaM ca eva carutantraM samApayet | vimuktotpAtadoShas tu jIvet tu sharadas shatam ||

(AVParis_67,2.1)     uddIpikA gR^ihe yasya valmIkA madhujAlakam | abjAnAM maNike shabde tailaM sthIyata eva vA ||
(AVParis_67,2.2)     ashubhA vikR^itir dadhnAM dugdhAnAM vA yadA bhavet | akasmAt ca praroheyur bIjAni kR^imayas tathA ||
(AVParis_67,2.3)     kAryo varuNayAgas tu vAruNIvidhipUrvakas | ud uttamaM pradhAnaM syAt paJNcAjyAhutayas tathA ||
(AVParis_67,2.4)     varuNas pAshapANis ca yadAsAM patir eva ca | she.aM tu pUrvavat ca eva carutantraM samApayet ||
(AVParis_67,2.5)     vimuktotpAtadoShas tu jIvet tu sharadas shatam ||

(AVParis_67,3.1)     gR^ihe yasya patet gR^idhra ulUko vA kathaM cana | kapotas pravishet ca eva jIvA vA araNyasaMbhavAs ||
(AVParis_67,3.2)     dhuryau ca patato yuktau gostrIjanma ca vaikR^itam | jAyante yamalAni eva ghoras svapnas ca dR^ishyate ||
(AVParis_67,3.3)     abhidravanti rakShAMsi yatra ca eva kumArakAn | unnidrako atunidro vA atyalpam atibhojanam ||
(AVParis_67,3.4)     Alasya ca evam eteShAM devatA yama ucyate | nAke suparNam iti etat sthAlIpAkasya homayet ||
(AVParis_67,3.5)     yamas pretapatis ca eva daNDapANis tathA Ishvaras | shamanas sarvAdbhutAnAm... ||

(AVParis_67,4.1)     anagnir utthito yasya dhUmo vA api gR^ihe kva cit | AmaM vA jvalate mAMsaM bhaveyur visphuliN^gakAs ||
(AVParis_67,4.2)     chattradhvajapatAkAs ca jvalante toraNAni ca || AsanaM ca eva ;ayyA ca vastrANi kusumAni ca ||
(AVParis_67,4.3)     hastyashvAnAM ca pucchAni varShatyaN^gAravarShaNam | akAle ca dishAM dAha oShadhInAM ca pAcanam ||
(AVParis_67,4.4)     hastinyas ca eva madyante agnirUpaM tad adbhutam | agniM dUtaM vR^iNImahe sthAlIpAkasya homayet ||
(AVParis_67,4.5)     agnir hiraNyapatis ca arciShpANis tathA Ishvaras | shamanas sarvAdbhutAnAm... ||

(AVParis_67,5.1)     suvarNaM rajataM vajraM vaiDUryaM mauktikAni ca | pravAlavastranAshas ca mitrANAM ca viparyayas ||
(AVParis_67,5.2)     ArambhAs ca vipadyante na soddhis karmaNAm api | carur vaishravaNas tatra abhi tyaM devam R^ik smR^itA ||
(AVParis_67,5.3)     vaishravaNo yakShapatis arthapANis tathA Ishvaras | shamanas sarvAdbhutAnAm... ||

(AVParis_67,6.1)     atha yasya svanakShatre ulkA nirghAta eva vA | rAhur grasati candrArkau kabandhaM darpaNe bhavet ||
(AVParis_67,6.2)     patet svayaM vA musalaM devatA vA kathaM cana | unmIlate ca eva yadA tathA ca api nimIlate ||
(AVParis_67,6.3)     prachidyate ca yadi vA tathA vA api prakampate | prayAto vA api dR^ishyeta pratisroto nadI vahet ||
(AVParis_67,6.4)     vimale na eva arkachAyA pratIpA vA api tu sAyakAs | pariveShas tu anabhreShu dR^ishyate candrasUryayos ||
(AVParis_67,6.5)     koshAt khaDgA nirgirante tUNAt ca eva tu sAyakAs | anAhatAni vAdyante nadante shabdam Aturam ||
(AVParis_67,6.6)     caruNA vaiShNavena eShAM yAgas kartavyas eva tu | idaM viShNus pradhAnaM syAt paJNcAjyAhutayas tathA ||
(AVParis_67,6.7)     sarvabhUtapatis viShnus cakrapANis tathA Ishvaras | shamanas sarvAdbhutAnAm... ||

(AVParis_67,7.1)     ativAto yatra bhavet rUpaM vA yatra vaikR^itam | kharakarabhamahiShA varAhA vyAghrasiMhakAs ||
(AVParis_67,7.2)     gR^idhrAs ca tathA gomAyus kR^ikalAsA vadanti ca | mAMsapeshaM ca rudhiraM pAMsuvR^iShTis tathA eva ca ||
(AVParis_67,7.3)     vAyurUpam idaM sarvam adbhutaM parikIrtitam | vAta A vAtu bheShajaM vAyau A yAhi darshata iti sthAlIpAkasya homayet ||
(AVParis_67,7.4)     vAyur mahAn nabhapatir vajrapANis tathA Ishvaras | shamanas sarvAdbhutAnAM mahAvyAhR^itayas tathA ||
(AVParis_67,7.5)     hutvA sviShTakR^itaM ca eva carutantraM samApayet | vimuktotpAtadoShas tu jIvet tu sharadas shatam ||

(AVParis_67,8.1)     atha ced anyashAkhasu kartA bhavati vedavit | japtvA sa R^igyajuHsAmnaM shatamAtraM samAhitas ||
(AVParis_67,8.2)     gAyatryaShTashataM japtvA yayajamAnas samAhitas | vAcayet tam upAdhyAyaM vastreNa kanakena vA ||
(AVParis_67,8.3)     dR^iShTAM ca eva adbhutaM yasmins tat ca api pratipAdayet | etAs tu dakShiNAs sarvAs shaktiyukto na hApayet ||
(AVParis_67,8.4)     yajamAnas tatsuto vA yas svayaM kartum arhati | brAhmaNAya visheSheNa dadyAt tAM dakShiNAM shubhAm ||
(AVParis_67,8.5)     japtvA atharvashiras ca eva kuryAt vipreShu pUjanam | shaktyA atha bhojanaM ca eva kuryAt vipreShu pUjanam ||
(AVParis_67,8.6)     etad evaM samAkhyAtam adbhutAnAM vishodhanam | caturNAm api varNAnAM yas kuryAt shraddhayA anvitas ||
(AVParis_67,8.7)     maraNaM na bhavet tasya na duHkhaM na daridratA | sidhyanti sarvakAryANi dharme ca asya matir bhavet ||
(AVParis_67,8.8)     etat puNyaM paritraM ca devatAyAgapUjanam | sarvashAntikaM ca eva pratipuruShaM nibodhata || pratipuruShaM nibodhata iti ||

(ParishiShTa_68. svapnAdhyAyaH)

(AVParis_68,1.1)     om athAtaH saMpravakShyAmi yad uktaM padmayoninA | upAN^gaM shukracArasta shubhAshubhanivedakam ||
(AVParis_68,1.2)     svapnAdhyAyaM pravakShyAmi kroShTuker vacanaM yathA | shashaMsire purA yaM hi shaunakAya mahAtmane ||
(AVParis_68,1.3)     nimittaj~nAnakushalAH sarvaM tasya tu pR^icchataH | grahA bhArgavabhaumArkAH paittikA dIptitejasaH ||
(AVParis_68,1.4)     kaphaprakR^itayo madhyA bR^ihaspatibudhendavaH | vAtaprakR^itayaH krUrA rAhuketushanaishcarAH ||
(AVParis_68,1.5)     teShAM tathA phalaM vidyAt saMnipAte yathAkramam | ete nava grahA j~neyA vAtapittakaphAtmakAH ||
(AVParis_68,1.6)     eShAM prakR^ititulyAnAM niShiktAnAM tu teShu vai | saMyogeShu ca jAtAnAM tulya prakR^ititA bhavet ||
(AVParis_68,1.7)     arkenduprabhavA deham upatiShThanti dehinaH | tasmAn niShicyamAneShu vAtapittakapheShu yaH ||
(AVParis_68,1.8)     eShAm anyatamo deho yAtiriktaH prakAshate | pracakShate sA prakR^itiH prakR^itij~nAnakovidAH ||
(AVParis_68,1.9)     tatra ye mAnisvAN^gAni R^ijavaH kalahapriyAH | uShNAH kapilaromANAaH svedanA anavekShaNAH ||
(AVParis_68,1.10)     bahvAshidurbhagAsh caiva mR^idvaN^gAH shishirapriyAH | lAlanAH shithilAN^gAsh ca priyAsh ca priyAsh ca lavaNAs tathA ||
(AVParis_68,1.11)     tanutvaÇnakharomANas tv AcAryAs tIkShNa eva ca | valIpalitabhUyiShThAs tathA khalatino narAH ||

(AVParis_68,1.13)     svapne caiva prapashyanti dishaH kanakapiN^galAH | maNDalAni samUhAMsh ca dikShu pItAruNaprabhAn ||
(AVParis_68,1.14)     shR^iN^gArimadirAn deshA¤ shuShkAM malajalAM mahIm | shuShkagulmadrumalatA dahyamAnaM mahad vanam ||

(AVParis_68,1.16)     palAshAni ca puShpANi karNikAravanAni ca | digdAhavidyucchulkAsh ca dIpyamAnaM ca pAvakam ||

(AVParis_68,1.18)     uShNArtAH shItakAmAs tu nimajjanti pibanti ca | kalahaM caiva kurvanti duHkhAny anubhavanti ca ||
(AVParis_68,1.19)     strIbhish caiva vimAnyante kShayante klAmayanti ca | ity evaM paittikA j~neyAH prakR^itisvapnalakShaNe ||
(AVParis_68,1.20)     prakR^itisvapnabhAvaish ca shleShmikANy api me shR^iNu | snigdhakeshanakhashmashrutatatvagroma[bhAShiNaH] ||

(AVParis_68,1.22)     sthiropacitasarvAN^gA bhavanti sukhabhAginaH | shirodarakaTiskandhapakShayor vimalekShaNAH ||
(AVParis_68,1.23)     priyAH priyamvadAH shUrAH kR^itaj~nA dR^iDhabhaktayaH | cirAd gR^ihNanti suciraM gR^ihItaM dhArayanti ca ||
(AVParis_68,1.24)     na krudhyanti cirAt kruddhAH saMbhavanty antakopamAH | pUjAbhir vipulAM bhUmim Avahanti kulasya ca ||
(AVParis_68,1.25)     khyApayanti ca sarvatra guNaish ca vipulair yashaH | mAMshoShNatAtimadhurapayohArAtha suprajAH ||
(AVParis_68,1.26)     na cirAc chuShyate caiShAM toyamAlyAnulepanam | nimIlitAsyanayanA niHshabdA niHprakampinaH ||
(AVParis_68,1.27)     svapanty ekena pArshvena ciraM sukhanibodhanAH | nAtiduHkhena jIvanti votpadyante sukhena tu ||
(AVParis_68,1.28)     shyAmAH shyAmAvadAtAsh ca shrImanto 'dR^iDharogiNaH | alpAshidIrghakAmAs tu bhavanty arthasahiShNavaH ||
(AVParis_68,1.29)     kShutpipAsAsahAsh cApi kaphaprakR^itayo narAH | svapneShu caiva pashyanti ramyaM candanakAnanam ||
(AVParis_68,1.30)     vikuDmalapalAshAni pauNDarIkavanAni ca | shubhAsh ca shishiraprAyA nadyaH shubhajalAvahAH ||

(AVParis_68,2.1)     gR^ihNIta samudgendvindravAyvagnyarkanadIM kShitim | samudraM vAhinIM dvIpaM laN^ghayed vA vasuMdharAm ||

(AVParis_68,2.4)     pariveShaH svayaM candre yo 'navastravasuMdharAm | parvatAgraM samAruhya kShitiM yash cAvalokayet ||
(AVParis_68,2.5)     A kaNThaM majjate yo hi mAnavaH shoNitArNave | rathena siMhayuktena parvataM cAdhirohati ||

(AVParis_68,3.1)     imAn dR^iShTvAshubhAn svapnAn prAtar utthAya satvaraH | nadIsaMgamatoyena mukhaM saMmArjya tattvataH ||

(AVParis_68,3.13)     yadi ca jayati damShTriNo narAn vA yadi ca bhavet sitamAlyadAnadhArI | yadi ca ruditi caivam Adi dR^iShTvA paraviShayaM hR^iShitas tatas tu yAyAt ||

(AVParis_68,4.1)     sa kaluShasalilAvapAMsumagno madhugh}R^itatailavasApradigdhagAtraH | malinavasanajIrNaraktavAsA yadi sumanobhir alaMkR^itaH svayaM vA ||
(AVParis_68,4.2)     svapiti jayati khAdati prahR^iShTo vilapati nartati gAyanaprahAsaiH | bhavati ca mudito labheta kanyAM yadi nR^ipatir nayasho bhavej jayArthI ||
(AVParis_68,4.3)     mayakharasUkaravAnarAdhirUDho hR^itamukuTAN^gadavastracihnanagnaH | vinihataturagadvipo narendro yadi patitadhvajavAMs tato na yAyAt ||
(AVParis_68,4.4)     narapatir aparAjitaH parair yo yadi ca paraiH parihasyate madadbhiH | yadi ca bhavati durdR^ishograrUpo <atha> na sa IdR^ishakaH parAn prayAyAt ||
(AVParis_68,4.5)     svapnAn dR^iShTvA shubhAn rAjA japadbhir abhimantritaH | yuktaH sa shakunair bhUpa utpAtagaNavarjitaH ||
(AVParis_68,4.6)     sahAyavAn susaMnaddho nimittaj~naiH samanvitaH | sumuhUrte sunakShatre prayAyAd vasudhAdhipaH ||

(AVParis_68,5.1)     tailAbhyaktash ca kR^isarAM bhuN^kte tailapariplutAm | mAtaraM pravished yash ca jvalitaM ca hutAshanam ||
(AVParis_68,5.2)     prAsadAt parvatAgrAd vA pated yash cApi mAnavaH | magnaH kardamakUpeShu jale yash cApi nashyati ||
(AVParis_68,5.3)     drumam unmUlayed yas tu pashyed rAj~nopasevakam | kumArIvadane yash ca vAnarIM vAdhigacchati ||
(AVParis_68,5.4)     raktakaNThagate vApi yasya kaNThe visarjati | vivarNo vApi pAshair yo badhyate mriyate tu saH ||
(AVParis_68,5.5)     kAMsyaM vA kAMsyapAtrIM vA yasya tejo 'dhirohati | acireNaiva kAlena so 'sinA vadhyate naraH ||
(AVParis_68,5.6)     yUpAgram adhiruhyAtha nAvAgram adhirohati | acireNaiva kAlena shUlAgraM so 'dhirohati ||
(AVParis_68,5.7)     muNDaH kAShAyavAso vA shvetaraktapaTo 'pi vA | svapne yasyAdhirohanti vyAdhis tasyAdhirohati ||
(AVParis_68,5.8)     shvA vA ajagaro godhA tarakShu shalyako 'pi vA | kR^ikalAso rurur vyAghro dvIpI yasyAdhirohati ||
(AVParis_68,5.9)     ahish ca raudrajaTilaH shvetaraktapaTo 'pi vA | svapne yam upatiShThanti vyAdhis tam upatiShThati ||
(AVParis_68,5.10)     mahIbhasmapradigdhAN^go nirAvaraNa eva ca | samasyAnAM sajAtAnAm utsavAnAM ca darshanam ||
(AVParis_68,5.11)     durgam adhvAnagamanam anUpAnAM ca sevanam | abhyaN^gash caiva gAtrANAM tilagomayakardamaiH ||
(AVParis_68,5.12)     suvarNamaNimuktAni bhUShaNaM rajatAni ca | darshanaM vApy athaiteShAM vyAdhInAM saMpraveshanam ||
(AVParis_68,5.13)     gAyanaM nartanaM hAsyaM vivAhakaraNaM tathA | Anandash ca pramodash ca vyasanasya ca darshanam ||
(AVParis_68,5.14)     purANaghR^itadigdhAN^go naro maraNam ApnuyAt | evam uktA mahotpAtA vividhAH pUrvacoditaH ||
(AVParis_68,5.15)     ulkAbhedAs tathA paJNca pariveShA nava smR^itAH | digdAho 'ShTavidhaH prokto vidyud aShTavidhA tathA ||
(AVParis_68,5.16)     catvAro bhUmikampAsh ca nirghAto 'ShTavidhas tathA | viMshatI dve ca vij~neyA bhedA hy ulkAdiShu smR^itAH ||
(AVParis_68,5.17)     mahotpAtAsh ca bahavaH shAntiyogeShu kIrtitAH | teShu sarveShu vidhivac chAntikAmo narAdhipaH ||
(AVParis_68,5.18)     atharvANaM ca vR^iNuyAt sarvashAstravidaM nR^ipaH | sa vR^ito bhayabhItena shamanArthaM mahAtmanA ||
(AVParis_68,5.19)     prajAnAm abhayaM samyag dApayet pR^ithivIpatiH | anantaraM gavAM pUjA brAhmaNAnAM visheShataH ||
(AVParis_68,5.20)     devatAyatane sadyo dohAn bhUmau prakArayet | satataM cAnulipyas tu puShpair dhUpair yathoditaiH ||
(AVParis_68,5.21)     pradIpair vividhaiH shubhraiH sarvadikShuprakalpitaiH | tathA balyupahAraish ca pAyasApUpasaMyutaiH ||
(AVParis_68,5.22)     hR^idyair bahuvidhair bhakShaiH sarvadikShuprakalpitaiH | tasminn evAntare shAnte goShThe vA jalasaMnidhau ||
(AVParis_68,5.23)     nirgatya nagarAd vApi shucau deshe samAhitaH | vR^iNuyAc chAntitattvaj~nAn utpAtavihitA¤ shubhAn ||
(AVParis_68,5.24)     ShoDashAShTau vR^itAs te ca purashcaraNashodhitAH | aN^gAni kuryur anye ca shatasaMkhyA dvijottamAH ||
(AVParis_68,5.25)     udayAste sukhAsInA japaM kuryur atandritAH | te sadasyA iti proktA vAcane yaj~nakarmaNi ||
(AVParis_68,5.26)     teShAM variShThaH shAntij~na upadraShTA manoharaH | sarvakarmasu vettA ya Anayet so 'py athAdarAt ||
(AVParis_68,5.27)     bhUmiM saMshodhya vidhivat kR^itvA tatra ca maNDapam | vidhivat kalpayed vediM yaj~napAtrANi ca svayam ||
(AVParis_68,5.28)     evaM yathoktavidhinA agnimanthanapUrvakAm | mahAshAntiM prayuJNjIta sarvopadravanAshinIm ||
(AVParis_68,5.29)     annair vastraish ca vividhaiH saMyuktAM bahudakShiNAm | kArayitvA mahAshAntiM varaM gAM ca nivedayet ||

(AVParis_68,5.31)     mahat sukham avApnoti kAryasiddhiM ca vindati | kAryasiddhiM ca vindati ||

(ParishiShTa_69. atharvahR^idayam)

(AVParis_69,1.1)     om upasaMgamya munayaH sarvaj~naM shAntamAnasam | apR^icchan gatamAtsyaryaM bhR^iguM brahmavidAM varam ||
(AVParis_69,1.2)     kAmA hi bahavo loke saMsthitA bhinnasAdhanAH | ekam eva paraM teShAM samyak tvaM brUhy asaMshayam ||
(AVParis_69,1.3)     samAsena pravakShyAmi yena sarvaM pradadyate | atiprashno 'yam udgIrNas tathApi kathayAmy aham ||
(AVParis_69,1.4)     sarvArthasAdhanArthAya shrutir AN^girasI hitA | svatejasA prajvalantI hR^idayaM tad athArvaNAm ||
(AVParis_69,1.5)     prabhAvaM tasya vakShyAmi upariShTAd yathAvidhi | duHsAdhyAni nimittAni tAni vedmi hi kAni cit ||

(AVParis_69,2.1)     akAle yasya jAyante dantAH keshair vivarjitaH | prabhUtalambakesho vA tathA hInAdhikAN^guliH ||
(AVParis_69,2.2)     dvidantash cApi jAyeta tasya karma svashAkhikam | svashAkhAyAM tu yat proktaM kuryAd vAtharvaNaM vidhim ||
(AVParis_69,2.3)     dvimUrdhA vA trinetro vA tathaikAkShir dvinAsikaH | hInahasto 'paro hy arthe na tv atharvashirAH sa ca ||
(AVParis_69,2.4)     kR^itopacAraH paJNca sapta shuddhAtmA sAdhyasatkR^itaH | sa shAntyudakam Acamya shAntavR^ikShasamIpataH ||
(AVParis_69,2.5)     shAntavR^ikShasamidbhis tu tilais trimadhurais tathA | homaM kuryAd atharvA tu tena nandati satkulam ||

(AVParis_69,3.1)     na labhed yady atharvANaM kuryAd dashaguNaM svayam | mahAvyAhR^itihomaM ca sAvitraM japam eva ca ||
(AVParis_69,3.2)     vikR^itAN^go 'dhikAN^go vA jAto hInAN^go eva vA | kulasyAdbhutam atyarthaM tad atharvA shamaM nayet ||
(AVParis_69,3.3)     kapyuShTrebhagavAdInAM jAyante 'N^gamukhaiH samAH | yasmin rAShTre nR^ipas tatra ShaNmAsAdd hi vinashyati ||
(AVParis_69,3.4)     kapyAdayo va jAyante anyasya tulyagAtrakAH | vR^ikShe 'nyavR^ikShajaM puShpaM jAyate phalam eva vA ||
(AVParis_69,3.5)     dvijottamam atharvANaM tatrecchec chAntim AtmanaH | kArayeta mahAshAntiM rAShTrasya ca purasya ca ||

(AVParis_69,4.1)     upasthite rAjyanAshe mahAraurava eva vA | durbhikShe marake vApi anAvR^iShTibhaye 'pi vA ||
(AVParis_69,4.2)     sarvaM rAShTre vinashyeta sasyaM shalabhamUShakaiH | akasmAn nirjalA vA syAd ashoShA vA mahAsarit ||
(AVParis_69,4.3)     tathAnyeShv apu anukteShu ghoreShUpasthiteShu ca | kuryuH shAntim atharvANo dvijA hy eteShu bheShajam ||
(AVParis_69,4.4)     labhate rAjyayogyo 'pi na rAjyaM raja^nandanaH | paThan na labhate vidyAM dvijaH shR^iNvann api shrutam ||
(AVParis_69,4.5)     Adhitsur api nAdhAnaM kuryAd AvAsam eva ca | kanyA pariNinIShur vA kAmyeShv iShTapatiM na ca ||

(AVParis_69,5.1)     vandhyA vA mR^itavatsA yA durbhagA strIprasU ca yA | sakR^itprasUtA yA nArI garbhaM gR^ihNAti naiva ca ||
(AVParis_69,5.2)     sUtikAle 'py atikrAnte garbhe sphuraNavaty api | na sUtiM labhate yA tu bahuputrIyate ca yA ||
(AVParis_69,5.3)     kR^iShIvalaH kR^iShIvalaM jayaty AyudhajIvy api | jayApsur vyavahAre vA saubhAgyaM sArvabhautikam ||
(AVParis_69,5.4)     athApahantuM bhayam evamAdikaM yadAbhilaShyet phalam uktam eva vA | tadAN^girasyaM varamantrasaMpadA sphurantam uccaiH sharaNaM vrajed dvijam ||
(AVParis_69,5.5)     rAtrau dvichAyavR^ikShaM vA kusvapnaM vApi riShTadam | divA grahAn nirIkSheta bhUmikampaivamAdikam ||

(AVParis_69,6.1)     jvAlAdbhutAny atha proktAni yAni ulkAdibhedA gaditAs tathA ye | svapnAdbhutAny api vAnyAdbhutAni gR^iheShu yAny arthavido vadanti ||
(AVParis_69,6.2)     eteShu shAntiM kurvIta amR^itAM vA sadakShiNAm | raudrIM vA vaishvadevIM vA abhayAM vAparAjitAm ||
(AVParis_69,6.3)     gobhUhiraNyavastrAnnais tilair vA saphalaiH shubhaiH | upAnacchattrasaMyuktAM gurvAbharaNasaMyutAm ||
(AVParis_69,6.4)     pratipatIyathoktaM vA yaH kurvIta vidhAnvit | etad utpAtajaM sarvaM mahAshAntyA pralIyate ||
(AVParis_69,6.5)     yasya rAj~no janapade atharvA shAntipAragaH | nivasaty api tadrAShTraM vardhate nirupadravam ||

(AVParis_69,7.1)     yasya rAj~no janapade sa nAsti vividhair bhayaiH | pIDyate tasya tad rAShTraM paÇle gaur iva majjati ||
(AVParis_69,7.2)     tasmAd rAjA visheSheNa atharvANaM jitendriyam | dAnasaMmAnasatkArair nityaM samabhipUjayet ||
(AVParis_69,7.3)     nityaM ca kArayec chAntiM grahaR^ikShANi pUjayet | bhUmidohAn prakurvIta devatAyataneShu ca ||
(AVParis_69,7.4)     catuShpatheShu goShTheShu tIrtheShv apsu ca kArayet | gotarpaNaM ca vidhivat sarvadoShavinAshanam ||
(AVParis_69,7.5)     evaM tu khyApayan rAjA sarvakAlaM jitendriyaH | anantaM sukham Apnoti kR^itsnAM bhuN^kte vasuMdharAm ||

(AVParis_69,8.1)     upasthitaM mR^ityum api dvijottamaH shamaM nayet | adhItyAtharvAN^girasas tAdR^isham AdhR^itavrataH ||
(AVParis_69,8.2)     dyutiM prabhAM sadA sphuran mantrapavitravAn naraH | nR^ipe dhanini cAnyatra shAntyAptvA dakShiNAM budhaH ||
(AVParis_69,8.3)     sIdan kuTumbakaH poShaM gR^ihItvAnyat samutsR^ijet | triH saMhitAM haviShyAdyaM japet kR^icchraM ca shuddhaye ||
(AVParis_69,8.4)     sAvitrIlakSham ayutaM sahasaram atha cottaram | japtvA dashAMshako homaH kAryo doShAnusArataH ||
(AVParis_69,8.5)     shatIranirmalo yas tu nArcito 'pi dvijottaram | amatsarI nitAntaM yaH so 'tra shAntiM samArabhet ||
(AVParis_69,8.6)     evaMvidho 'N^girA yatra yAni sAdhyAni sAdhayet | na nyUnaM tatra kiMcit syAd iti tad bhR^igubhAShitam ||
(AVParis_69,8.7)     laghushAntyudakavidhinA gAyatryA vApu atharvakaH | kuryAt sarvam idaM jAnann atharvahR^idayaM budhaH ||

(AVParis_69,9.1)     ye na jAnanty adhItA api shrutim AN^girasIM dvijAH | atharvahR^idayaM cApi na te vedavidaH smR^itAH ||
(AVParis_69,9.2)     atharvahR^idayaM vettA atharvA paramaH smR^itaH | nAtharvaNe 'py idaM deyaM guror vidveShayAyini ||
(AVParis_69,9.3)     anyashAkhyaM dvijo mohAt pAThayan pravilIyate | atharvahR^idayaM buddhvA yaH paThed bhaktipUrvakam ||
(AVParis_69,9.4)     atharvA nAdbhutaM tasya shAntir eva sadA bhavet | shAntir eva sadA bhavet ||

(ParishiShTa_70. bhArgavIyANi)

(AVParis_70,1.1)     oM saMpUjya vidhivat prAj~naM vidvAMso munayaH purA | apR^icchan bhR^igum avyagraM sarvasattvahite ratam ||
(AVParis_70,1.2)     lokatrayaniviShTAnAm utpAtAnAm anekadhA | bhinnAnAM shamanaM noktaM vada tv asaMshayaM mune ||
(AVParis_70,1.3)     pratyuvAca bhR^igur viprAn shR^iNutAhitamAnasaH | utpAtashamanatritvaM kathyamAnam asaMshayam ||
(AVParis_70,1.4)     tatra viprAn pravakShyAmi duriShTashamanakShamAn | atharvAN^giraso vede vidhij~nAn sarvakarmaNAm ||
(AVParis_70,1.5)     ahiMsAsatyadAkShiNyashaucashraddhAsamanvitAH | shrutismR^itisadAcArAH kulashIlavayo 'nvitAH ||
(AVParis_70,1.6)     teShAm ekaH pradhAnatve yaH shAnto dvijasattamaH | bhR^igvaN^girovid atyarthaM shuciH syAt sAdhusaMmataH ||
(AVParis_70,1.7)     brahmANaM taM nR^ipaH kuryAd dhotAraM sarvavedinam | evam ukte bhR^iguM viprAH procur vigatakalmaSham ||
(AVParis_70,1.8)     hotAro bhUmibhartÌNAM mahAshAnteH prakIrtitAH | nanu kShINe vidvan svadharmapracyute 'pi vA ||
(AVParis_70,1.9)     tatra shAntau prayuktAyAM kasya shAntiphalaM bhavet | nR^ipo 'py adhArmikaH kuryAd brahmaNas tarpaNaM purA ||
(AVParis_70,1.10)     tataH kR^itA mahAshAntI rAjAnaM pAti sarvataH | sa vR^itaH pAvanaM gacched dvijAnAM pAvanAya vai ||
(AVParis_70,1.11)     dvAdashAhaM vrataM tatra payomUlaphalAshanaiH ||

(AVParis_70,2.1)     trINi tryahANi kurvIta payomUlaphalaiH shubhaiH | anashnaMsh ca tryahaM dhIraH sa purashcaraNo bhavet ||
(AVParis_70,2.2)     tathaikonaM shataM nÌNAM shushrUShUNAm akalmaSham | anuktavac ca tryahaM tat karmaNaH karaNe kShamam ||
(AVParis_70,2.3)     kR^icchraM cApi hitaM kR^itvA kuryuH karma samAhitAH | shuddhAtmAno japair homair vaidikair vItamatsarAH ||
(AVParis_70,2.4)     tataH paraM purodhaHsu divyaM tatram avApnuyAt | grahAtithyaM ca saMrabhya dishAM yAgaM ca sarvataH ||
(AVParis_70,2.5)     nakShatreShu ca sarveShu yAgaM kR^itvA vidhAnataH | tato 'mR^itamahAshAntyA sthApayet padmasaMbhavam ||

(AVParis_70,3.1)     sAvitryA lakShahomaM tu bhaume tiShThed vishAradAH | kuryur deyaM ca dAnAnAM viprebhyo yasya yat priyam ||
(AVParis_70,3.2)     gobhUmikAJNcanAshvAnAM ratnAnAM dhAnyavAsasAm | rathAnAM vAraNAnAM ca dAnaM kAmam ataH param ||
(AVParis_70,3.3)     tuShyeyur yena vA viprAH saMbhavo yasya yasya hi | tat tat sarvam upAdeyam eSha dAnavidhiH smR^itaH ||
(AVParis_70,3.4)     dadyAc ca gurave grAmaM dhenuM vAsoyugaM tathA | alaMkAraish ca saMpUjya prINayet prItamAnasaH ||
(AVParis_70,3.5)     anena vidhinA bhaumam adbhutaM shamayed guruH | eSha eva vidhir j~neyo viyatye 'py adbhutAshraye ||

(AVParis_70,4.1)     visheSho 'yaM tu sAvitryA dashalakShAMs tu homayet | homasamAhitamanAH kuryAc ca ghR^itakambalam ||
(AVParis_70,4.2)     dhenUnAM dvAdashaM deyaM shataniShkasamanvitam | gurave dIyamAnaM tac chamayaty ambarAdbhutam ||
(AVParis_70,4.3)     divyAdbhuteShu kartavyaH koTihomasamanvitaiH | gosahasraM ca dAtavyaM gurave dakShiNAvidhiH ||
(AVParis_70,4.4)     eSha prokto vidhiH samyag divyAniShTavipatkare | subhikShakShemasaMpattyA prajAnAM puShTivardhanaH ||
(AVParis_70,4.5)     koTihomeShu sarveShu dravyabhedAshrayaM phalam | shAntipuShTyabhicArArthaM tan me nigadataH shR^iNu ||
(AVParis_70,4.6)     saumyavR^ikShAshrayAH kAryAH samidhaH shAntim icchatA | arkakAshmaryanimbAnAM samidbhiH shatrushAtanam ||
(AVParis_70,4.7)     durnAmakaNTakambUnAM samidbhish ca visheShataH | bhagnasphuTitavR^ikShANAM phalaM shatrunibarhaNam ||
(AVParis_70,4.8)     bilvapadmotpalAnAM tu shucideshaprarohiNAm | sarvadA sarvakAmAMs tu homaiH prApnoti mAnavaH ||
(AVParis_70,4.9)     tilavrIhiyavAdInAM dadhno madhughR^itasya ca | payogodhUmashAlInAM hotA shAntiM samArabhet ||
(AVParis_70,4.10)     sarveShAM haviShAM caiva ghR^itaM shAntikaraM smR^itam | sarvadravye ghR^itaM tasmAd dhome prakShepam arhati ||

(AVParis_70,5.1)     yaj~nopavItinA kAryaM shAntikarma vipashcitA | upavItaM tu pitryeShu sarveShv eva samArabhet ||
(AVParis_70,5.2)     madhvAjyadadhidugdheShu bhakShyamANe vilepane | yantravAhanashastreShu bhavaneShv AyudheShu ca ||
(AVParis_70,5.3)     darpaNe bhaktapAtre ca maNimuktAphaleShu ca | bhUShaNeShu tathAnyeShu shayyAyAm AsaneShu ca ||
(AVParis_70,5.4)     kAkolUkakapotAnAM madhor vA darshanaM bhavet | anyeShAM cAprashastAnAm Agamo mR^igapakShiNAm ||
(AVParis_70,5.5)     ashvetAnAM ca puShpANAM sarIsR^ipagaNasya ca | vasAlohitamAMsAnAm asthimajjAshiroruhAm ||5 ||

(AVParis_70,6.1)     akasmAc caiva saMghAte darshane nakhabhasmanAm | rasAnyatve rasAnAM ca durgandhe vAnimittaje ||
(AVParis_70,6.2)     padmapuShpAkR^itir yatra dR^ishyate madhusarpiShi | kR^isarApAyase caiva kShayas tasya dhanAyuShoH ||
(AVParis_70,6.3)     ghR^ite vA madhudadhni vA yadA padmAkR^itir bhavet | svastiko vApi dR^ishyeta tadA maraNam Adishet ||
(AVParis_70,6.4)     vikAro yatra dR^ishyeta kShIrodanahavihShu vA | shrotriyAya tu tad dadyAd bhAvaiva shamayen naraH ||
(AVParis_70,6.5)     yatrasthaM cAdbhutaM pashyet tatrApi pratipAdayet | kuryAd vA vAruNIM shAntiM parameNa samAdhinA ||

(AVParis_70,7.1)     anyAkR^itiShu vApy etad ye sthAne shAntikArakAH | teShAm athAkShayaM vidyAd AyuShArthadhanena vA ||
(AVParis_70,7.2)     calite jvalite pAte sphurita utpatite tathA | mahAjanagajAshvAnAM sthAne vidyAn mahad bhayam ||
(AVParis_70,7.3)     tatra yudhyanti jAtInAM bhayaM tat syAd asaMshayam | tatrApi cArthanicayaiH pashubhir vidyayApi vA ||
(AVParis_70,7.4)     utpAtashamanArthaM tu ye kriyA na prayuJNjate | narAH kShipraM vinashyante sAnvayAH saparicchadAH ||
(AVParis_70,7.5)     viprANAM bhojanaM kAryaM sahasrasyAyutasya vA | balipuShpopahAraish ca devatAnAM prasAdanam ||
(AVParis_70,7.6)     kartavyaM ca yathAnyAyaM shAntikarma vipashcitA | evaM kR^ite bhayaM sarvaM tatkShaNAd eva nashyati ||

(AVParis_70,8.1)     shubhAshubhasthitaM caiva munayo bhR^igum abruvan | sa pratyuvAca puruShu saMvatsarasamAshraye ||
(AVParis_70,8.2)     shItoShNavR^iShTikAleShu vItadoSheShu sarvadA | saMvatsarAkhyaH puruSho nirupadrava ucyate ||
(AVParis_70,8.3)     yadi nirghAtabhUkampadigdAhAdivivarjitaH | ketubhish caiva yujyeta yadi vAdityakIlakaiH ||

(AVParis_70b,20.1)     prAsAdaM toraNaM dvAraM prAkAraM kAshyapaM gR^iham | shayanAsanayAnaM ca dhvajaM chattraM sacAmaram ||
(AVParis_70b,20.2)     anagninA yadi dahed vidyutA vApi nirdahet | saptAhAbhyantare tatra niyataM nR^ipater vadhaH ||

(AVParis_70b,23.2)     devatA bhramate yatra mR^ityus tatra vinirdishet | garjanaM vApi kUpAnAm upasargas tu jAyate ||
(AVParis_70b,23.3)     pratisrotavahA nadyo bhavanti ca kathaM cana | ShaDbhir mAsair vijAnIyAt paracakrAbhimarshanam ||
(AVParis_70b,23.4)     akAlajaM phalaM puShpaM shItoShNatvam akAlajam | anyaM svAminam icchanti nadyash cAkAlasaMbhavAH ||
(AVParis_70b,23.5)     acalaM ca calaM yatra calaM vA<py> acalaM bhavet | rAjA vinashyate tara desho vApi vinashyati ||
(AVParis_70b,23.6)     divA tArA yatra pashyec chvetaH pakShy atha vA bhavet | rAtrau cendrAyudhaM pashyed deshabhaN^gaM vinirdishet ||
(AVParis_70b,23.7)     shashakaM jambukaM vApi sUkaraM hariNaM tathA | sthAnamadhye yadA pashyec chUnyaM bhavati nishcayam ||
(AVParis_70b,23.8)     araNyamR^igajAtIyAH svayaM yAnti nR^ipAlayam | tat sthAnaM tu bhavec chUnyaM bhagnaprAkAratoraNam ||
(AVParis_70b,23.9)     prAkAraveshmabhiTTIShu toraNe gokule 'pi vA | madhUni yatra dR^ishyante tatra vai kasya kiM phalam ||........................

(ParishiShTa_70c. bArhaspatyAni)

(AVParis_70c,22.1)     om AsInaM tu himavati bR^ihaspatiM sukhAvaham | gautamaH paripR^icchati vinayAt saMshitavrataH ||

(ParishiShTa_71. aushanasAdbhutAni)

(AVParis_71,1.1)     papracchoshanasaM kAvyaM nAradaH paryavasthitaH | divyAMsh caivAntarikShAMsh ca utpAtAn pArthivAMs tathA ||
(AVParis_71,1.2)     R^itUnAM ca viparyAse tathaiva mR^igapakShiNAm | amAnuShANAM vyAhAre sthAvarANAM vyatikrame ||
(AVParis_71,1.3)     yonivyatikare caiva mAMsashonitavarShaNe | anagnijvalane caiva tathA yAnAnusarpaNe ||
(AVParis_71,1.4)     shastraprajvalane caiva caityashuShkavirohaNe | liN^gAyatanacitrANAM rodane garjane tathA ||
(AVParis_71,1.5)     udapAnataDAgAbAn jvalane garjane 'pi vA | matsyasarpadvijAtInAM rasAnAM ca pravarShaNe ||

(AVParis_71,2.1)     AyudhAnAM prajvalane garjane ca visheShataH | puShpe phale ca vR^ikShANAm akAle ca virohaNe ||
(AVParis_71,2.2)     prAsAdAdrivimAnAnAM prAkArANAM ca kampane | gItavAditrashabdAsh ca yatra syur animittataH ||

(AVParis_72,3.14)     AyudhAkArarUpANi shvetavarNAkR^itIni ca | paJNcavarNAni cAbhrANi tathA daNDanibhAni ca ||
(AVParis_72,3.15)     yadA candrArkayor madhye kR^iShNaM bhavati maNDalam | sa shaN^kur iti vij~neyo grahaH paramadAruNaH ||
(AVParis_72,3.16)     tatra rAj~no vadhaM vidyAt sarvabhUtabhayAvaham | tatra kuryAn mahAshAntim amR^itAM vishvabheShajIm iti ||

(AVParis_72,4.1)     atha yasminn eva janapade gobrAhmaNasUtasAMvatsaravaidyAnAM parivrAjakacAraNavAnaprasthabrahmacAriNAM vApi saMkaraH pravartate tad adbhutaM vidyAt
(AVParis_72,4.2)     karmasaMkaraM yaj~nasaMkaraM vyavahArasaMkaraM ca yatra ca dharmo 'dharmeSha pIDyate tad adbhutaM vidyAt
(AVParis_72,4.3)     teShAm aj~nAtaprAyashcittaM yad aj~nAtam anAmnAtam iti madhye juhuyAt puruShasUktaM ca teShv akR^itaprAyashcitteShu mahAdbhutAni prAdurbhavanti ||
(AVParis_72,4.4)     divyAnIty AcakShate devagR^iheShv atha hasanti gAyanti rudanti kroshanti prasvidyanti pradhUmAyanti prajvalanti prakampanty unmIlayanti nimIlayanti lihitaM sravanti parivartayanti vA
(AVParis_72,4.5)     teShAm prAdurbhAvagamaneShv anyarAjAgamanaM vA vidyAd udagraM vA[N^gegam] avR^iShTishastrabhayaM bubhukShAmAraM jAnapadam amAtyAnAM rAj~no vinAsham
(AVParis_72,4.6)     teShu sarveShu bhR^igvaN^girovidam ity uktaM sa catuShpatha IshAnaM prapadyeta || oM prapadye bhUH prapadye bhuvaH prapadye svaH prapadye janat prapadya iti prapadyeta
(AVParis_72,4.7)     kapilAnAm aShTashatasya kShIreNa pAyasaM shrapayitvA kapilAsv alabhyamAnAsu dogdhrINAM shatasya kShIreNa pAyasaM sharapayitvA prAJNcam idhmam upasamAdhAya paristIrya barhI raudreNa gaNena shAntA juhuyAt || sarpir juhuyAt pAyasaM juhuyAc chuklAH sumanasa upahared brAhmaNAn bhaktenopepasanti tA eva gA dadyAd rAjyaM vA parimitakAlaM tasya parituShTaye gosahasraM kartre dadyAd grAmavaraM ca ||

(AVParis_72,5.1)     atha yatraitac chayane vAtha vastre vA jAyate yad dhutAshanaH | etad atyadbhutaM nAma sarvakShayakaraM nR^iNAm ||
(AVParis_72,5.2)     atra brAhmIM mahAshAntiM kArayed bahudakShiNAm | bahvannAM bahusaMbhArAm anUcAnasudakShiNAm | rAjyakAmo 'rthakAmo vA pUjayet tu bR^ihaspatim ||
(AVParis_72,5.3)     sR^ijanti devA divyAdbhutAni prAg upasargAt pratibodhanArtham | kAryANi vighnAni tathA janAnAM karmAkule varNasamAkule ca ||
(AVParis_72,5.4)     daivyopasR^iShTena balena kAryaM kArya ca shAntiH praNipatya devAn | tatopasargAd vighnAt pramucyate divi ced aniShTaM na punaH sa kuryAt ||
(AVParis_72,5.5)     pR^ithivyAm antarikShe ca divi cApy upalakShayet | ceShTitaM sarvabhUtAnAM rutaM ca mR^igapakShiNAm ||

(AVParis_72,6.1)     grAme kule vA yadi vApi deshe rAjany amAtyeShu tathA dvijeShu | bhAvaH pashUnAM vikR^ito virUpas tad adbhutaM tasya deshasya vidyAt ||
(AVParis_72,6.2)     amAtyabhedo vividhaikashIrSha ekadvishIrShe bhavati dvirAjyam | apAdahaste mriyate hy amAtyo jAte kavandhe nR^ipatir vinashyet ||
(AVParis_72,6.3)     yadAdhikAN^go yadi vAN^gahIno bhavet pashUnAM vikR^ito virUpaH | strINAM tathaiva vikR^ito virUpas tad adbhutaM tasya deshasya vidyAt ||
(AVParis_72,6.4)     anAsyaM vApy anoShThaM vA jAyate ced vidUlakam | arUpam asarUpaM vA jAyate ced vidUlakam ||
(AVParis_72,6.5)     adharAdInn acakShur vA jAyate ced vidUlakam | etad atyadbhutaM nAma rAShTre rAjyakShayamkaram ||
(AVParis_72,6.6)     tam adbhiH snAtaM surabhiM sugandhiM gatAsum agnau juhuyAd ghR^itAktam | ganeNa raudreNa ghR^itaM ca hutvA tathA mahAtmA shivam asya kuryAt ||
